****BANDH, PROTEST, RALLIES WITHIN MIZORAM****

****w.e.f. 2014 – till date****

****2014****

4.2.2014 Around 80 members of YMA volunteers/members under YMA Sub-Headquarters Mamit launched search operation for Deep Mandal (one of the three hostages who is still held in captivity by abductors) till date. The search party of YMA members held a meeting today at West Phaileng under the leadership of Pu.Lalhmachhuana, Assistant Secretary CYMA. The search party will halt for tonight at Damparengpui. The Search operation is being launched under the command of Pu.H.Vanlalhlua, President YMA Sub-Headquarters Mamit.

10.2.2014 Sangau Block Youth Organisation (SBYO) General Headquarters, Sangau burnt the copy of Mizoram Rural Development Department (MGNREGA) 2014 Calendar today, i.e.10.2.2014 in protest against the alleged wrong display of achievement of Rural Development in Sangau village. The SBYO urged Rural Development Department, Government of Mizoram to tender public apology at the earliest.

12.2.2014 1) Around sixty (60) student activists of Mizo Students' Union (MSU) General Headquarters organized a peaceful demonstration today in front of Raj Bhawan South Gate in protest against the alleged rape of one Mizo teenager at Delhi on 7.2.2014. The MSU also submitted a memorandum addressed to Hon'ble Minister, Ministry of Home Affairs through the Governor of Mizoram seeking for the safety and security of the people of North East living in Delhi.

 2) Mizoram Postal Employee Union (MPEU) have also joined the two-day strike called by National Federation of Postal Employees from today due to which all postal officers within Aizawl city shall remain closed during 12-13.2.2014.

22.2.2014 In a bid to sanitize and stop the illegal sale of liquor at Phunchawng which is a village at the entrance of Aizawl city, a raid was conducted on 22.2.2014 under the aegis of Phunchawng Local Council consisting around 230 volunteers. During the sanitization operation, a substantial amount of local made liquor, around 180 litres, were seized and the same was disposed off.

3.3.2014 Last night, i.e. 2.3.2014, local angry mob of Lawngtlai Vengpui locality assembled near the main gate of District Jail, Lawngtlai in protest against the alleged assault case of Pu Laltanpuia (35 yrs) S/o K. Hautawna (L), Lawngtlai Vengpui by two accused persons namely, Lalfakliana (20 yrs) S/o Lalmalsawma and Laltanpuia (24yrs) S/o L.C. Vanmawia. The irate mob finally dispersed after 74 rounds of ammunition were fired in the air by Armed Police following the order of Magistrate. The situation is closely monitored and no untoward incident is reported so far.
11.3.2014 Around fifty (50) MNYF activists assembled at Mizo Hnam Run, Aizawl last night at around 7:00 PM in protest against shifting of those Electronic Voting Machines affected by the election petition filed by the Opposition Mizo National Front in Guwahati High Court. They were however peacefully dispersed at around 8:30 PM after they got assurance from Election Officials that those EVMs affected by the election petition will remain under the safe custody of District Election Officers/RO.

24.3.2014 1) All NGOs (i.e. CYMA, MUP, MHIP, MZP &amp; MSU) staged a Protest Rally within Aizawl City in protest against Bru voting inside the Tripura Transit Camps during the ensuing Lok Sabha Election-2014. Around 1600 participants/protesters participated and peacefully marched from Millennium Centre to the premises of the office of Chief Electoral Officer (CEO), Khatla. During the rally, the following NGO leaders addressed the public at Millennium Centre, Vanapa Hall and infront of CEO Office :-

 1) Infront of Millennium Centre :

 (i) Lalhmachhuana, President, MZP

 (ii) Pu Saihminga Sailo, President, MUP

 2) Infront of Vanapa Hall :

 (i) Zodinpuia, President, MSU

 (ii) Dr.Thanpuii, Vice President, MHIP

 3) Infront of the office of CEO, Khatla :

 (i) Pu Lalbiakzuala, President, CYMA

 The following slogans were chanted during the rally and procession :-

 (i) We don't want voting of Tuikuk (Bru) voters from outside the state of  Mizoram.

 (ii) Bru Tripura Transit Camps should be removed.

 (iii) We don't want/strongly opposed casting of votes by Bru displaced voters  (who refused to repatriate back Mizoram).

 (iv) Will continue to fight against the decision of ECI on arrangement of  voting by Bru from outside the state of Mizoram.

 The Protest March peacefully ended at 1:10 PM after the protestors burnt a copy of Bru Electoral Roll as a mark of protest against voting by Bru refugees from Mizoram living in Tripura as voters of Mizoram. The following Joint Resolution was also adopted today :-

 (i) Strongly objected/opposed to the decision of the Election Commission of India (ECI) for voting by those Bru refugees (who refused to repatriate despite repeated appeals) living in Tripura Transit Camps as voters of Mizoram in the ensuing Lok Sabha (MP) election. Urged the ECI to review its decision and also threatened to intensify its protest against it.

 (ii) Demand for permanent settlement of adamant Bru refugees (who refused to repatriate despite repeated appeal) in Tripura and their respective Electoral Roll should also be transferred to Tripura.

  (iii) Asked/Requested all the political parties of Mizoram not to conduct  poll campaign within Tripura Transit Camps.

 2) Lalhmachhuana,President, MZP in his address to the Protest Rally at Millennium Centre today stated that Brus should stop spreading baseless allegations against Mizos and he added that the sentiment of the people of Mizoram should be respected by the election officials. He also warned to take more extreme measures for securing the demand of all NGOs of Mizoram.

 3) Zodinpuia, President, MSU also addressed the Protest rally at Vanapa Hall today. He stated that the Mizo people are a peace-loving community and he claimed that some elements from Bru community always spread anti-Mizo attitude resulting in disruption of the peaceful atmosphere of Mizoram. He also accused the ECI of listening only to the distorted plight of Brus and never accepting the demands of the people of Mizoram.

1.4.2014 Today i.e. 1.4.2014 around twelve (12) members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) &amp; Mizo Student Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Aizawl led by Zodinpuia, President, MSU and Michael Lalramsanga, Finance Secretary MZP hang up one black flag in the office building of Directorate of Election, Upper Khatla, Aizawl in protest against casting of votes through postal ballot by Bru voters residing in Tripura Relief Camps.

2.4.2014 Maxi-Cab/Pick-Up Owners Association, Saiha District organized picketing in front of the office of Deputy Commissioner, Saiha today from 6:00 AM and it ended peacefully at 12:30 PM after a joint meeting was held at the office chamber of Deputy Commissioner, Saiha District.

5.4.2014 Around 200 United Democratic Front (UDF) activists took out procession and rally today, i.e. 5.4.2014 within Aizawl City from 11:00 AM and peacefully ended at 1:15 PM. In a brief function held at Millennium Centre, Aizawl, Pu K. Vanlalvena, Secretary, MNF said that the aim of the procession is to demand for stepping down of the ruling Congress government in Mizoram due to the alleged rigging/tampering of EVMs. In his address to the rally held at Israel Point, Pu Lalthlengliana, MNF General Secretary also accused the sitting Chief Minister of Mizoram of assuming the office after rigging the EVMs during the last Mizoram General Election-2013. Pu K. Liantlinga, Vice President, ZNP also delivered a speech at Bazar Bungkawn in which he praised Pu K. Chhawnthuama for his bold and courage statement .
 In a function held infront of Vanapa Hall, Pu Lalmuanpuia Punte and Dr. H. Lallungmuana expressed their strong demand for dissolution of the present Government of Mizoram and appealed the party activists to stand united for removal of the Congress government.
 The following resolutions were unanimously adopted/passed after the end of the procession and rally :-

 1) Demand for immediate resignation of Pu Lal Thanhawla led government in Mizoram due to their involvement in EVM rigging/tampering case.

 2) Youth of UDF activists would fight for removal of the Congress government in Mizoram till the end.

7.4.2014 The Statewide 72 hours total bandh called by NGO Coordination Committee in Mizoram has been evoking an overwhelming support from the public with business establishments, educational institutions remaining closed in most parts of the State. The Bandh has affected the ongoing electoral poll process as polling parties could not leave their places of duty due to road blockade and stiff resistance from the NGOs volunteers in Aizawl, Mamit, Serchhip, Champhai, Kolasib, Lunglei. However, there was no report of any major untoward incident from any part of the State till 1:00 PM today i.e. 7th April 2014. The brief reports from the District headquarters are as follows :-

**(i) Aizawl District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh has been strictly enforced in Aizawl since 5:AM this morning and no polling parties could leave for their places of duty so far. NGOs volunteers organized picketing duties at different locations within Aizawl city blocking vehicular movements and other activities. All commercial establishments, educational institutions are closed and the street look deserted due to the total bandh. All the security force/police officials alongwith Sector magistrates turned up in time however, polling officials, drivers, etc. could not turn up due to strong pressure from the NGOs volunteers .

**(ii) Kolasib District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh also received an overwhelming support from the general masses with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed. All 9 (nine) polling parties are also unable to proceed to their respective places of duty due to the total bandh.

**(iii) Lawngtlai District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh is not organized throughout the District except in Chawngte village where the bandh is organized during 8:00 AM-12:00 noon. Normal life is not affected in Lawngtlai town. 29 polling parties left Lawngtlai this morning at 6:00 AM and due to stiff resistance at Khawmawi, Lunglei District by NGOs volunteers, some of these polling parties were asked to change their route via Rulkual and 50 polling parties also left for their places of duties at 10:00 AM. Around 20 polling parties also left at 1:00 PM today.

**(iv) Champhai District :**

 In the district headquarters at Champhai, the total bandh evoked an overwhelming support from the public with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed within the town. All the 13 polling parties scheduled to proceed to their respective polling stations today could not leave Champhai due to stiff resistance from the NGO volunteers.

**(v) Mamit District :**

 Bandh also received a good support from the public and after the 37 polling parties with escort failed to cross the barricade of local NGO volunteers at Mamit Dinthar locality, all the polling parties returned back to the Office of DEO, Mamit. All commercial establishments, educational institutions remain closed due to the bandh.

**(vi) Lunglei District :**

 The total bandh also received a good response from the public with all vehicles remained off the road and shops, educational institutions remained closed.

 In Lunglei District, polling parties for the following 16 (sixteen) polling stations had already reached their destination last night i.e 6.4.2014 :-

 (i) Kawnpui ‘W’ (ii)Marpara S-II (iii) Marpara S-I (iv) Darngawn (v) Terabonia (vi) Bunghmun (vii) New Sachan (viii) Sesawm (ix) Mauzam (x) Laisawral (xi) Tuikawi (xii) Old Sachan (xiii) Sumasumi (xiv) Ukdasury (xv) Kawizau (xvi) Samuksury.

**(vii) Serchhip District :**

 The total bandh also received an overwhelming support from the public with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed within the town. 77 polling parties are scheduled to leave Serchhip town tomorrow i.e. 8.4.2014

**(viii) Saiha District :**

 In the District headquarters at Saiha, the total bandh is not observed today and all the 52 polling parties left for their respective places of polling stations today as per schedule.

15.4.2014 Around 40 youth of UDF who went to Lengpui Airport today to receive Pu K. Chhawnthuama assembled around Sairang Police Station at around 3:30 pm and demanded to meet him personally. The assembled crowd, shouting a slogan -'Long live Pu K. Chhawnthuama!', includes MNYF President, Pu L.Thangmawia, MNYF Vice President, Pu Saihnuna Sailo, ZNP Secretary Pu J. Laldinliana, ZNP Secretary P.C. Vanlalruata and Pu Lalmuanpuia Punte who is also a Secretary of ZNP. The crowd however, dispersed peacefully.
29.4.2014 Today, i.e. 29.4.2014 @ 9:00 AM, around 160 volunteers of Buhchangphai Branch YMA reconstructed 4 (four) Farm huts belonging to 2 (two) victims, namely- (i) R.K. Laldawngliana, Buhchangphai and (ii) R. Kapzuala, Falkland, Aizawl under the protection of 1st IR Bn. All the volunteers dispersed at around 1:10 PM after having a brief function at the place of incident. During the brief function, Buhchangphai Branch YMA leaders stated that their action is only a sign of claiming the territory of Mizoram and further appealed all the YMA members to keep vigil on the Assam-Mizoram boundary issue.

 At this juncture, around 25 volunteers of Buhchangphai Branch YMA managed to sneak into nearby Genda village (Bru village), Assam and threatened them to evacuate the village within 3 days.

 However, @ 4:00 PM, a group of Assam Police numbering 30 to 40 came to the place of incident and dismantled all the reconstructed Farm huts again, taking advantage of the absence of 1st IR Bn. on duty at the site. At the time of this incident, one platoon of 1st IR Bn. proceeded to Buhchangphai site awaiting for the replacement of another platoon.

9.5.2014 Around 40 members of the so called ‘Justice For Mizoram’ gathered today, i.e. 9.5.2014 at the premises of Aizawl District Court in support of Pu K. Chhawnthuama, who attended the Court hearing today. The Court process was however, completed before this group could organize itself properly. Leaders of this same group later met Aizawl District Deputy Commissioner, Pi Juhi Mukherjee, IAS demanding classification order for Pu K. Chhawnthuama citing that he is a prominent citizen. Pi Juhi Mukherjee, Deputy Commissioner explained that the matter would be decided on the basis of Medical Report of Pu K. Chhuanthuama furnished by a Psychiatrist. Discontent with the reply of Deputy Commissioner, Aizawl, the agitated members of ‘Justice For Mizoram’ refused to disperse for a brief period of time. However, at 7:55 PM, the agitated members peacefully dispersed after Deputy Commissioner, Aizawl agreed to fulfill their demand.

19.5.2014 Mizoram Forest Field Staff (MFFS) held a meeting today i.e 19.5.2014 at Tuikhuahtlang, Aizawl under the chairmanship of Pu Lalthantluanga, President, MFFS and was attended by 34 members. The meeting reviewed the incident that took place on 16.5.2014 at Selam area, Champhai District where the angry villagers of Selam burnt one Forest &amp;Environment Department's truck (MZ-01-D-6940) due to misunderstanding between a team of Forest Protection Squad and Selam villagers. The meeting instructed all of its members to assembly tomorrow i.e 20.5.2014 @ 11:00 AM at Aizawl City Park to discuss about their course action on Selam incident.

21.5.2014 today i.e 21.5.2004 @ 7:15 AM a police party numbering 117 personnel (armed and unarmed police) accompanied by two Executive Magistrates i.e. SDO (C) Khawzawl and BDO Ngopa reached Selam village, Champhai District. The ring leaders of Selam village who spearheaded the violence on 16.5.2014 are arrested by Mizoram Police at around 1:30 PM after the ring leaders refused to surrender before the Police.

29.5.2014 1) Activists from Dinthar Veng NGOs assembled today @ 10:30 AM infront of the Office of the Chief Judicial Magistrate Office, Aizawl and observed a silent protest against Malsawmtluanga (21) S/o Ronghinglova, Ramrikawn and C. Lalzuiliana (52) S/o Thanmawia (L), Dungtlang who had allegedly raped and molested three youths from their locality during the early part of this month. The accused were produced before the Chief Judicial Magistrate, Pi Sylvie Z. Ralte today. However no untoward incidents were reported during this event.

 2) Members of Mizoram University Teachers Association, Mizoram University Non-Teaching Employees Association and MZU Students Association gathered at Vaivakawn, Aizawl today, i.e. 29.5.2014 @ 9:00 AM in protest against the delay in repair works of Vaivakawn to Mizoram University approach road. The protesters stopped all vehicles and shouted in unison for works to begin at once. The road block was called off at around 3:00 PM after the delegation of the contractor (i.e. Sunshine Overseas Ltd.) and representatives of Mizoram University students, teachers and non-teaching staff associations signed the following points of agreement in presence of EE, PWD, Aizawl Road North Division and SDC, Aizawl District :-

 (i) that black-topping work of a stretch of road between FCI Godown to MZU Gate will be undertaken from tomorrow or from the first sunny day.

 (ii) that efforts will be taken to complete the work before the coming monsoon period

 (iii) that suspension of black-topping work from FCI Godown to MZU Campus is due to ‘diversion/engagement of labour to other works’ and henceforth, such type of engagement should be avoided.

 (iv) that steps will be taken for resumption of resurfacing work of road  from the junction of Ch.Chhunga High School to Ropaiabawk.

2.6.2014 1) Today i.e. 2.6.2014 around 50 residents of Hlimen locality assembled at Lakhuihkawr (the disputed local council boundary of Melthum locality and Hlimen locality) to receive the team of Aizawl Municipal Council (AMC) led by H. Lalruatliana, Superintendent, AMC. The AMC team have inspected the dispute local council boundary area following the complaint submitted by members of Melthum Local Council. However, no untoward incident is reported.

 2) Information has been received that today i.e. 2.6.2014 around 20 villagers of Selam village arrived at Champhai to show their solidarity for the arrested ring leaders of Selam village. It is reported that the said villagers threatened to launch hunger strike &amp; sit- in demonstration in demand for release of their village leaders. Judicial Magistrate, Champhai District will hear the bail petition of the said arrested ring leaders of Selam village tomorrow i.e 3.6.2014.

3.6.2014 Saiha-Aizawl Maxi Cab Owners Association has suspended its Sumo service operation from today, i.e. 3.6.2014 in demand of hike in passenger fare from Rs.700/- to Rs.800/-. Meanwhile, Mizoram Maxi Cab Owners Association (MMCOA) clarified that the ongoing suspension is not acknowledged by MMCOA.

4.6.2014 Information has been received that students of Government Borai High School, Zawlnuam started boycotting regular class w.e.f. today, i.e. 4.6.2014 in protest against the reported absence of Science teacher in their school for a long time. It was reported that Borai High School Science teacher had only attended only one day for this year.

13.6.2014 Today, the Underwear Seller Association of Lunglei launched a hunger strike at 7:30 AM at DC Office compound in protest against the order of the DC, Lunglei compelling the hawkers on the roadside in between the residence of Pu S. Laldingliana, MLA to Agriculture Complex to demolish their seats. The Hunger Strike is led by their President, Zoremmawii and 27 members were present. The Police peacefully dispersed all the agitators at 11:00 AM without any untoward incident.

25.6.2014 Today @ 7:00 AM, around 50 (fifty) members team of MZP left Tlabung for Borapansury-I to construct a small godown for storing building materials for construction of Zofate Chawlhbuk. No untoward incident is reported so far.

2.7.2014 Students of Zawlnuam Government KR High School (Kristian Ramthar High School) and Borai High School boycotted classes from yesterday, i.e. 1.7.2014 in protest against non-posting of Science teachers at the two schools. In this regard, MZP Zawlnuam Sub-Headquarters held a meeting today, i.e. 2.7.2014 at MZP Office, Zawlnuam and threatened to call a 48 hours Road Block of NH-44 (Mizoram to Tripura) w.e.f. 7.7.2014 unless the Government immediately post Science Teachers at the said two schools.

7.7.2014 MZP Hqrs. Zawlnuam has organized 48 hrs. Total Bandh w.e.f. today i.e. 7.7.2014@ 6:00am. Around 40 volunteers have participated during the bandh. 1 company, 2 platoons of security forces from Mamit DEF and 4th IR Bn. are deployed to maintain law and order situation under the supervision of Addl.SP, Mamit.

8.7.2014 MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam continue to enforce its 48 hours total bandh today, i.e. 8.7.2014 as no positive response is received from the Government. Volunteers from Borai High School and K.R. HSS performed duty and closed the entire road passing through Zawlnuam town.

9.7.2014 1) The 48 hrs long blockade of NH-44A at Zawlnuam organised by the MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam has been called off this morning at 6:00 AM. In a joint meeting held last night at Zawlnuam, the MZP and NGOs like VC, YMA, MHIP and church leaders of Zawlnuam village decided that Borai High School and K.R. High School will remain closed w.e.f. 9.7.14 and other 13 Government offices like BDO, ICDS, P&amp;E, Agriculture, Horticulture, Minor Irrigation, SSA, Vety, PHE and Soil Departments will also be closed w.e.f. 14.7.14 and decided to proceed till their demands are fulfilled by the Government. The joint NGOs also demanded for posting of Medical Officer, Lab. Technician and installation of X-Ray machine at Zawlnuam PHC.

 2) MZP General Headquarters organised a sit-in demonstration today at 9:00 AM infront of Directorate of Higher &amp; Technical Education building, McDonald Hill, Zarkawt. A good number of around 60 students who did not get college admission participated in the demonstration. The demonstration, however, was called off at 3:30 PM after the MZP leaders had a meeting with the Pu K. Lalnghinglova, Secretary, H&amp;TE. It was reported that a joint meeting will be held tomorrow, i.e. 10.7.14 @ 10:00 AM wherein MZP leaders, Secretary H&amp;TE, Director H&amp;TE and College Principals of various colleges within Aizawl City will attend the meeting to discuss the matter. It was further reported that the students are informed to gather at the Directorate of H&amp;TE during the meeting. Besides, the matter will be raised by Pu Lalruatkima, MLA, MNF party at the Assembly Session during zero hours on the same day.

10.7.2014 Around 60 agitating students continued their ‘sit-in demonstration’ today @ 9:30 AM infront of Directorate of Higher &amp; Technical Education building, McDonald Hill, Zarkawt and all of them peacefully dispersed at 11:40 AM after the Government of Mizoram agreed to admit 57 students at Aizawl North College, T. Romana College and Hrangbana College, Aizawl.

14.7.2014 Normal functioning of all Government offices, schools and colleges within Zawlnuam area was paralysed w.e.f. today, i.e. 14.7.2014 @ 6:00 AM due to indefinite office and school picketing called by all NGOs (YMA, MHIP &amp; MUP) under the aegis of MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam. The office and school picketing was called in demand of immediate posting of Science Teachers at Government Borai High School and Government K.R. High School, Zawlnuam, Mamit District. However, all roads leading to Zawlnuam area remains open and vehicles are plying on the road smoothly.

15.7.2014 Office and school picketing called by all NGOs (YMA, MHIP, MUP) under the aegis of MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam continued today, i.e. 15.7.2014 w.e.f. 6:00 AM. Around 200 students and 150 volunteers from NGOs performed picketing duty within Zawlnuam area in demand of immediate posting of Science Teacher at Government Borai High School and Government K.R High School, Zawlnuam. The Joint NGO's of Zawlnuam also threatened to intensify its agitation/protest if Government fail to post Medical Officer (Doctor) at PHC, Zawlnuam on or before 17.7.2014.

16.7.2014 Office and school picketing called by all NGOs (YMA, MHIP, MUP) under the aegis of MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam continued today, i.e. 16.7.2014 w.e.f. 6:00 AM. Volunteers from NGOs and students performed picketing duty within Zawlnuam area in demand of immediate posting of Science Teacher at Government Borai High School and Government K.R. High School, Zawlnuam. The Joint NGO's Zawlnuam also threatened to intensify its agitation/protest if Government fails to post Medical Officer (Doctor) at PHC, Zawlnuam on or before 17.7.2014. All roads leading to Zawlnuam area remained open and vehicles are plying on the road smoothly.

17.7.2014 1) Shops and commercial establishments were shut down within Aizawl today, i.e. 17.7.2014 due to a 12-hour (5:00 AM to 5:00 PM) protest called by Mizoram Merchant Association (MIMA) opposing implementation of Aizawl Municipal Council (AMC) Licensing Regulations-2012 within AMC area.

 The protest organized under the initiatives of MIMA has received an overwhelming support from influential Joint NGOs Coordination Committee (CYMA, MHIP, MZP, MSU). Today morning, around 70 members of MIMA and supporters of the protest assembled infront of Millennium Centre, Aizawl and the following persons addressed the gathering :-

 (i) Pu P.C. Laldinthara, President, MIMA

 (ii) Pu Lalbiakzuala, President, CYMA

 (iii) Pu Lalhmachhuana, President, MZP

 (iv) Pu R. Lallawmsanga, General Secretary, MSU

 (v) Dr. Thanpuii, Vice President, MHIP

 The volunteers went to New Market Sobji Bazaar and requested all the vegetable vendors to join the protest and following the request of the volunteers, all the vegetable market within New market area also look deserted.

 The Aizawl Municipal Council authorities, however, said insisting on Tribal Certificate from the applicants, as was being demanded, would be unconstitutional. So far, 534 nos.of Trade License had already been issued and out of which, 39 had been issued to non-tribal under this AMC Licensing Regulations-2012. No untoward incident is reported during the 12-hours protest.

 2) Office and school picketing called by all NGOs (YMA, MHIP, MUP) under the aegis of MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam continued today, i.e. 17.7.2014 w.e.f. 6:00 AM. Volunteers from NGOs and students performed picketing duty within Zawlnuam area. Today, Pu Rohnuna, Addl. DC, Mamit District went to Zawlnuam and held a talk with leaders of MZP and Joint NGO's Zawlnuam at BDO Zawlnuam Quarter. He informed the agitating leaders that Government has taken steps for fulfilling their demands and he also added that a file for posting Medical Officer (Doctor) at PHC Zawlnuam is under process and requested them to call off their agitation. However, the persuasion failed to convince the agitating leaders and the leaders are determined to carry on the protest till their demands are fulfilled. All roads leading to Zawlnuam area remained open and vehicles are plying on the road smoothly.

18.7.2014 Office and school picketing called by all NGOs (YMA, MHIP, MUP) under the aegis of MZP Headquarters, Zawlnuam continued today, i.e. 18.7.2014 w.e.f. 6:00 AM. Volunteers from NGOs and students performed picketing duty within Zawlnuam area. Today, a joint meeting of all NGOs and VCs of Zawlnuam was held under the aegis of MZP, Zawlnuam at MZP office, Zawlnuam from 3:00 PM. The meeting decided to call off its agitation w.e.f. 21.7.2014 (Morning) and also endorsed leaders of YMA, MZP, MHIP and Block Congress, Zawlnuam to pursue their demand to the Government. The meeting decided to wait the response of the Government till 31.7.2014.

28.7.2014 1) Joint Action Committee, Government HSS School organized picketing of DEO's Office, Saiha and GHSS Office today, i.e. 28.7.2014 @ 9:00 AM in demand of posting Lecturers, i.e. Mizo &amp; Sericulture Subject at GHSS, Saiha.

 2) Activists from MZP Headquarters, Lunglei and Lunglei Government College Students’ Union burnt a copy of transfer order of three Assistant Professors today, i.e. 28.7.2014 @ 11:00 AM at Lunglei Government College Campus. The two student organisations demanded cancellation of the said transfer order. The three Assistant Professors are currently posted in Lunglei Government College, Lunglei.

30.7.2014 1) A peaceful procession was organised by Salem Veng MHIP today i.e.30.7.14@10:00am from Arhuan, Salem Veng to Mualpui kawn, Salem Veng in protest against the assault of Tlangthanmawii(38) by her husband Lalfelkima(41) S/o Lalkhawsiama of Salem Veng on 28.7.14. The protestors chanted slogans and displayed placards and posters protesting such violent acts and demanded immediate eviction of the culprit from Salem Veng beside giving strong warning against him. The protestors numbered around 180 dispersed at 12:30pm. No untoward incident took place during the protest march.

 2) Volunteers of Hmar Veng YMA Branch, Bairabi have delayed the Train from leaving/departing Bairabi Station for about 4(four)hours today i.e 30.7.2014 in demand of re-scheduling of the departure time of the Train from Bairabi. The YMA claimed that the current departure timing causes inconveniences to many Mizo commuters/passengers.

 3) Joint Action Committee of Government Higher Secondary School(GHSS), Saiha organised picketing of the office of DEO, Saiha and RMSA Principal office today and will intensify its agitation by picketing the Office of Deputy Commissioner, Saiha District tomorrow i.e. 31.7.2014. It further threatened to organise Total Bandh within Saiha District if their demand is not met by the Government

31.7.2014 Joint Action Committee of Government Higher Secondary School (GHSS), Saiha organised picketing of the office of Dy. Commissioner, Saiha District today i.e. 31.7.2014. No untoward incident is reported so far.

4.8.2014 Around 70 youths of Lunglei organized a Protest Rally today i.e 4.8.2014 at Lunglei in demand of immediate repairing of the 132 KV power sub-station. Southern part of Mizoram have been under darkness due to the failure of the said power sub-station.

7.8.2014 A procession was organized by various NGOs in Saiha, demanding that specialist Doctor (gynae) should be posted at Civil Hospital, Saiha.

13.8.2014 Employees of State Bank Of India (SBI), Aizawl Branch, organized a rally in protest against the abduction of a SBI employee in Garo Hills, Meghalaya by unknown groups and they also demanded for his safe release from the hands of the abductors.

25.8.2014 Today, i.e. 25.8.2014, Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) conducted written examination for recruitment of the post of Staff Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department, Government of Mizoram amidst a strong protest from three Nurses Associations of Mizoram, viz. All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA), All Mizoram Contract Nurses Association (AMCONA) and Non-Government Nurses Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM). Around 330 agitating nurses from the above mentioned three associations assembled near two MPSC Exam Centres, i.e. Pachhunga University College and Central Government Higher Secondary School, Aizawl and after a brief clash with the Police and the agitating nurses, 269 candidates appeared for the written exam. AMNUDA, AMCONA and NOGNAM demanded for cancellation of written examination and instead urged the government to conduct the recruitment through personal interview only. Information has been received that the agitating nurses are still determined to intensify its protest tomorrow i.e. 26.8.2014 second day/final day of written examination for the said post.

26.8.2014 1) Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) continued to conduct written examination for recruitment of the 20 post of Staff Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department, Government of Mizoram amidst a strong protest from three Nurses Associations of Mizoram, viz. All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA), All Mizoram Contract Nurses Association (AMCONA) and Non-Government Nurses Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM).

 A group of agitators numbering around 300-400 from the above mentioned three associations assembled near MPSC Exam Centres, i.e. Pachhunga University College, Aizawl to prevent the aspiring candidates from entering the Exam Centre. However, after a brief clash with the Police and the agitators, altogether, 210 candidates appeared for the written exam under Police protection.

 In the afternoon, at 3:00 PM leaders of AMNUDA, AMCONA and NOGNAM called a Press Conference at Aizawl Press Club and briefed the media on the following main points :-

 (i) Demand conduct of recruitment for the 20 post of Nurses only through personal interview.

 (ii) Trained Nurses are competent enough in theory and practical, therefore, it is felt meaningless to conduct written examination.

 (iii) Demand for proper Service Rules for Nurses in Mizoram.

 (iv) Blame parents of some Nurses in Mizoram for not understanding the concept of Nursing profession.

 (v) Accuse the candidates for being too self-centric and neglecting the dignity of the profession of Nurses.

 2) Picketing of Government High Schools and Educational offices organized today at Lawngtlai by Lai Students Association was fully cooperated by the staff and students of these schools and offices. The leaders of the student association declared that, if their agitation do not yield satisfactory results, they will resort to new methods to meet their demands for appointing teachers for Geography and Sociology subjects at Government Higher Secondary School, Lawngtlai.

27.8.2014 Lai Students Association Gen. Hqrs., Lawngtlai continued their picketing on Govt. High Schools and Educational offices within Lawngtlai area for the second day in a row. Until and unless a satisfactory response is received from the Govt, the students association intends to carry out their agitation.

28.8.2014 Today, Lai Students Association, General Headquarters, Lawngtlai continued picketing of Government High Schools and Education Offices within Lawngtlai area for the third day in a row.

29.8.2014 Today, i.e. 29.8.2014, Lai Students' Association (LSA) Lawngtlai continued picketing of Government High Schools and Education Offices within Lawngtlai area for the fourth consecutive day in demand of immediate posting of Teachers/Lecturers of Sociology and Geography at Government Higher Secondary School, Lawngtlai. Apart from the above mentioned offices, the agitating students also started picketing of the offices of DC, Lawngtlai, DRDA, BDO and Supply office from today. Moreover, information has been received that the LSA threatened to intensify their agitation by organising total bandh on 1.9.2014 (Monday) from 7:00 AM onwards within Lawngtlai area.

30.8.2014 On 30.8.2014, All Mizoram Contract Nursing Association (AMCONA), Non-Government Nursing Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM) and All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA) organized ‘Sit-in Demonstration’ infront of Millennium Centre, Aizawl and around 40 members participated in the said protest. After the demonstration, a joint meeting was held at Nurses’ Conference Hall, Aizawl Civil Hospital under the leadership of Pi Lalhmingmawii, President, AMNUDA and was attended by 50 members. The joint meeting passed the following points of resolution :-

 (i)  Praised the Government for its approval to recruit 50 post of Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department only through personal interview. At the same time, blamed those applicants who recently appeared for the written exam for the recruitment of 25 post of Nurse despite a strong protest from AMCONA, NOGNAM and AMNUDA.

 (ii) Urged the Government and public to respect the dignity of nursing profession and asserted that, nursing profession is one form of profession under Medical Science and should not be compared with other non-medical profession.

 (iii) Urged the Government to conduct separate written exam for its  members who could not enter the MPSC Exam Centre due to closure of  the gate by Police.

Except the AMC Chairman and the Chief Executive Officer no other staff attempted to attend office.

Around 300 people took part in the picketing and no staffs from AMC attempted to attend office. Without any untoward incident, the picketing was temporarily called off at 3:30 PM. 3.9.2014 1) Picketing against AMC staff entered its third day and around 150 members from NGOs took part in the picketing. At 12:00 Noon today, a meeting was convened at Thuampui YMA Committee Room and the meeting was presided over by Pu Lalbiakzuala, President CYMA and 15 members were present in the meeting. The meeting decided to continue with the picketing as there has been no efforts made by the AMC staff to fulfill their demands and if no positive feedback as desired by the NGO Coordination Committee is received within this week, the NGO Coordination Committee, from next week, will resort to more severe measures to meet their demands.

 2) Lai Students Association (LSA) called off their agitation today, i.e. 3.9.2014 at 5:00 PM after they were convinced by the steps adopted by the Government.

4.9.2014 1) Today, i.e. 4.9.2014 @ 3:10 PM, a joint meeting between Political Party Coordination Committee comprising of leaders from MNF, ZNP and MPC and NGO Coordination Committee was convened at Thuampui YMA Committee Room and the picketing was called off indefinitely from today after the Political Party Coordination Committee assured the NGO Coordination Committee that they will take up the on-going issue to the Government. The meeting came out with the following agreements :-

 (i) The Political Party Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) will make efforts to materialize the demands of the NGO Coordination Committee regarding the AMC Licensing Regulations Act-2012 latest by 30th September 2014

 (ii) The Political Party Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) will ensure that while the AMC is in the process of amending the Licensing Regulations, the AMC will not make efforts to introduce the Licensing Regulation, 2012.

 (iii) The Joint Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) also  stated that they will take necessary steps in amending the alleged  loopholes found in proposed Property Tax.

25.9.2014 Thousands of students took out a protest rally today, i.e. 25.9.2014 within Aizawl City in demand of annulment of the inclusion of Chakma students in Category-I of the State Technical Entrance Examination (STEE). The agitating students were divided into two groups and marched towards office of the Technical Wing of Higher &amp; Technical Education Deaprtment, Chaltlang causing disruption of traffic movement within Aizawl City. All roads leading to Chaltlang area were blocked by the agitating students. They were, however, unable to cross the Police cordon at two locations, i.e. at Chaltlang Dawrkawn and near the office of Technical Wing, H&amp;TE Department. All the agitating students peacefully dispersed at around 2:20 PM after the leaders of MZP General Headquarters reached an agreement with the Government of Mizoram.

 Similarly, in some of the District Headquarters like Lunglei, Mamit, Kolasib, Champhai and Serchhip, the concerned MZP Sub-Headquarters have also organized a peaceful protest/agitation.

 In Champhai, around 700 students participated in a protest rally and the rally ended peacefully at 1:25 PM after passing resolutions like cancellation of seat allotment to Chakma students under STEE, demand of immediate release of arrested student leaders, demand of resignation of Dr. B.D. Chakma from the Cabinet, etc.

 In Mamit, around 80 students staged a peaceful sit-in demonstration in front of the Office of the Deputy Commissioner (DC), Mamit District. It was called off at 1:30 PM.

 In Lunglei, around 300 students have also participated in a protest rally and the rally ended peacefully at around 2:30 PM after the student leaders addressed the rally.

 In Kolasib, around 300 students organised a peaceful sit-in demonstration infront of the Office of the Deputy Commissioner, Kolasib and dispersed peacefully at 1:00 PM after passing resolutions like demand of immediate release of arrested student leaders, asked fifteen Chakma students to discontinue their training at DIET, Kolasib, etc.

 Today, at around 10:30 AM, around 300 students staged a sit-in demonstration infront of Office of the Deputy Commissioner, Serchhip and the students peacefully dispersed at 11:00 AM after student leaders read out the objectives of their demonstration.

(Pi Vanlalhruaii has been accused of involving in illicit liquor business by the NGOs) Although Pi Vanlalhruai took this matter to the court, and the court issued a stay-order for her, she left Zuangtui areas under heavy pressure from the NGOs. At the moment, no impending law and order problems is anticipated as the victim left the areas before the dateline fixed by the Joint NGOs.

****2015****

22.1.2015 Today, i.e. 22.1.2015, around 1100 party activists/workers of MNF, the main opposition party of Mizoram took out a procession christened as ‘Mipui Thlavang Hauhna Kawngzawh’ (procession to safeguard the interest of the people) within Aizawl City. The participants in the protest rally held different placards which read, ‘We don't want selling of liquor in Mizoram,’ ‘We will continue to safeguard the interest of the people of Mizoram,’ ‘We are fed up with government under family-dynasty.’ etc. The protest rally peacefully ended at around 2:15 PM after which sitting MNF MLA’s and party leaders submitted a Memorandum to Hon’ble Governor of Mizoram highlighting the following points for justifying their protest rally :-

 (i) Increase of price of rice

 (ii) Motor Vehicle Tax

 (iii) Blood unit price

 (iv) Upward revision of various taxes and utility charges

 (v) Increase of land revenue and fees, etc

 (vi) MLPC Act

 In Saiha, around 100-120 MNF party workers attended the protest rally and the procession commenced at 10:30 AM from Vety junction and peacefully ended @ 12:15 PM at Bazar junction. During the procession, the participants chanted the following slogans:

 (i) We protest hike in price of Rice to Rs.15 per Kg

 (ii)  We protest increase in water and electric tariff.

 (iii) We protest increase in land revenue tax and fees

 (iv) We condemned the government that lifted liquor prohibition

 In Kolasib town, Public meeting was held at Kolasib Diakkawn under the aegis of Kolasib Block MNF Committee and passed the following resolutions :-

 (i) Urge the Congress Government led by Pu Lal Thanhawla to stop indulging in expensive and luxury affairs.

 (ii) Demand for immediate roll back of hike in price of rice.

 (iii)  Demand for immediate roll back of hike in traffic of water and electric charges.

 (iv)  Strongly condemned the decision of the Congress Government to lift Liquor Prohibition and demand for immediate repeal of MLPC Act.

 (v) Demand for immediate repair of dilapidated conditions of road, especially linking Kolasib to Kawnpui and Bairabi to Rengtekawn before the onset of monsoon.

 (vi) Urge the Congress Government to take immediate measures to stop harassment of Mizo land owners along Assam-Mizoram border area.

 In Lunglei town, around 300 MNF party activists participated in the procession and the protest rally peacefully concluded at around 2:00 PM.

 In Champhai, around 100 MNF party activists peacefully staged a protest rally within Champhai town.

 In Mamit, around 50 MNF party workers pasted posters in different locations within Mamit town and they peacefully dispersed at around 2:15 PM.

 In Serchhip, around 130 MNF activists participated in the procession which started from AOC Veng to Bazar Veng. Speeches were delivered by Pu C. Lalramzauva, Adviser, MNF General Headquarters and Pu H. Rammawi, Ex-Minister.

 In Lawngtlai, the procession started from Chawngte Peng (L-4) to Areopagi (Bazar). Around 130 activists took part in the procession. Pu Lalduhsaka, MDC and Pu Lalramliana Colney, President, MNF, Lawngtlai delivered speeches.

 In Chawngte 'C', around 60 activists of MNF took part in the procession.

 In Tlabung, around 200 persons took part in the procession which commenced from Zodin Veng to Bazar Veng. Pu P. Thanhawla, Pu P.R. Chakma and Pu Vanlalmawia delivered speeches.

25.2.2015 The State-wide Total Bandh called by MNF party in protest against Congress Government's decision to hike the price of rice, increase in tax, hike in electricity bill, water bill and charging of blood processing fee, etc evoked a good response in different parts of Mizoram except within Chakma Autonomous District Council area where polling of Village Council Elections was held today, i.e. 25.2.2015.

 In the State capital, Aizawl, the bandh passed off peacefully at 3:30 PM. All Government, party and private offices, shops, markets and other educational institutions were closed during the bandh. The streets of Aizawl were left deserted except some vehicles; most of security forces, hospital staffs and private vehicles carrying patients (on emergency) were seen on the roads. Police deployment was made in all the important picket points/junctions to prevent untoward incidents.

 In Aizawl, Pu Tawnluia, MNF Sr. Vice President &amp; Chairman, Action Committee, today @ 3:00 PM called a Press Conference at Mizo Hnam Run during which he thanked the people of Mizoram for their support for the state-wide bandh. He clarified that MNF party was not against/protest in imposing of tax per se but what the MNF party protesting was massive hike in taxes, etc. He further said that the decision to impose a steep hike in taxes on land revenue, price of essential commodities, etc brought an enormous problems and burdens to common people and demanded the Government of Mizoram to immediately rollback such decision.

 In a statement, he said that on 22.1.2015, MNF Youth Wing had staged mass rally/procession in Mizoram in protest against the decision of Congress Government to hike rice price, etc. He also mentioned that Memorandum of grievance was also submitted to the Governor against the ruling Congress. He added that the purpose of the bandh is to safeguard the interest of the people of Mizoram. He also stongly accused Congress Government of failing in financial management and austerity measures. Commenting on the recent tragedy over the death of patients admitted in Kolasib Hospital and TB Hospital, Falkland he blamed the Health Minister of failing to take responsibility. He also asked the Government to take measures for prevention of incident of abduction especially on the western side of Mizoram.

 In Sakawrdai, Darlawn and Saitual of Aizawl District, the bandh passed off peacefully at around 1:00 PM .

 In Mamit District, the total bandh had been observed in major towns and villages such as Mamit, West Phaileng, Kawrthah, Kanhmun, Phuldungsei, Rengdil, Luimawi and Saikhawthlir. In Zawlnuam, MNF volunteers had displayed posters, etc within the town instead of observing total bandh. The bandh was peacefully called off at Kanhmun village @ 12:30 PM and in Kawrthah, the bandh passed off peacefully @ around 1:00 PM. All the remaining towns and villages within Mamit District have peacefully called off the total bandh at 2:00 PM.

 In Saiha District, the shutdown had been observed in Saiha and Tuipang village. All offices, shops, banks, business establishments and schools were closed during the bandh. The bandh was called off @ 3:45 PM.

 In Kolasib District, the total bandh received a good support in Kolasib, Bilkhawthlir, Bairabi, Vairengte, Buhchangphai and Kawnpui throwing normal life out of gear. At Bairabi, the bandh passed off peacefully @ around 1:00 PM. The total bandh within the entire Kolasib District was called off at 3:30 PM.

 In Vairengte, a team of officials from Assam led by Pi Kimi Thado, ACS with Dholai Police, CRPF came to the duty/picket point of MNF volunteers at Auto stand located along NH 54 in between Vairengte, Mizoram and Lailapur, Assam and raised their concern over the activities of MNF volunteers. However, after clarification was made, no untoward incident was reported and both the parties dispersed peacefully at 3:30 PM.

 In Champhai District, the total bandh had also evoked a good response from the public and it was peacefully called off at 2:30 PM.

 In Serchhip District, normal life also got paralysed due to the total bandh and it was peacefully called off at 3:10 PM.

 In Lunglei District, the total bandh received a good support from the public and was called off peacefully at 3:40 PM.

 However, in Lawngtlai District, except within CADC area, due to the indefinite total bandh launched by Young Lai Association (YLA) since yesterday, i.e. 24.2.2015, the bandh is still enforced while writing this report. YLA has launched indefinite total bandh within Lai Autonomous District Council area in demand of better roads, posting of EE in P&amp;E Department, etc. Information has been received that the YLA Central Executive decided to dissolve YLA Diltlang branch for their objection to the demand of CYLA.

2.3.2015 1) Today, thousands of students from different colleges within Aizawl city joined the protest march/ procession jointly organized by Mizoram Students Union, Gen. Hqrs. and Aizawl City College Joint Students Union(ACCJSU). One group of students from northern side of Aizawl started the procession from Chanmari junction and proceeded towards Vanapa Hall. Similarly, the other group of students commenced the march from Sikulpuikawn and both the processions culminated in a rally held in front of Vanapa Hall at 12:40 pm and passed the following resolutions:-

 1. Payment of Rs.758.98 lakhs of 2013-14 Pre-Matric Minority Scholarship by the Government within March 2015.

 2. Payment of Rs.538.39 lakhs of 2014-15 Post Matric Tribal Scholarship by the Government before 10th March, 2015.

They peacefully dispersed at 1:50 PM.

25.3.2015 A team of MZP led by Lalhmachhuana, President and L. Ramdinliana, General Secretary, Mizo Zirlai Pawl General Headquarters conducted verification drive against non-locals running business in the name of local residents (Mizos) and without legal permits within Khatla Local Council area, Aizawl today, i.e.24.3.2015 from 2:00 pm. The MZP team instructed owners of 11 (eleven) shops to shut down their shops as they claimed that they were running business without having trade licences. The MZP also expressed their intention to continue cracking down of illegal business run by non-locals in Mizoram.

9.4.2015 1) In a show of their protest against frequent transfer and sacking of Governors in Mizoram, today i.e. 9.4.2015, MZP General Headquarters, Aizawl has staged a 'Silent protest' along the roadside from the main gate of Mizoram State Assembly House, Treasury Square to Raj Bhavan Northern Gate while the Hon'ble President of India arrives in Aizawl for his two day visit to the state of Mizoram.  2) Around 30 activists of MSU General Headquarters, Aizawl assembled in front of Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) Office today to picket against Pu Andrew Lalherliana, Chairman, MPSC. 10.4.2015 Today, i.e. 10.4.2015, around 5000 people took out a procession within Chawngte town, Lawngtlai District in protest against the recent Amendment of the Mizoram (Selection of Candidates for Higher &amp; Technical Courses) Rules, 1999 made by the Government of Mizoram. The procession was organized by all political parties and NGOs within Chakma Autonomous District Council (CADC) area under the aegis of Chakma National Council of India (CNCI), Mizoram. During the procession a copy of the said amendment rules was also burnt. In this regard, a memorandum was submitted to Hon'ble Chief Minister of Mizoram through SDO(C) Chawngte, highlighting the following points :-

 (i) That, the Chakmas and Brus in Mizoram are the most backward in almost all socio-economic indicators from that of Zo-ethnic people of the state.

 (ii) That, the Chakmas and Brus are as indigenous as that of Zo-ethnic people of Mizoram.

 (iii) That, the Chakmas and Brus are disadvantage groups in all respect vis-à-vis the Zo-ethnic people of the state.

 The processionists carried placards which read the following messages :-

 (i) No racism in the land of democracy.

 (ii) Down with racist rule.

 (iii) We demand reservation of seats in Technical Courses for the Chakmas in Mizoram.

 (iv) Mizoram Government cannot question racism in Delhi while racism is rampant in the state.

The Chakma Joint NGOs intended to organise procession again on 3.8.2015 followed by an indefinite Total Bandh if their demand is not fulfilled by CADC authority. The CADC authority, however, claimed the allegation against them as propaganda of some political party. The Executive Council of CADC intended to hold a meeting tomorrow at 10:00 AM to discuss this issue.

 2) About 30 (thirty) students of National Institute of Technology (NIT), Mizoram gathered near the gate of Raj Bhawan @ 12:00 Noon today, i.e. 30.7.2015 and displayed placards showing, 'No Campus, No Safety', 'We want justice' and 'Is this Engineering?'. They intended to meet Hon'ble Governor, Lt. Gen (Rtd.) Nirbhay Sharma, PVSM, AVSM, UYSM, VSM today to discuss the following problems being faced by them. As they could not get appointment, they dispersed at 12:40 PM.

4.8.2015 Today, i.e. 4.8.2015 @ 6:30 AM, a mob of around 150-200 people attacked Chawngte/ Kamalanagar Police Station, Lawngtlai District after 9 (nine) leaders of Joint Chakma NGOs have been arrested this morning (4:30 AM to 5:30 AM) at Chawngte Police Station on the ground of preventive measures for the 'Total Bandh' called by Joint Chakma NGOs (CYCA, MCSU &amp; CMS) w.e.f. 6:00 AM today. The angry mob pelted stones and damaged some of the properties of Chawngte Police Station like window panes, Solar plates, etc and to disperse the irate mob, the Police resorted to lathi charge and eventually opened fire (around 8 rounds) as ordered by Executive Magistrate, Pu Lallawmawma. Unfortunately, one Class-XI student identified as Agosh Chakma (16 yrs) S/o Nomoni Chakma, Kalamanagar Higher Secondary School (HSS) succumbed to injury suspected to have been caused by a deflected bullet. Three Policemen also sustained minor injuries. In the ensuing violence, the angry mob ransacked and damaged several properties belonging to the CADC leaders, including residential buildings and vehicles within Chawngte town. The arrested 9 (nine) leaders of Joint Chakma NGOs were released at 10:15 AM and the violent mob also dispersed at around 12:00 noon.

Meanwhile, Police party headed by Addl. SP, Mamit District and SDPO West Phaileng assisted by around 50 Police personnel had already stationed at early this morning at Marpara to take stock of the situation. It was reported that an agreement had reached between the two parties although there were reports of altercation at 2/3 places at Marpara. Situation is reportedly under control.

28.10.2015 Information has been received that today, i.e. 28.10.2015, a peaceful rally has been organised at Marpara South @ 12:00 Noon. It was attended by about 100 persons and the rally ended peacefully at 2:30 PM after adopting the following resolutions :-

 (i) Immediate arrest of the persons who were involved in the assault of innocent Mizo youths.

 (ii) No innocent Mizos should be assaulted in future.

 (iii) Steps may be taken towards checking of illegal foreigners residing in Mizoram.

 (iv) Whenever any kind of misunderstanding occur in future, the matter should be immediately brought to the notice of concerned local/state authority.
9.11.2015 Today @7:00am, around 400 activists of NGO co-ordination committee(YMA, MZP, MSU, MHIP&amp;MUP) organized picketing against a team of State Election officials, Mizoram at Mamit in protest against Election Commission of India(ECI)’s instruction to conduct Special Summary Revision of Electoral Roll of Bru refugees living in the 6 relief camps of Tripura. The picketing duty NGO activists has been deployed within Mamit under the supervision of a team of NGO Co-ordination committee who came to Mamit from Aizawl. After DC, Mamit District failed to persuade the NGO activists, the security personnel made an attempt to disperse the activists. However, as the activists outnumbered the security force, the team of State Election officials could not proceed to Tripura today as per schedule. The NGO activists also peacefully dispersed at around 4:00pm. Meanwhile, a team of NGO co-ordination committee, Aizawl comprising of 19 members returned to Aizawl today.

13.1.2016 A new Liquor Shop at Bawngkawn Lunglei Road owned by Pi Ramnghaki, D/o Pu Hrangchuanga of Bawngkawn was ransacked by a mob of Bawngkawn locality numbering around 500 (five hundred) last night, i.e. 13.1.2015 @ 12:30 AM by overpowering the Police on duty at the spot. The residents of Bawngkawn locality were asked to gather at Bawngkawn Traffic point last night i.e. 12.1.2015 @ 9:30 PM through Public Information system and at around 11:00 PM, the irate mob proceeded towards the Liquor Shop. Due to the tussle between the irate mob and the Police, some Policemen sustained minor injuries. The proprietor of the Liquor Shop stated that liquor worth around Rs. 5 lakhs were destroyed by the irate mob.

18.1.2016 1) Today, i.e. 18.1.2016 @ 9:00 AM, around 80 members of Aizawl City College Joint Students Union (ACCJSU), Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Differently Abled Society (DAS), Physically Challenged Society (PCS) and Zoram Entu Pawl (ZEP) under the aegis of Mizo Student Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Aizawl assembled infront of the office of Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities (PwD), Chaltlang, Aizawl in protest against extention of the re-employment period of Pi B. Sairengpuii, MSS (Rtd.) as Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities under Government of Mizoram. They carried placards and chanted slogans demanding resignation of Pi B. Sairengpuii from the post of Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities. They peacefully dispersed at around 11:30 AM after they learnt that Pi B. Sairengpuii would not attend the office for the day. Leaders of ACCJSU and MBS will hold a Joint Meeting this evening at MSU office under the aegis of MSU General Headquarters and the meeting is likely to discuss about their roadmap for agitation against Pi B. Sairengpuii, etc.

 2) Last night, i.e. 17.1.2016 at around 10:30 PM, about 70 residents of Vairengte assembled infront of Vairengte Police Station after an incident of altercation between three civilians and Armymen took place on the same night @ 8:30 PM within the area of CIJW School, Vairengte. It is reported that three civilians (residents of Vairengte) namely, (i) C. Lalrinpuia (31 yrs) S/o Lalzarmawia, (ii) Zosangpuia (19 yrs) S/o Lalthlengliana and (iii) Lalenkawla (18 yrs) S/o Lalhmingmawia had altercation with an Armyman namely, Sanjay Kumar (30 yrs) S/o Surendra Kumar of CIJW School over road traffic, etc due to which one civilian C. Lalrinpuia (31 yrs) S/o Lalzarmawia was beaten by Armymen and he sustained injuries (as the other two civilians fled from the spot). However, due to timely intervention of Vairengte Police, leaders of Vairengte NGOs and Senior Army Officers of CIJW School, Vairengte, the residents of Vairengte who assembled infront of Vairengte PS peacefully dispersed at 4:00 AM this morning, i.e. 18.1.2016. CIJW School, Vairengte agreed to meet all the medical expenditure incurred by the injured person.

21.1.2016 Today i.e. 21.1.2016 around 1300 strong students took out a possession within Aizawl City under the aegis of Mizo Students Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) in protest against extension of the re-employment period of Pi B.Sairengpuii as Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities (PwD) under Government of Mizoram. The students marched from Zarkawt Junction to the office of the Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities, Chaltlang, Aizawl. The demonstrators further staged a 'Sit-in demonstration' infront of the office of Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities at Chaltlang, Aizawl demanding removal of Pi B.Sairengpuii before 5:00 PM today. At around 4:00 PM, the agitating students tried to break Police Barrickade infront of the office of Commissioner, (PwD) and the Police were compelled to resort to Lathi charge and Tear Gas as the agitating students started attacking the Police personnel by pelting stone etc. Finally, at around 5:00 PM, all the agitating students withdrawn from the spot of demonstration i.e. infront of Office of Commissioner, PwD, Chaltlang and march towards Vanapa Hall, Aizawl and they dispersed from Vanapa Hall premises at 6:20 PM. During the clash between the two sides, 3(three) students and 8 (eight) Police personnel reportedly sustained minor injuries. In this regard, Bawngkawn PS Case No 26/16 Dt. 21.1.2016 u/s 143/145/147/149/152/ 353/427 IPC has been registered.

  Information has been received that leaders of Mizo Students Union (MSU), Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) decided to intensify their agitation tomorrow i.e. 22.1.2016 and decided to assemble infront of Vanapa Hall at 9:00 AM. Further, leaders of the students expressed their readiness to discuss about their demand with any representative of the Government of Mizoram and at the sametime expressed their strong determination to continue the agitation till their demand is fulfilled by the Government. The meeting of the leaders of MSU, MBS and ACCJSU is being held at MSU Office from 6:30 PM and the meeting is underway while writing this report.

22.1.2016 Today, i.e. 22.1.2016 @ 9:00 AM, more than 2000 (two thousand) students under the aegis of Mizo Students’ Union (MSU), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) and Mizoram Blind Society (MBS) gathered infront of Vanapa Hall, Aizawl in continuation of their protest against extension of re-employment period of Pi B. Sairengpuii as Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities (PwD) under Government of Mizoram. The demonstrators blocked the main road at Vanapa Hall at around 10:00 AM. At the same time, Mizoram Police have made elaborate security arrangement within Aizawl City to prevent any untoward incident due to the agitation. At the same time, P.C. Lalrinhlua, President, MSU and Lalruatpuia, President, ACCJSU met Pu P.C. Lalthanliana, Hon'ble Minister, i/c Social Welfare Department in his bungalow and received the revocation order of Pi B. Sairengpuii, MSS (Rtd) (vide Memo No.B.13016/35/2010-SWD, Dt.22.1.2016) and the agitation was called off at around 11:30 AM. The students also dispersed peacefully after passing the following resolutions :-

 (i) Urged the Government of Mizoram to immediately appoint new Commissioner, PwD having special knowledge or practical experience in respect of matters relating to rehabilitation of persons with disabilities

 (ii) Urged the Government of Mizoram to immediately frame recruitment rule for the post of Commissioner, PwD under Government of Mizoram.

 (iii) Demanded payment of compensation to the injured students (who sustained injuries during the clash with Police force).

3.2.2016 Today i.e 3.2.2016 around 500 residents of Ramthar locality, Lunglei took out a procession within Lunglei town in protest against the death of HS.Lalmuankima S/o HS Ngaihzuala (L), Ramthar on 1.2.2016 who was assaulted by three youths of Lunglei on the night of 13.1.2016 and later on succumbed to his injuries at Lunglei Civil Hospital. The procession was held under the aegis of Joint Action Committee, Ramthar, Lunglei. They dispersed peacefully at around 1:00 PM after passing the following resolutions :-

 (i) Demanded exemplary punishment against the three accused persons.

 (ii) Demanded ex-gratia payment to the family of HS.Lalmuankima (L)

 (iii)  Demanded setting up of Police Beat Post within Ramthar Village Council area.

 It may be mentioned that all the three accused persons namely (i) Lalduhawma (30 yrs) S/o Suaktlaia, Lunglawn, Lunglei (ii)C.Lalmuanzuala (17yrs) S/o C.Lalhmachhuana, Lunglawn,Lunglei (iii) Lalruatfela (17yrs) S/o Lalbiaksanga, Lunglawn, Lunglei were already arrested by Lunglei Police and a criminal case vide Lunglei PS Case No.8/2016 dt.16.1.2016 u/s 325/34 IPC has already been registered.

10.2.2016 Consequence upon the alleged sexual assault of a juvenile by H.R. Laldinga (19) S/o Tlangchawimawia of Saipum, Kolasib District at Saipum on yesterday, i.e. 9.2.2016 @ 3:30, MHIP, Saipum organised a demonstration this morning, i.e. 10.2.2016 infront of 1st IR Bn. Post, Saipum, where the accused was temporarily kept for his safe custody by the village authority. The demonstrators demanded the authority to take severe action against the accused. The matter was taken up by Vairengte Police Station and a case vide Vairengte PS Case No. 6/16 Dt.9/2/2016 U/s 6 of POCSO Act has been registered. The victim was sent for medical examination and the accused has been kept under Police Custody.

1.3.2016 Today, i.e. 1.3.2016, commercial vehicles like City Buses, Taxis, Trucks, Pickups, Maxicabs stayed off the roads across the state of Mizoram due to strike called by Commercial Vehicle Joint Action Committee (CVJAC) in protest against the Government's decision to hike Vehicle Tax, order for rotational plying of taxis, cancellation of all Mizoram Plying Permit, cancellation of replacement of old vehicles, impose of compulsory payment of life-time (15 years) tax on vehicle. As many as 26 (twenty six) Government buses including Mizoram State Transport buses were pressed into service within Aizawl city today. Hundreds of commercial vehicles (Trucks, Maxicabs) were also stranded on the National Highway (NH-54) at Rengtekawn, etc which is one of the lifeline of Mizoram.

 The leaders of Commercial Vehicle Joint Action Committee (CVJAC) held a meeting today @ 1:00 PM at the office of Mizoram Tipper Drivers &amp; Owners Association, Bawngkawn. Pu Jeffry L. Fanai, General Secretary, CVJAC chaired the meeting and was attended by 35 members. The meeting decided to intensify its agitation tomorrow, i.e. 2.3.2016 and also threatened to boycott the KTP General Conference to be held at Champhai during 3rd - 6th March, 2016 unless positive response is received from the Government.

 However, Pu Lalmalsawma, IAS, Chief Secretary has immediately convened a joint meeting with the leaders of CVJAC in his office chamber today @ 5:00 PM. The joint meeting decided to constitute a team of officials (study group) to study the grievances and demands of the CVJAC and as a result of which leaders of CVJAC agreed to call off their strike. Further, taxi services will resume from tomorrow, i.e. 2.3.2016 within Aizawl city till further order. The joint meeting was attended by Addl. Secretary (Home); DC, Aizawl; SP, Aizawl; SP, Traffic; Director, Transport and seven (7) members of CVJAC led by Jeffry L. Fanai, General Secretary, CVJAC.

22.9.2016 Today, i.e. 22.9.2016 @ 10:30 AM, residents of Zohnuai Veng, Lunglei, numbering around 200 (two hundred) gathered infront of CJM office, Lunglei and demanded to see Stephen Lalchawiliana (26), S/o H. Remlalliana of Lawngtlai, the accused for the murder of C. Lalsawmliana (33), S/o C. Lalrinawma, Zohnuai, Lunglei on 27.8.2016 vide Lunglei PS Case No.186/16, Dt.27.8.2016 u/s 302 IPC. The residents of Zohnuai were reportedly irritated over the Hearing of the Case by CJM yesterday, i.e. 21.9.2016, prior to the predetermined date for hearing, i.e. today. The angry crowd pelted stones at the office of CJM and they reportedly destroyed window glasses and windowpanes of CJM office. They also forcibly tried to enter into the office of the CJM. However, Police have guarded the gate of the office and prevented the mob from entering the office. It was further reported that some sections of the mob have entered and ransacked the official quarters of Pu R. Malsawmdawngzuala, CJM, Lunglei located at AP Tlang, Lunglei and the quarters of one staff of CJM, Lunglei. They destroyed most of the furnitures, windows, TV, refrigerator, utensils, etc. and burnt the mattressess of Pu R. Malsawmdawngzuala. Leaders of Sub-Headquarters YMA, Lunglei also rushed immediately to CJM Office to pacify the angry crowds and acted as mediator. However, the effort of leaders of Sub-Headquarters YMA, Lunglei to control the situation had failed. The Executive Magistrate, Lunglei then declared impostion of Section 129 of CrPC for the dispersal of the unlawful assembly @ 4:15 PM. Acting upon the imposition of Section 129 of CrPC, the Police have arrested 17 (seventeen) members of the unlawful assembly and were kept into police custody. Criminal cases are being registered at Lunglei PS and the situation is under control for the time being.

About 2500 students from Government Hrangbana College, Government Aizawl North College, Government Aizawl West College, Pachhunga University College, Government Aizawl College, T.Romana College and Women Polytechnic participated at the procession whereas Government Johnson College, Zirtiri Residential Science College, Government J. Thankima College, Mizoram University and Aizawl Law College did not participate.

 The following resolutions were passed during the procession :-

 i) Slammed the Government over sending of Mizo students to an unverified Institution outside the State and urged the Government to take care of them.

 ii) Insisted the Political Executives of Mizoram to seek an apology to the students of NIAS for making adverse remarks on them.

 iii) Urged the Government to take measures for facilitating the students to appear their exam and take initiative against issuance of fake certificates to the students.

 iv) Demanded the Government to provide compensation to the students of  NIAS over the pecuniary loss incurred by them at NIAS. They also  expressed their commitment to continue their protest if the Government do  not give compensation to the students immediately.

17.8.2017 Today, i.e. 17.8.2017, Chakma National Council of India (CNCI), Mizoram State Committee and Chakma NGOs, Kamalanagar, Chawngte organised 'Chakma Black Day' by gathering at Kamalanagar-II (Rexi Square) in condemnation of the Radcliffe Award of Bengal Boundary Commission which awarded Chittagong Hill Tracts unjustly to Pakistan during partition of Indian Sub-Continent in 1947. As many as 200 (two hundred) people participated at the 'Chakma Black Day' and they burnt the copy of the Radcliffe Award of Bengal Boundary Commission. Shri Rasik Mohan Chakma, President, CNCI, Mizoram; Shri Alak Bikash Chakma, Vice President, CNCI, Mizoram and Shri Amarsmriti Chakma, Vice President, CNCI, Mizoram delivered speeches during the function in which they demanded the intervention of Government of Great Britain in resolving the crisis of Chakmas in Bangladesh. They also urged the International Chakma community to start observing the Chakma Black Day. The gathering was peacefully called off @ 1:30 p.m.

Members of MIZUTA organized 'Demand Day' in protest against the alleged apathetic attitude of Central Government towards their demand like implementation of the recommendation of Pay Review Committee headed by V.S. Chauhan, etc. The peaceful protest was organized as per the nationwide protest called by All India Federation of University and College Teachers' Organization (AIFUCTO) and Federation of Central University Teachers' Association.

6.9.2017 Mizoram University Students' Council (MZUSC) staged indefinite shutdown of Mizoram University w.e.f. today, i.e. 6.9.2017 @ 8:30 a.m. As many as 500 (five hundred) agitating students gathered infront of Mizoram University Main Entrance Gate and they obstructed all staff of Mizoram University including Prof. Lianzela, Acting Vice Chancellor from entering MZU Campus. At around 10:30 a.m, a small function was held near MZU Main Entrance Gate in which Pu Malsawmsanga,Vice President, MZUSC and Pu Vanlalzuata, General Secretary, MZUSC addressed the students. They stated that MZUSC will continue their strike until Vice Chancellor of MZU is appointed. They also urged all the students and staff of MZU to support the initiative taken by MZUSC and also appealed Mizoram University Students' Discussion Forum to cancel their proposed holding of National Level Workshop on the topic "Youth and Politics in India with special reference to North East India" on 7.9.2017. Leaders of MZUSC also asked all the students of MZU to perform picketing duty tomorrow, i.e. 7.9.2017 at MZU.

 During the meeting they chanted a slogan, "We demand a regular Vice Chancellor" and displayed banners/placards which read "Justice for MZU", "University without regular VC is like a Cabinet without Modiji", etc. They also passed a resolution that "All academic as well as non-academic activities be shut down until and unless regular Vice Chancellor is appointed."

8.9.2017 MSU General Headquarters and Regional Headquarters, Lunglei and Sub-Headquarters in some District capitals observed today, i.e. 8.9.2017 as 'Zo Hnam Chhan Ni' (Day of Safeguarding Zo Tribe). As a part of the observation, about 10 (ten) MSU activists performed picketing duty within Aizawl City against non-Mizo shops from 6:30 a.m. The picketing duty closed down about 10 (ten) non-Mizo shops today and no untoward incident was reported.

As many as 29 (twenty nine) supply Trucks are reportedly stranded at National Higway-54 near Kolasib due to the strike.

 2) Students' Union of Pachhunga University College (PUC), a Constituent College of MZU organised picketing duty today, i.e. 11.9.2017 at the main entrance of their College in support of the initiative taken by MZUSC for the immediate appointment of regular Vice Chancellor of MZU. They boycotted classes and obstructed Teaching staff and Non-teaching staff from entering the College campus. Meanwhile, other colleges within Aizawl City are functioning smoothly as they did not join the strike (picketing).

14.9.2017 MNF General Headquarters organised State-wide Total Bandh today, i.e. 14.9.2017 from 5:00 a.m in protest against dilapidated condition of roads in Mizoram and the alleged laxity of the incumbent Congress Ministry to repair the roads. Total Bandh was organised in Aizawl, District Headquarters, Sub-Divisional Headquarters, Towns and Villages and it was enforced by party workers at MNF General Headquarters, Sub-Headquarters, Blocks and Units.

 MNF General Headquarters made 41 (forty one) duty posts within Aizawl City and leaders of MNF General Headquarters watched and monitored the said posts. Consequence upon the Total Bandh, all Government offices, Schools and Colleges within Mizoram were closed down.The Total Bandh was called-off at 3:00 p.m without any untoward incident.

Agitating members of MZUSC dispersed peacefully without any untoward incident.

However, Lunglei to Aizawl Maxi Cab Service Drivers' Welfare intended to resume service/plying w.e.f. tomorrow, i.e. 29.9.2017 at their own existing fare, i.e. Rs. 440/- .

29.9.2017 1) Today, i.e. 29.9.2017 @ 10:00 a.m, MSU General Headquarters and Aizawl City Colleges Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) organised procession from Vanapa Hall and they marched towards Chakma House, Hunthar Veng, Aizawl. Lalmalsawma, President, MSU delivered a speech and they called-off the procession @ 1:35 p.m
