3.2.2018 Around 200 (two hundred) students from Govt. J. Thankima College organised a demonstration on Saturday, i.e. 3.2.2018@ 10:00 a.m. at Govt. J. Thankima College Landsite, Bawngkawn Brigade area, in protest against the alleged construction of House by Pi B. Lalhmangaihi, Chaltlang Dingdi Veng which was occupied by Pi Ramfangzauvi &amp; Family within the college area. The protestors pulled down portion of the wall, kitchen shed and damaged 2 (two) water storages. The situation was kept under control by the timely intervention of Police. It is reported that some leaders of MZP and MSU had joined the demonstration. The following resolutions were passed by the protestors :-

  (i) Pi Ramfangzauvi &amp; Family should evacuate themselves from Govt.  J. Thankima College Landsite, Bawngkawn Brigade Area.

  (ii) Government of Mizoram should evict the families who are allegedly   occupying Govt. J. Thankima College Landsite at Bawngkawn  Brigade Area.

  (iii) Eviction should be completed by the State Government on or before   10.2.2018.

  (iv) Students of Govt. J. Thankima College will hold protest   demonstrations if their demands for eviction of the family is not  met.

6.2.2018 on 6.2.2018 @ 1:00 p.m, around seventy (70) residents of Melbuk Village, Mizoram forcefully retrieved Twenty (20) vehicles owned by individuals from Melbuk which were detained by Myanmar Police at the bank of Uilui River, near the Indo-Myanmar border approximately 45 Kilometres from Champhai. These vehicles mostly of medium vehicles carrying fertilizers were reportedly detained by the Myanmar Police since 28th November, 2017 for allegedly entering into their territory without proper permit.

 According to information received, these villagers surprised the Myanmar Police personnel posted at this place during their lunch break and tied them up before taking away these vehicles but no injury was caused to Myanmar Police.

 Residence of Melbuk Village claimed that they have been taking enormous efforts to reclaim these vehicles detained by Myanmar Police. They had requested the Deputy Commissioner of Tiddim and Falam, Myanmar about this issue but to no avail. The owners of these vehicles have not received any seizure memo from Myanmar authorities; in fact, all they had received was that their vehicles were not confiscated. As these vehicles were reportedly the main source of income for the residents of Melbuk, they forcefully retrieved their vehicles.

9.2.2018 In a protest demonstration held today, i.e. 9.2.2018 @ 12:40 at Sazaikawn, Lunglei, Youths of Lunglei demanded speedy execution of On-going Road Construction works between Lunglei to Kanghmun South. The agitators launched blockade at Lunglei - Sazaikawn road and caused delay to a group of MsLA led by Pu Zodintluanga, Hon'ble UD &amp; PA Minster from attending the inaugural function of Multipurpose Hall at Sazaikawn. Other MsLA included Pu PC. Thanliana, Hon'ble Minister for Social Welfare ; Pu S. Laldingliana, MLA, Vice Chairman, HPC Lunglei and Pu Chalrosanga, MLA, Lungei West. Around 60 (sixty) youths participated in the agitation and the blockade was lifted by 2:00 p.m. The following resolutions were passed by the agitators:-

 (i) Demanded immediate Release Order of Road Maintenance Funds between Lunglei to Kanghmun South currently pending with the Finance Department. The release order must be made on 9.2.2018.
 (ii) PWD must reinforce road construction labourers at Lunglei - Kanghmun South.

  (iii) Publication of names of Contractor(s) engaged in the Lunglei - Kanghmun South Road construction works.

 (iv) Completion of road construction work before 15th April 2018.

 (v) Allocation of additional funds for Lunglei - Kanghmun South road construction.

21.2.2018 Yesterday, i.e. 20.2.2018, at around 10:30 a.m, miscreants suspected to be members of Students' Union of Govt. J. Thankima College dismantled the house of Pi B. Lalhmangaihi which was rented by Pu R. Lalhmingmawia at Bawngkawn Brigade Veng, Aizawl which was supposedly constructed within the premises of Govt. J. Thankima College land site. The tenants were away while the incident took place. The miscreants have already fled the scene when Police arrived at the place of occurrence. Situation is under close watch.
27.2.2018 Today, i.e. 27.2.2018, around 50 (fifty) members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) from Aizawl and Bairabi constructed "Zofate Chawlhbuk" (Shed) at Zophai near Bairabi located at Mizoram- Assam border. The construction work of 12x6 feet shed was reportedly completed at around 4:00 p.m followed by a short function held at the Shed under the chairmanship of L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, President, MZP. It was also reported that Assam Police, Assam Forest Deptt. staff and Mizoram Police commanded by Commandant IstIR Bn., Mualvum were present at the spot during the construction. The Assam Police reportedly requested for demolition of the shed by a joint Assam and Mizoram Police force in order to avoid further escalation of Law and Order problem at the disputed site.

28.2.2018 It has been reported that 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' constructed by Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) yesterday, i.e. 27.2.2018 at Zophai located at Mizoram-Assam border has been demolished by unknown miscreants reportedly with an excavator last night, i.e. 27.2.2018 at around 9:25 p.m, barely five (5) hours after it was constructed by MZP. In this regard, an FIR has been lodged at Bairabi Police Station by Ricky Zorinsanga, President, MZP Sub-Headquarters, Bairabi last night itself. At the same time, in their Press Release issued today, i.e. 28.2.2018, MZP strongly condemned the demolition of Zofate Chawlhbuk which they claimed was constructed within their own plot of land within the territory of Mizoram. They also expressed their intention to re-construct 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' at the same disputed site on 8.3.2017. They also demanded that those miscreants responsible for the demolition of the shed should be arrested on or before 5thMarch, 2018 and that all the materials of the shed that were stolen from the site should be returned to MZP. Around 40 (forty) Mizoram Police personnel are performing duty at Bairabi in order to prevent any untoward incident at the disputed site and its surrounding areas.

9.3.2018 Yesterday, i.e. 8.3.2018, a large number of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) from Aizawl, Kolasib and Bairabi town went to Zophai near Bairabi with an intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk (Shed) near Assam-Mizoram border. At around 11:45 a.m yesterday, a minor scuffle broke out between members of MZP and Assam Police when some members of MZP tried to unload their building materials from the vehicle. The Assam Police resorted to Lathi-charge, as a result of which around 15 (fifteen) MZP members and some media persons from Mizoram reportedly sustained minor injuries. Adamant with their intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk, a good number of MZP members remain camped at the disputed site throughout last night, i.e. 8.3.2018 and the Assam Police also performed duty at the site the whole night. The Government of Mizoram promptly sent Pu Lalrinmawia Ralte, Political Adviser to Chief Minister and other officials last night itself to prevent further escalation of dispute at the site and no further untoward incident was reported last night.

 Today, i.e. 9.3.2018 around 40 (forty) members of Aizawl City College Joint Students’ Union (ACCJSU) led by Lalnunpuia, President, ACCJSU left Aizawl for Zophai to join MZP. It has also been reported that leaders of Central Young Mizo Association (CYMA) including some members of political parties have also proceeded to the site.

 Today, i.e. 9.3.2018 at around 6:00 p.m, Pu Lalrinmawia Ralte, Political Adviser to Chief Minister; Pu Lalbiakzama, Addl. Secretary, Home Department; DC, Kolasib and SP, Kolasib held a meeting with leaders of MZP at the residence of Pu Sanghmingthanga, Bairabi. The Government officials advised leaders of MZP to approach the Court with matters regarding the land dispute to tackle the issue legally. Appeals have been reportedly made to the students not to go ahead with their intention to reconstruct the shed at Zophai in order to avoid further escalation of Law and Order problems and to leave the issue in the hands of higher officials between the two states. In this regard, it has been reported that leaders of MZP are likely to appeal and appraise the proposal to their members present at the disputed site.

 In order to prevent any untoward incident, hundreds of Mizoram Police under the command of SP, Kolasib and Commandant, 1st IR Bn. are performing duty in and around the disputed site. A good number of MZP members and Assam Police are still present at the site while writing this report.

 It may be pertinent to mention here that Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) had constructed a Shed named ‘Zofate Chawlhbuk’ at Zophai near Bairabi on 27.2.2018 as they strongly claimed that the said land belongs to Pu Ch. Chhunga (L), the first Chief Minister of Mizoram. At the same time, a Police Duty Post have also been constructed supposedly by Assam Police at the same disputed site on 2.3.2018 but the two structures were dismantled within same days they were constructed.

10.3.2018 Today, i.e. 10.3.2018 @ around 11:00 a.m, a scuffle broke out again between Assam Police and members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) when around 100 (hundred) strong MZP members proceeded to the disputed site at Zophai near Bairabi along Assam - Mizoram border with their building materials to reconstruct ‘Zofate Chawlhbuk’ at the site. The students were intercepted by Assam Police before they reached the disputed site and they subsequently used force to disperse them. It has been reported that the Assam Police initially used Lathi but later on resorted to firing and around 8 (eight) shots were reportedly fired as a result of which one Ricky Lalchhandama, Secretary i/c Establishment, MZP reportedly sustained gunshot injury on his right ankle and around 49 (forty nine) others sustained injuries on their persons. Out of 49 (forty nine) injured MZP members, 7 (seven) of them reportedly sustained serious injuries and were referred to other Hospitals for necessary treatment. The Assam Police burnt down the temporary shed constructed by the MZP near the disputed site and the following vehicles belonging to MZP members were also ransacked by the Assam Police today :-

 Sumo  - 1 no

 Taxi  - 1 no

 Car (Nano) - 1 no.

 M/Cycles - 3 nos.

 After they were forcefully dispersed by the Assam Police, at around 12:30 p.m, the MZP members gathered in front of Bairabi Police Station wherein they expressed their anger to the Mizoram Police for their inaction in the wake of atrocities committed against them by Assam Police. Thereafter, they proceeded to Bairabi PHC where their fellow students are being treated with their injuries.

 The MZP passed the following resolutions regarding the border issue as under:-

 1. Zofate Chawlhbuk shall be constructed at Zophai by MZP.

 2. MZP strongly condemned the use of firearms against their members by  Assam Police.

 3. MZP strongly condemned Government of Mizoram for not taking  significant steps towards protection of the State territory.

 4. The Assam Government should duly compensate the students whose  properties have been destroyed by the Assam Police.

 5. MZP will look after the injured students and will not leave them in the  lurch.

 6. MZP is thankful to residents of Bairabi for their support.

 7. MZP will organise a procession in Aizawl and at all other MZP Hqrs. &amp;  Sub-Hqrs. on 12.3.2018 (Monday) in order to show their strong  determination to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk.

12.3.2018 Today, i.e. 12.3.2018 @ 10:30 a.m, a procession called ‘Ram Humhalh Kawngzawh’ was organised under the aegis of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) in Aizawl and in other towns of the State such as Lunglei, Champhai, Serchhip, Kolasib, Thenzawl, Vairengte, Sairang, Saitual, Tlabung, Bairabi, Bilkhawthlir, Zawlnuam and Mamit wherein a large number of students took to the streets. Situation was peaceful in all the towns and it has been reported that an effigy of Shri. Adil Khan, DC of Hailakandi District, who had reportedly given the firing order against MZP members on 10.3.2018, was burnt by MZP at Tlabung.

  In Aizawl, the procession began at 10:30 a.m from Chandmari in the North and from Sikulpuikawn in the South and converged at Vanapa Hall. Around 6,000 (six thousand) students participated in the procession who shouted slogans condemning the State Government for its alleged inaction relating to the border issue and their strong intention to construct Zofate Chawlhbuk at Zophai. A function was held in front of Vanapa Hall under the chairmanship of Michael Lalramsanga, Treasurer, MZP Gen. Hqrs. wherein Lalnunmawia Pautu, Gen. Secy., MZP; B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP; R.B. Lalmalsawma, President, MSU and Zorammawia, Vice President, Aizawl City Colleges Joint Students’ Union (ACCJSU) and Pu Vanlalruata, President, CYMA delivered speeches. Adamant with their intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk, B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP announced before the gathering that MZP will reconstruct 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' at Zophai on 14.3.2018 (Wednesday). They also appealed all political parties of the State not to politicise the issue in order to gain political advantage.

 MZP passed the following resolutions today :-

  i) MZP strongly condemned the Assam Government for invoking Section 144CrPC on the soil of Mizoram and also condemned the State Government for turning a deaf ear to the border issue.

   ii) Government of Mizoram should protect the boundary of the State.

  iii) MZP will continue to render utmost effort to protect Mizoram and her people.

   iv) 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' should be reconstructed.

 The processionists peacefully dispersed @ 1:30 p.m and no untoward incident has been reported from any part of the State today. Further input indicated that MZP will hold an Extended Office Bearers’ Meeting at their office tomorrow, i.e. 13.3.2018 @ 10:30 a.m and they are likely to discuss their future course of action regarding the border issue.

13.3.2018 The Mizoram Journalists’ Association (MJA) General Hqrs. had observed a Sit-in Demonstration in front of Vanapa Hall today, i.e. 13.3.2018 from 12:00 noon - 1:00 p.m in protest against the alleged brutal attack on Journalists by personnel of Assam Police on 10.3.2018 at Zophai, Kolasib District at Mizoram-Assam border. The same had also been observed in other Districts by MJA members across the State. Pu Lal Thanzara, Hon'ble I&amp;PR Minister who visited the MJA Sit-in Demonstration in front of Vanapa Hall today @ 12:25 p.m had expressed support for their cause and told Journalists that the Government had already conveyed displeasure to Assam Government, and also wished speedy recovery to the injured Journalists. The Minister was accompanied by Pu P.C. Lalthanliana, Hon'ble Minister, LAD and Pu Chalrosanga, MLA. The Press Council of India, in a letter dated 10.3.2018 addressed to the Chief Reporter, Chief of Bureau, had also expressed strong condemnation of Assam Police for their brutal acts on Journalists, and demanded the Assam Government to identify and take strict action against Police personnel involved in the assault.

2.4.2018 1) Today, i.e. 2.4.2018 @ 10:00 a.m, around 150 (one hundred fifty) students of National Institute of Technology (NIT), Mizoram staged a Sit-in demonstration in front of NIT, Mizoram office at Chaltlang, Aizawl in protest against the alleged mismanagement of NIT Mizoram by officials of NIT, Mizoram. The Sit-in demonstration continued till 6:00 p.m today and is likely to be resumed by 9:00 a.m tomorrow, i.e. 3.4.2018. Leaders of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) and North East Students' Organization (NESO) also expressed their support to the students of NIT in their agitation. In a letter addressed to the Hon'ble Chief Minister of Mizoram and to the Ministry of Human Resource Development (HRD) dated today, i.e. 2.4.2018, students of NIT, Mizoram accused NIT, Mizoram of mismanaging NIT administration especially that of the hostel which led to the death of Devsharan Kumar (B.Tech Ist Yr) on 31.3.2018. Students of NIT, Mizoram urged the Hon'ble Chief Minister of Mizoram and authorities of HRD Ministry to take steps towards improving the NIT administration and also to take necessary action against the erring officials. Students of NIT, Mizoram also intended to meet the Hon'ble Governor of Mizoram at the earliest.

 2) Lawngtlai District Land Owners' Association (LDLOA) held a meeting at their office, Lawngtlai today, i.e. 2.4.2018 @ 7:00 a.m under the chairmanship of Pu H. Remmawia, President, LDLOA. The meeting decided to stage indefinite blockade of a highway constructed under the Kaladan Multi-Modal Transit Transport Project (KMMTTP) from today, i.e. 2.4.2018 in protest against alleged non-payment of compensation for their lands to be acquired for the ongoing highway construction works. The LDLOA slammed the Central Government for turning a deaf ear to their demands even after the Deputy Commissioner of Lawngtlai had reportedly approved as many as 303 (three hundred three) compensation applications. They passed a resolution that LDLOA will not allow any constructions works to be carried out by RDS and ARSS companies at the site and that any violation of the diktat will invite stern reaction from the LDLOA.

Around 100 (one hundred) students of NIT, Mizoram organised a demonstration in front of the office of Director, NIT, Mizoram at Chaltlang, Aizawl since 11:50 a.m today.

 2) Lawngtlai District Land Owners’ Association (LDLOA) continued blockade of the under construction Kaladan Multi-Modal Transit Transport Project (KMMTTP) highway today, i.e. 4.4.2018 in demand for immediate payment of compensation for their lands acquired for the ongoing Highway construction works. They do not allow any construction works to be carried out by RDS and ARSS companies at the site since 1stApril, 2018. At the same time, the Assistant General Manager (AGM) of RDS Project Ltd. has sought the intervention of the Chief Engineer (Highways), Mizoram PWD to resolve the issue in consultation with all concerned departments for timely completion of the works.

9.4.2018 1) Khawzawl District Implementation Demand Committee (KDIDC) in a Press Release issued today, i.e. 9.4.2018 highlighted that they organised a public rally at Dinthar Bazar, Khawzawl, Champhai District this morning demanding immediate implementation of Khawzawl as a full-fledged District. Around 300 (three hundred) residents of Khawzawl participated in the rally and passed the following resolutions:-

 (i) The State Government must declare Khawzawl as a full-fledged District before a Model Code of Conduct is enforced in the State.

 (ii) If the State Government implements Khawzawl as a full-fledged District, only Congress party may contest Tuichang Constituency in the upcoming Mizoram Legislative Assembly General Election, 2018. 

 (iii) If Khawzawl is not declared as a full-fledged District along with other towns, Congress party may not take the trouble of contesting the Constituency and KDIDC volunteers will take all necessary steps towards implementation of its demands.

 2) Tawipui South Joint Action Committee in a Press Release issued on 8.4.2018 demanded that :-

 (i) The State Government should cancel the transfer order of Headmaster, Govt. High School, Tawipui South and that two posts of Teacher that are lying vacant at the High School due to transfer and retirement of incumbent Teachers must be filled immediately.

 (ii) The State Government should take necessary action to run Govt. Primary School-I, Tawipui South as an English Medium School from the Academic Session 2018-2019.

 (iii) The State Government must appoint Ayush Doctor, Dental Surgeon, Pharmacist and Health Supervisor (Male) at the Primary Health Centre (PHC), Tawipui.

 (iv) A Police Station/Out Post should be opened at Tawipui South.

 In demand for immediate implementation of their various demands, Tawipui South Joint Action Committee begun indefinite picketing of all Educational Institutions at Tawipui South from today, i.e. 9.4.2018.

High School, Tawipui South and immediate posting of two Teachers at the same school, etc. It has been reported that if no positive response is received from the State Government, they will continue with their strike tomorrow, i.e. 11.2.2018 and that they are likely to convene a meeting tomorrow to discuss their future course of action on the issue.

 The processionists adopted resolutions demanding the Government to immediately take steps to create a new Administrative District for the Northern Hill area which they claimed is lagging far behind in terms of developments compared to other parts of Mizoram, and that the 41 (forty one) villages within their demand area should not be divided or included in other districts. 4.5.2018 The imbroglio between Zokhawthar NGOs and Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab operators over the rate of Maxi Cab Fare continued till today, i.e. 4.5.2018 as the Maxi Cab operators on Champhai side had stopped and stranded 4 (four) Sumos carrying passengers from Zokhawthar at Ruantlang en-route Champhai today @ 3:00 p.m. It is reported that about 25 (twenty five) Maxi Cab drivers remained on duty at Ruantlang today which has been seen as a fallout of the Zokhawthar NGO's stoppage of Maxi Cab Service since 30.4.2018 demanding lowering of rate of Maxi Cab fare from ` 150/- to ` 100/-. It is learnt that the 4 (four) Sumos stranded at Ruantlang had come after agreeing the rate fixed by the Zokhawthar NGOs, i.e. ` 100/-.

8.5.2018 The two-day Total Bandh called by Tawipui South JAC was observed from 5:00 a.m today, All Government offices and Educational Institutions remained closed. The National Highway 54 has been blocked and about 150 (one hundred fifty) persons turned up for Bandh duty. Around 35 (thirty five) different vehicles have been stranded at the time of writing this report. The situation is reported to be otherwise peaceful and no untoward incident reported during the day.

9.5.2018 1) The imbroglio between NGOs of Zokhawthar and Maxi cab operators over the rate of Maxi Cab fare continues even as DTO Champhai served a notice to the Maxi Cab operators to follow the rate fixed by the Government. Following the stoppage of Maxi cab service by NGOs of Zokhawthar and the counter action by the Maxi Cab operators, the DTO had issued by a notice on 8.5.2018 to the Champhai to Zokhawthar Sumo Service Association to follow the Government approved rate, i.e. Rs. 67.20 (Rs. 2.40 per km unmetalled) and threatened to initiate action to the extent of cancellation of their Route permit. It may be recalled that the Maxi Cab operators had earlier charged Rs. 100/- and later increased the rate to Rs.150/- on their own. In reply to this, the Maxi Cab operators had submitted a petition to the DTO Champhai in which they pleaded that even Zokhawthar to Aizawl service Maxi Cabs had not been following Government approved rates, and also that the rates of Taxi and Two wheeler service within Zokhawthar Town are Rs. 100/- and Rs. 50/- respectively which is much higher in comparision to that of Champhai to Zokhawthar.

 In the meantime, the Villace Council and NGOs of Melbuk had also issued a statement on 8.5.2018 expressing support to the NGOs of Zokhawthar stating that not only the people of Zokhawthar, but also the people of Melbuk had been affected by the increase of Maxi Cab fare.

 It is reported that the Maxi Cab owners of Zokhawthar are willing to ply at the rate of Rs. 100/- whereas, the Association maintained their stand at Rs. 150/-.

 2) The 2nd day of Total Bandh organized by Tawipui South JAC was observed today. All together 33 (thirty three) vehicles have been stranded and about 175 (one hundred seventy five) people turned up for bandh duty. The situation is reported to be otherwise peaceful without untoward incident during the day. A meeting between the JAC leaders and the officials of District administration was held at 3:00 p.m at VC Conference Hall. Outcome of the meeting is awaited.

10.5.2018 1) Following the notice issued to the Maxi Cab operators to follow the Government approved rates, the Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab operators met the DTO, Champhai today, i.e. 10.5.2018 @ 1:00 p.m in his office chamber in which the DTO had offered them to continue their service at the rate of Rs. 100/- instead of Rs. 67.20/- (Government approved rate). It is learnt that the Maxi Cab operators will have a consultation amongst themselves on the offer made by the DTO, and in the meantime, called off their duty near Ruantlang temporarily for coming two/three days.

 2) The two-day Total bandh organized by Tawipui South JAC had been called off at 7:00 p.m tonight, i.e. 10.5.2018 following the assurance by DC, Lunglei to pursue their demands with the Government except their demand pertaining to establishing a Rural RD Block at Tawipui South. The JAC will decide their further course of action if their demands are not met by the Government on or before 30.5.2018.

21.5.2018 1) A Sit-in demonstration was staged in front of Vanapa Hall, Aizawl today, i.e. 21.5.2018 organised by Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) and North East Students' Organisation (NESO) in protest against the Citizenship Amendment Bill, 2016 which incorporated the provisions of regularisation of Citizenship of foreign nationals namely, Bangladesh, Afghanistan and Pakistan if he/she resides in India for a period of six (6) years which they perceived will open the doors for assimilation of Zo-indigeneous people by foreign nationals. The programme was chaired by B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP and a speech was delivered by L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, President, MZP. MZP has urged all MsLA to pass a Resolution opposing this Bill in the Assembly House. It is reported that around 80 (eighty) students including 54 (fifty four) students from Springfield HSS attended the Sit-in demonstration programme. It is also reported that representatives from CYMA, MUP, MHIP and MSU expressed their resentment against the Citizenship Amendment Bill, 2016.

24.5.2018 The impasse over the rate of Maxi Cab fare on Champhai - Zokhawthar route had finally been solved as both the NGOs of Zokhawthar and the Maxi Cab operators agreed at the rate of Rs. 100/- after several rounds of negotiations. It is reported that a meeting between NGOs of Zokhawthar and Maxi Cab Operators (Champhai - Zokhawthar Sumo Service Association and Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab Owners Welfare Committee) held last night (23.5.2018) at Zokhawthar YMA Hall which was attended by about 30 (thirty) members, had reached an agreement and decided to continue their service at the rate of Rs. 100/- from today, i.e. 24.5.2018.

6.6.2018 Mizoram Underground Returnees Association (MURA) has decided to go ahead with their proposed hunger strike from this evening, i.e. 6.6.2018 at their office to press upon the MPCC to fulfill the agreement with respect to grant of rehabilitation to the MURA members. In a statement issued today, MURA has expressed disappointment with the MPCC for non-implementation of the agreement signed almost ten years ago, and stated that they had to carry out a 'fast unto death' until their demands are met. It is reported that 20 (twenty) persons have volunteered for the hunger strike to be started from this evening at their office at Tuikual.

7.6.2018 Mizoram Government Lumpsum Grant-in-aid Higher School Association (MIGLAHSSA), 9 (nine) Higher Secondary Schools run by local bodies, observed 'Demand Day', today, i.e. 7.6.2018 in which they attended school without teaching the students in demand for up-gradation to Adhoc-aided status. In each school, the teachers addressed their students apprising them of the reasons for their action and the need for up-gradation of their school. They claimed that the Government's neglect compelled them to resort to this action and that they will continue pressing their demand so that these 9 (nine) schools, which have been managed by local citizens for more than 13 years, can get Adhoc-aided status.

As per the agreement, BSNL will upgrade the Internet Broadband speed from the current 14 Mbps to 100 Mbps within 6 (six) months. BSNL has also agreed to give a 50% rebate for three months, i.e. March to May, 2018 to its postpaid subscribers.

MNYF also urged the Government not to engage the 4 (four) incumbent Lottery Firms in future as their performance was far from satisfactory and strongly demanded the investigation of Lottery Scam by Central Bureau of Investigation (CBI) to unearth the truth. MNF also asserted that they would take all possible efforts to fulfill their demands, the Press Statement added.

26.7.2018 1) In connection with the demands made by Mizoram Govt. Lumpsum Grant-in-Aid Higher Secondary School Association (MIGLAHSSA), it has been reported that Joint Students' Union, Managing Boards and Joint Action Committee of the 9 (nine) Lumpsum Grant-in-Aid Higher Secondary Schools commenced road blockade, closure of all Schools and picketing of Government Offices (except Hospitals) in their respective areas from 6:00 a.m today, i.e. 26.7.2018. Road blockades at West Phaileng, East Phaileng and Thingsulthliah had been temporarily called off @ 3:30 p.m, 6:00 p.m and 6:00 p.m respectively which will be resumed tomorrow @ 6:00 a.m, while it has been continued in other places till the writing of this report. Police force has been deployed for continuous duty in each village by concerned District Authorities. There has been no report of any major untoward incident reported due to the demonstration so far.

 2) Today, i.e. 26.7.2018 @ 11:00 a.m, about 20 (twenty) MSU members entered the Office of the Director, National Institute of Technology (NIT) at Chaltlang as they reportedly learnt that Dr. Bijayanta Mohanty, Asst. Professor, Civil Engineering Department was still taking class despite their notice to leave Mizoram, and vandalized the Director's Room accusing him of allowing Dr. Bijayanta Mohanty to continue his service till date. Thereafter, the MSU again entered and vandalized Civil Engineering Classroom also. The value of the property destroyed/damaged is estimated to be approximately Rs. 4,47,832/-. It may be recalled that the MSU had demanded transfer of Dr. Bijayanta Mohanty out of Mizoram on 7thMarch, 2018 for his alleged misconduct with the students. In this regard, Bawngkawn PS Case No. 175/18 dated 26/7/2018 u/s 448/506/427/34 IPC has been registered.

 3) The Joint Students’ Union of 9 (nine) Schools of MIGLAHSSA in a Press Release issued today, i.e. 26.7.2018 expressed gratitude to the public for their support and cooperation. They further notified that the road blockades would be continued tomorrow and their members from Thingsulthliah village will remain on duty at Tuirini point, so that the highway (en-route Champhai) will be blocked from tomorrow onwards.

27.7.2018 In connection with the demands made by Mizoram Govt. Lumpsum Grant-in-Aid Higher Secondary School Association (MIGLAHSSA), it has been reported that Joint Students' Union, Managing Boards and Joint Action Committee of the 9 (nine) Lumpsum Grant-in-Aid Higher Secondary Schools continued road blockade, closure of all Schools and picketing of Government Offices (except Hospitals) in their respective areas today, i.e. 27.7.2018. Lungdar tomorrow, i.e. 27.7.2018 and Zobawk from 30.7.2018 (Monday). It is reported that Phullen, N.E. Khawdungsei, Thingsulthliah and Sakawrdai are yet to decide their future course of action. There has been no report of any major untoward incident reported due to the demonstration so far.

9.8.2018 Mizoram Government Aided School Association (MIGASA) started observing ‘No Teaching Day’ from today, i.e. 9.8.2018 which will last till 17.8.2018 in their demand for upgradation to Adhoc Grant-in-Aid Status. There are 27 (twenty seven) High Schools and 33 (thirty three) Middle Schools under MIGASA.

10.8.2018 It has been reported that leaders of NGO Coordination Committee expressed serious concern over the conduct of Electoral Roll Revision of voters at Bru Refugee Camps in Tripura as per the direction of Election Commission of India in spite of repeated appeals made by the NGO Coordination Committee not to conduct Electoral Roll Revision. It has also been reported that Langkaih Group YMA, Taitesena Group YMA and Mizo Zirlai Pawl Sub-Hqrs., Zawlnuam under the direction of NGO Coordination Committee, launched a road blockade at Zawlnuam today, i.e. 10.8.2018 @ 2:00 p.m, preventing the Booth Level Officer (BLO) and party coming from Mamit to conduct Electoral Roll Revision at Bru Refugee Camps in Tripura. Consequent upon this, leaders of YMA and MZP held a meeting in the Office of BDO, Zawlnuam to discuss their further action.

31.8.2018 Khawzawl District Implementation Demand Committee (KDIDC) organised Khawzawl District Implementation Demand Procession today, i.e. 31.8.2018 @ 9:30 a.m. Around 600 (six hundred) people participated in the procession. Pu Malsawmdawngliana, Chairman, KDIDC in his speech highlighted that KDIDC will continue to take all the necessary initiative for the implementation of Khawzawl District. The procession ended at around 11:40 a.m.

5.9.2018 All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit took out a procession today, i.e. 5.9.2018 @ 12:00 noon from Charkawn, Mamit to Deputy Commissioner Complex, Mamit in demand for transfer of Shri. Bhupesh Chaudhary, Deputy Commissioner from Mamit District. Around 800 (eight hundred) persons took part in the procession. Leaders of All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit including leaders of CYMA, MZP, etc. delivered speeches during the procession which ended at around 1:50 p.m. The following resolutions were passed by All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit :-

 i) All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit protest the discreet conduct of Electoral Roll Revision at Tripura.

 ii) All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit will not allow polling of votes by the Bru voters outside of Mizoram in the upcoming MLA General Election - 2018.

 iii) All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit expressed doubt over Shri. Bhupesh Chaudhary to conduct free and fair MLA Election-2018 at Mamit District.

  iv) All NGOs &amp; All Political Parties, Mamit demanded the State Government to issue transfer order for Shri. Bhupesh Chaudhary out from Mamit District on or before 10.9.2018.

10.9.2018 Today, i.e. 10.9.2018, about 100 (one hundred) members of MPCC, following the decision taken by All India Congress Committee, gathered in front of Vanapa Hall with banners and placards in protest against the recent hike in the price of Oil and Gases by BJP Government. Shri. Pradyut Bordoloi, Vice President, Assam Pradesh Congress Committee, who was sent by All India Congress Committee for this purpose stated that, ever since the BJP came into power, there is unprecedented price rise in oil and natural gas and Rupee is now at its lowest value. He further pointed out that RSS, who are the driving force of the BJP Government are all against the people of North East. He also added that BJP/RSS would like to prop up MNF in the front and will try to rule Mizoram by proxy and that is why MNF has not been protesting against the anti-Mizoram and anti-people policies of the BJP Government in Delhi.

11.9.2018 Information has been received that Tlabung RD Block Demand Committee organised a procession today, i.e. 11.9.2018 @ 12:30 a.m. from Zodin Junction to Bazar Bungkawn in which around 400 peoples participated. The procession passed a resolution which condemned the Government for not creating Tlabung RD Block till date even though the area is one of the most in need. The resolution also demanded its immediate creation while stating that no Political Party should attempt to take opportunistic advantage of the situation and that they fully supported any decision taken by the Demand Committee in pressing their demand, even to the extent of boycotting the coming State Legislative Assembly General Election.

17.9.2018 A procession organised by the MIGLAHSSA Joint Students' Union was carried out as intended earlier in which about 250 (two hundred fifty) students from various 9 (nine) Community-run Higher Secondary Schools participated. Speeches were delivered at Chanmari, Zarkawt and Vanapa Hall mainly deploring the Government's failure to concede their demand for an Adhoc Grant-in-Aid status. A resolution was adopted stating they would seek all possible steps to create new Government who would concede their demand if the Government fails to fulfil their demand during the current term.

18.9.2018 NGO Coordination Committee, Aizawl held a meeting last night, i.e. 17.9.2018 @ 7:30 p.m at CYMA Office which was followed by CYMA CEC Emergency Meeting @ 8:30 p.m at the same venue. CYMA came to know that Mamit DC had left Mamit for Aizawl @ 6:30 p.m the same evening and spread emergency notice for public gathering to receive him. The public gathered at Aizawl Tennis Court (around 150), New Secretariat Gate-1 (around 50) and Gate-2 (around 70) under the aegis of CYMA and later dispersed @ 12:15 to 12:30 a.m after the DC did not arrive as expected.

 Input has been received that all NGOs Mamit picketed Mamit DC Office and Mamit DC Office was closed today. More than 1,000 (one thousand) persons gathered in front of Mamit DC Office gate. The public gathering was presided over by Pu Lalropuia, Treasurer, Sub-Hqrs. YMA, Mamit. Pu K. Ely Rosanga, President, Sub-Hqrs. YMA, Mamit addressed the picketers and burnt the effigy of Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary and they dispersed @ 10:50 a.m.

19.9.2018 Information has been received that NGO Coordination Committee, Mamit had stopped picketing of Mamit DC Office and the Office is opened normally as Mamit DC, Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary left Mamit. But they stated that they will strongly react if Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary return to Mamit. Input has been received that NGO Coordination Committee, Aizawl do not have action plan, but they intended to hold Coordination Committee Meeting soon to deliberate on whether to organize a procession or Total Bandh in demand of the transfer out of Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary from Mizoram.

20.9.2018 Information has been received that All Mizoram Tanker Drivers' Association called off their strike following talks with Police authorities in which it was decided to relax 'No Entry' between Edenthar and Thuampui, Aizawl. They have resumed transportation of Oil from today, i.e. 20.9.2018.

24.9.2018 NHM (National Health Mission) Contractual Association of Mizoram (NCAM) has issued a statement today, i.e. 24.9.2018 informing all its members across Mizoram to wear black badges today to show their grievances over non-receipt of their salaries regularly. About 30 (thirty) members gathered at High Field later in the afternoon today @ around 2:15 p.m with an intention to submit a Memorandum to the Hon'ble Health Minister, with a copy to the Hon'ble Chief Minister.

 It has been reported that the NCAM members, upon learning that the Hon'ble Health Minister had left office for the day, dispersed @ 4:00 p.m and notified all its members presently staying in Aizawl to assemble at High Field to submit the Memorandum tomorrow at 11:00 a.m.

25.9.2018 MNYF in a Press Release issued today, i.e. 25.9.2018 stated that MNYF submitted a memo today to Pu Lal Thanzara, Hon'ble PWD Minister demanding the publish of Enquiry Report on the collapsed of Tuirini Bridge before the end of September, 2018. The PR stated several MNF youths led by 2 (two) of their leaders went to submit the memo and Pu Lalzahawma Khiangte, MNYF Treasurer addressed these youths in which he stated that Pu Lal Thanzara has no idea the reason and those responsible for the collapsed of Tuirini Bridge which clearly indicated that he is incompetent to execute the responsibilities of his office.

 It has been reported that MNYF led by their 2 (two) leaders numbering around 20 (twenty) proceeded towards Chief Minister's Office (CMO) to submit the memo @ 11:00 a.m. MPYCC, having caught wind of this also proceeded towards CMO and around 50 (fifty) members gathered in front of CMO. In order to prevent possible altercation between both party youths, the Police prevented all MNF youths from entering the premises and allowed 10 (ten) persons to enter with another 5 (five) led by their leaders entering the building to submit the memo after which they left the CMO peacefully. It was also reported that MPYCC intended to block if all of them were allowed to enter the CMO premises which could possibly have led to a serious Law and Order situation.

26.9.2018 It has been reported that Kolasib District MNF Joint Block Committee organised National Highway (NH-54) Road Block today, i.e. 26.9.2018 from 5:00 a.m at the following points, viz. Kawnpui, Khuangpuilam, Rengtekawn Zero Point, Bairabi, Bilkhawthlir Chemphai peng, Bualpui and Vairengte-Lailapur Aurorickshaw Stand. 28.9.2018 1) All India Organization of Chemists &amp; Druggists (AIOCD) closed their shop today, i.e. 28.9.2018 in protest against 'On-line Sale of Medicine through E-Portal'. In support of this, Mizoram Chemists &amp; Druggists Association (MCDA) also closed all their shops excluding Hospital Canteens and Government Pharmacies. Posters showing the reason of their strike and regret for inconveniences to patients were attached on the walls of their shops.

 2) AMFU Gen. Hqrs. organized a Protest March, "Mizoram Kuthnathawktute Chhanchhuahna Kawngzawh" today, i.e. 28.9.2018 as a demand for implementation of Land Reform and Agricultural Marketing, in which around 200 (two hundred) members participated. The procession started from Chanmari Kawn @ 12:30 p.m wherein a short programme was held. Pu Lalnungliana, Vice President, AMFU addressed the public in which he asked public forgiveness for the inconvenience they caused due to their procession and Pu Zion Lalremruata, Gen. Secretary also delivered a speech. Pu Lalnungliana also burnt copies of ‘The Mizoram Agriculture Produces (Restriction on Movement) Order, 1994’ and ‘The Mizoram Agriculture Products Prohibition (Amendment) Order, 1999’. The procession halted at Israel Point in which Pu R. Laltluanga, Treasurer, AMFU delivered a speech and stated that the Government neglected the farmers and they need a new Government who cares for the farmers. The procession was stopped at Vanapa Hall and Pu Joseph H. Lalthanzuala, President, AMFU addressed the procession and stated that it is sad to organize a protest march because the Government neglected the farmers and that the Government’s claim of farmers as their VIP is a lie. He also stated that they condemned the accusation of farmers as being responsible for the low production of food and agricultural products. He further stated that NLUP scheme is not designed for the development of farmers but for political tools. Gingers brought by the farmers were dumped in front of Vanapa Hall as it is claimed there is no market. They shouted together demanding for Land Reform, Regulated Market and Government who cares for farmers. They also held placards, "We want good marketing system", "We want to sell our products at a better price", “We demand APLM Act Implementation", "We want a reliable system of Agriculture Marketing", etc. The procession was dispersed at 2:15 p.m and it was followed by an Executive Committee Meeting at AMFU Office, Venghlui, Aizawl. The meeting was chaired by Pu Joseph H. Lalthanzuala and attended by 15 (fifteen) members. The meeting decided to wait for the Government till 3.10.2018 and if there is no action taken from the Government, they intended to organise Economic Blockade date and time of which will be decided later.

 3) Champhai MZP had started closing down all Educational Institutions and Government Offices today, i.e. 28.9.2018. About 450-500 College students participated in the picketing which was done at the following 8 (eight) places :-

 i) District Court, Zote.

 ii) SDEO's Office, Bethel.

 iii) BDO's Office, Ruantlang.

 iv) PHED Office, Vengsang.

 v) Chief Medical Officer's Office, Vengsang.

 vi) DEO/SSA Office, Kahrawt.

 vii) Chanem Building (Treasury Office and Supply Department Office).

 viii) DC/SP Offices, Keifangtlang.

 The MZP picketers converged at their Office at Chanem Building @ 3:30 p.m in which they discussed about their future course of action and decided to go further ahead with their 'Action Plan' on 1.10.2018.

1.10.2018 The DC, Champhai had promulgated 144 CrPC, 1973 yesterday, i.e. 30.9.2018, prohibiting gathering of more than 5 (five) persons with intention to disrupting official works within 1(one) Km of DC and SP Offices. As soon as the MZP noticed about the Promulgation order, members of MZP proceeded to DC Complex and gathered the whole night. Police immediately encircled DC Office to restraint MZP to enter into vicinity of DC Complex. MZP Sub-Hqrs. of Khawbung, Dungtlang, Farkawn, Khuangleng and Hnahlan also issued a Press Release yesterday, i.e. 30.9.2018 for supporting the agitation of MZP Hqrs., Champhai. In continuation of the agitation, MZP Hqrs., Champhai organized a procession today, i.e. 1.10.2018 as demand for filling up the posts of Ophthalmologist and Orthopaedic at Champhai District Hospital. The procession was started from Champhai Vengsang @10:00 a.m in which around 500 (five hundred) students participated in the procession. The agitating College students were joined by Higher Secondary Students today. Students held placards and raised slogans of demanding Orthopaedic and Ophthalmologist at Champhai District Hospital and blamed the Mizoram Government for the neglect of District Hospital, Champhai. After conducting the peaceful procession at around 11:00 a.m, OBs of MZP were called by DC, Champhai and told the good news about the Mizoram Government proposal for posting of Ophthalmologist. The agitating students gathered at Govt. Champhai College Complex waiting for the posting order of the demand doctors and further instructions from their leaders. Agreement was made by making condition that Ophthalmologist will be posted and Government of Mizoram will do its level best for posting of Orthopedic as soon as possible. The MZP officially withdrew their agitation at 2:30 p.m.

3.10.2018 Mizoram Maxi Cab Owners' Association (MMCOA) organized an indefinite strike in which all Maxi Cab service ceased their service from today, i.e. 3.10.2018 as a demand from the Government to raise Maxi Cab rate for metalled road @ Rs.3/-per Km/head and unmetalled road @ Rs. 3.50/- per Km/head and also re-issue of All Mizoram Permit. Information has been received that there was no Maxi Cab service throughout the State in support of this strike.

 MMCOA issued a Press Release today, i.e. 3.10.2018 in which they condemned the Press Release issued by the Mizoram Consumers’ Union yesterday, i.e. 2.10.2018 regarding against the indefinite strike organized by MMCOA. In their PR, they accused the MCU of interfering beyond their duties. The PR also asked public to bear with them for the inconvenience caused due to their strike.

6.10.2018 Mizoram Maxi Cab Owners Association (MMCOA) held an Executive Meeting on 6.10.2018 @ 4:30 p.m at MMCOA Office, Chaltlang which was chaired by Pu C. Lalthanmawia, President, MMCOA and attended by 10 (ten) members. They issued a Press Release which stated that their indefinite strike was called-off due to announcement of MLA Election for Mizoram State and further added notes of apology to the public for inconvenience they caused during the strike.

10.10.2018 1) CYMA organized a procession today, i.e.10.10.2018 @ 11:00 a.m as a demand for dissolution of Chakma Autonomous District Council (CADC) which they believed was created illegitimately. The procession started from two points - Sikulpuikawn and Chanmari simultaneously and moved towards the courtyard of Vanapa Hall, around 8,000 (eight thousand) members participated and students also participated as well. At Chanmari Kawn, a short function was held before the procession started which was presided over by Pu Lalrochuanga Pachuau, Treasurer, CYMA and L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, MZP President delivered a speech. A short function was also held at Sikulpuikawn which was presided over by Pu Peter Chhakchuak, Asst. Secretary, CYMA and Pu R. Lalngheta, Vice President, CYMA delivered a speech. The procession started from two points was converged at the courtyard of Vanapa Hall which was followed by a short function in which Pu R. Lalngheta presided over the programme and Pu Vanlalruata, President, CYMA addressed the participants. Slogans were raised and placards against CADC were also displayed during the procession. The procession ended peacefully at 12:40 p.m. After the procession, around 10 (ten) CYMA leaders met Governor at his residence and submitted a petition for permanent abolition of unconstitutional and illegal creation of CADC. The petition contains that Chakmas were not the indigenous inhabitant of Mizoram and they are illegal migrants and foreigners who entered Mizoram illegally. Even the indigenous peoples (Mizos) have no rights in CADC areas. There were a number of lapses and unconstitutional procedure for the creation of CADC which violated North Eastern Areas Re-organization (NEAR) Act, 1971 and UT Act, 1971. They strongly requested the Governor to abolish the unconstitutional and illegal creation of CADC in Southern Mizoram.

 Simultaneous processions were also carried out by 5 (five) Sub-Hqrs., 7 (seven) Groups and 6 (six) Branches at various town/villages within the State in which more than 10,000 (ten thousand) members participated.

 In regard to the procession held within Aizawl City and various parts of Mizoram today, CYMA issued a Press Release today itself wherein they expressed their gratitude towards those who participated in their procession which was held today and further added their apology to public for causing inconvenience in the said regard. CYMA in their PR also requested public cooperation towards their initiatives in safeguarding Mizoram and its people in the future.

 2) MZP Hqrs. Champhai is intending to restrain the Chakma students who are going to give Secondary School (Cl-X) and Senior Secondary School (Cl-XII) Examinations at Zokhawpui Higher Secondary School (National Institute of Open Schooling), Champhai. 10 (ten) Chakma students from Lunglei Study Centre have reached Champhai to give exam at NIOS Centre Champhai, scheduled on 11.10.2018. Leaders of MZP Champhai Hqrs. have informed Pu Lalhmingmawia, Teacher of Lunglei Study Centre, who accompanied the Chakma students at Champhai that the MZP would not allow Chakma students to do examination. Later @ around 5:00 p.m, leaders of MZP Hqrs. Champhai went to the place where the Chakma students are accomodated (Pu Chalbawiha building, Champhai Vengthlang) and warned them not to give examination at Champhai and not to choose Champhai Centre in future. It is learnt that the Chakma students accordingly agreed to go back and they are planning to return to their place on 11.10.2018.

****w.e.f. 2014 – till date****

****2014****

4.2.2014 Around 80 members of YMA volunteers/members under YMA Sub-Headquarters Mamit launched search operation for Deep Mandal (one of the three hostages who is still held in captivity by abductors) till date. The search party of YMA members held a meeting today at West Phaileng under the leadership of Pu.Lalhmachhuana, Assistant Secretary CYMA. The search party will halt for tonight at Damparengpui. The Search operation is being launched under the command of Pu.H.Vanlalhlua, President YMA Sub-Headquarters Mamit.

10.2.2014 Sangau Block Youth Organisation (SBYO) General Headquarters, Sangau burnt the copy of Mizoram Rural Development Department (MGNREGA) 2014 Calendar today, i.e.10.2.2014 in protest against the alleged wrong display of achievement of Rural Development in Sangau village. The SBYO urged Rural Development Department, Government of Mizoram to tender public apology at the earliest.

12.2.2014 1) Around sixty (60) student activists of Mizo Students' Union (MSU) General Headquarters organized a peaceful demonstration today in front of Raj Bhawan South Gate in protest against the alleged rape of one Mizo teenager at Delhi on 7.2.2014. The MSU also submitted a memorandum addressed to Hon'ble Minister, Ministry of Home Affairs through the Governor of Mizoram seeking for the safety and security of the people of North East living in Delhi.

 2) Mizoram Postal Employee Union (MPEU) have also joined the two-day strike called by National Federation of Postal Employees from today due to which all postal officers within Aizawl city shall remain closed during 12-13.2.2014.

22.2.2014 In a bid to sanitize and stop the illegal sale of liquor at Phunchawng which is a village at the entrance of Aizawl city, a raid was conducted on 22.2.2014 under the aegis of Phunchawng Local Council consisting around 230 volunteers. During the sanitization operation, a substantial amount of local made liquor, around 180 litres, were seized and the same was disposed off.

3.3.2014 Last night, i.e. 2.3.2014, local angry mob of Lawngtlai Vengpui locality assembled near the main gate of District Jail, Lawngtlai in protest against the alleged assault case of Pu Laltanpuia (35 yrs) S/o K. Hautawna (L), Lawngtlai Vengpui by two accused persons namely, Lalfakliana (20 yrs) S/o Lalmalsawma and Laltanpuia (24yrs) S/o L.C. Vanmawia. The irate mob finally dispersed after 74 rounds of ammunition were fired in the air by Armed Police following the order of Magistrate. The situation is closely monitored and no untoward incident is reported so far.
11.3.2014 Around fifty (50) MNYF activists assembled at Mizo Hnam Run, Aizawl last night at around 7:00 PM in protest against shifting of those Electronic Voting Machines affected by the election petition filed by the Opposition Mizo National Front in Guwahati High Court. They were however peacefully dispersed at around 8:30 PM after they got assurance from Election Officials that those EVMs affected by the election petition will remain under the safe custody of District Election Officers/RO.

24.3.2014 1) All NGOs (i.e. CYMA, MUP, MHIP, MZP &amp; MSU) staged a Protest Rally within Aizawl City in protest against Bru voting inside the Tripura Transit Camps during the ensuing Lok Sabha Election-2014. Around 1600 participants/protesters participated and peacefully marched from Millennium Centre to the premises of the office of Chief Electoral Officer (CEO), Khatla. During the rally, the following NGO leaders addressed the public at Millennium Centre, Vanapa Hall and infront of CEO Office :-

 1) Infront of Millennium Centre :

 (i) Lalhmachhuana, President, MZP

 (ii) Pu Saihminga Sailo, President, MUP

 2) Infront of Vanapa Hall :

 (i) Zodinpuia, President, MSU

 (ii) Dr.Thanpuii, Vice President, MHIP

 3) Infront of the office of CEO, Khatla :

 (i) Pu Lalbiakzuala, President, CYMA

 The following slogans were chanted during the rally and procession :-

 (i) We don't want voting of Tuikuk (Bru) voters from outside the state of  Mizoram.

 (ii) Bru Tripura Transit Camps should be removed.

 (iii) We don't want/strongly opposed casting of votes by Bru displaced voters  (who refused to repatriate back Mizoram).

 (iv) Will continue to fight against the decision of ECI on arrangement of  voting by Bru from outside the state of Mizoram.

 The Protest March peacefully ended at 1:10 PM after the protestors burnt a copy of Bru Electoral Roll as a mark of protest against voting by Bru refugees from Mizoram living in Tripura as voters of Mizoram. The following Joint Resolution was also adopted today :-

 (i) Strongly objected/opposed to the decision of the Election Commission of India (ECI) for voting by those Bru refugees (who refused to repatriate despite repeated appeals) living in Tripura Transit Camps as voters of Mizoram in the ensuing Lok Sabha (MP) election. Urged the ECI to review its decision and also threatened to intensify its protest against it.

 (ii) Demand for permanent settlement of adamant Bru refugees (who refused to repatriate despite repeated appeal) in Tripura and their respective Electoral Roll should also be transferred to Tripura.

  (iii) Asked/Requested all the political parties of Mizoram not to conduct  poll campaign within Tripura Transit Camps.

 2) Lalhmachhuana,President, MZP in his address to the Protest Rally at Millennium Centre today stated that Brus should stop spreading baseless allegations against Mizos and he added that the sentiment of the people of Mizoram should be respected by the election officials. He also warned to take more extreme measures for securing the demand of all NGOs of Mizoram.

 3) Zodinpuia, President, MSU also addressed the Protest rally at Vanapa Hall today. He stated that the Mizo people are a peace-loving community and he claimed that some elements from Bru community always spread anti-Mizo attitude resulting in disruption of the peaceful atmosphere of Mizoram. He also accused the ECI of listening only to the distorted plight of Brus and never accepting the demands of the people of Mizoram.

1.4.2014 Today i.e. 1.4.2014 around twelve (12) members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) &amp; Mizo Student Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Aizawl led by Zodinpuia, President, MSU and Michael Lalramsanga, Finance Secretary MZP hang up one black flag in the office building of Directorate of Election, Upper Khatla, Aizawl in protest against casting of votes through postal ballot by Bru voters residing in Tripura Relief Camps.

2.4.2014 Maxi-Cab/Pick-Up Owners Association, Saiha District organized picketing in front of the office of Deputy Commissioner, Saiha today from 6:00 AM and it ended peacefully at 12:30 PM after a joint meeting was held at the office chamber of Deputy Commissioner, Saiha District.

5.4.2014 Around 200 United Democratic Front (UDF) activists took out procession and rally today, i.e. 5.4.2014 within Aizawl City from 11:00 AM and peacefully ended at 1:15 PM. In a brief function held at Millennium Centre, Aizawl, Pu K. Vanlalvena, Secretary, MNF said that the aim of the procession is to demand for stepping down of the ruling Congress government in Mizoram due to the alleged rigging/tampering of EVMs. In his address to the rally held at Israel Point, Pu Lalthlengliana, MNF General Secretary also accused the sitting Chief Minister of Mizoram of assuming the office after rigging the EVMs during the last Mizoram General Election-2013. Pu K. Liantlinga, Vice President, ZNP also delivered a speech at Bazar Bungkawn in which he praised Pu K. Chhawnthuama for his bold and courage statement .
 In a function held infront of Vanapa Hall, Pu Lalmuanpuia Punte and Dr. H. Lallungmuana expressed their strong demand for dissolution of the present Government of Mizoram and appealed the party activists to stand united for removal of the Congress government.
 The following resolutions were unanimously adopted/passed after the end of the procession and rally :-

 1) Demand for immediate resignation of Pu Lal Thanhawla led government in Mizoram due to their involvement in EVM rigging/tampering case.

 2) Youth of UDF activists would fight for removal of the Congress government in Mizoram till the end.

7.4.2014 The Statewide 72 hours total bandh called by NGO Coordination Committee in Mizoram has been evoking an overwhelming support from the public with business establishments, educational institutions remaining closed in most parts of the State. The Bandh has affected the ongoing electoral poll process as polling parties could not leave their places of duty due to road blockade and stiff resistance from the NGOs volunteers in Aizawl, Mamit, Serchhip, Champhai, Kolasib, Lunglei. However, there was no report of any major untoward incident from any part of the State till 1:00 PM today i.e. 7th April 2014. The brief reports from the District headquarters are as follows :-

**(i) Aizawl District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh has been strictly enforced in Aizawl since 5:AM this morning and no polling parties could leave for their places of duty so far. NGOs volunteers organized picketing duties at different locations within Aizawl city blocking vehicular movements and other activities. All commercial establishments, educational institutions are closed and the street look deserted due to the total bandh. All the security force/police officials alongwith Sector magistrates turned up in time however, polling officials, drivers, etc. could not turn up due to strong pressure from the NGOs volunteers .

**(ii) Kolasib District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh also received an overwhelming support from the general masses with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed. All 9 (nine) polling parties are also unable to proceed to their respective places of duty due to the total bandh.

**(iii) Lawngtlai District :**

 The 72 hours total bandh is not organized throughout the District except in Chawngte village where the bandh is organized during 8:00 AM-12:00 noon. Normal life is not affected in Lawngtlai town. 29 polling parties left Lawngtlai this morning at 6:00 AM and due to stiff resistance at Khawmawi, Lunglei District by NGOs volunteers, some of these polling parties were asked to change their route via Rulkual and 50 polling parties also left for their places of duties at 10:00 AM. Around 20 polling parties also left at 1:00 PM today.

**(iv) Champhai District :**

 In the district headquarters at Champhai, the total bandh evoked an overwhelming support from the public with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed within the town. All the 13 polling parties scheduled to proceed to their respective polling stations today could not leave Champhai due to stiff resistance from the NGO volunteers.

**(v) Mamit District :**

 Bandh also received a good support from the public and after the 37 polling parties with escort failed to cross the barricade of local NGO volunteers at Mamit Dinthar locality, all the polling parties returned back to the Office of DEO, Mamit. All commercial establishments, educational institutions remain closed due to the bandh.

**(vi) Lunglei District :**

 The total bandh also received a good response from the public with all vehicles remained off the road and shops, educational institutions remained closed.

 In Lunglei District, polling parties for the following 16 (sixteen) polling stations had already reached their destination last night i.e 6.4.2014 :-

 (i) Kawnpui ‘W’ (ii)Marpara S-II (iii) Marpara S-I (iv) Darngawn (v) Terabonia (vi) Bunghmun (vii) New Sachan (viii) Sesawm (ix) Mauzam (x) Laisawral (xi) Tuikawi (xii) Old Sachan (xiii) Sumasumi (xiv) Ukdasury (xv) Kawizau (xvi) Samuksury.

**(vii) Serchhip District :**

 The total bandh also received an overwhelming support from the public with commercial shops, educational institutions remaining closed within the town. 77 polling parties are scheduled to leave Serchhip town tomorrow i.e. 8.4.2014

**(viii) Saiha District :**

 In the District headquarters at Saiha, the total bandh is not observed today and all the 52 polling parties left for their respective places of polling stations today as per schedule.

15.4.2014 Around 40 youth of UDF who went to Lengpui Airport today to receive Pu K. Chhawnthuama assembled around Sairang Police Station at around 3:30 pm and demanded to meet him personally. The assembled crowd, shouting a slogan -'Long live Pu K. Chhawnthuama!', includes MNYF President, Pu L.Thangmawia, MNYF Vice President, Pu Saihnuna Sailo, ZNP Secretary Pu J. Laldinliana, ZNP Secretary P.C. Vanlalruata and Pu Lalmuanpuia Punte who is also a Secretary of ZNP. The crowd however, dispersed peacefully.
29.4.2014 Today, i.e. 29.4.2014 @ 9:00 AM, around 160 volunteers of Buhchangphai Branch YMA reconstructed 4 (four) Farm huts belonging to 2 (two) victims, namely- (i) R.K. Laldawngliana, Buhchangphai and (ii) R. Kapzuala, Falkland, Aizawl under the protection of 1st IR Bn. All the volunteers dispersed at around 1:10 PM after having a brief function at the place of incident. During the brief function, Buhchangphai Branch YMA leaders stated that their action is only a sign of claiming the territory of Mizoram and further appealed all the YMA members to keep vigil on the Assam-Mizoram boundary issue.

 At this juncture, around 25 volunteers of Buhchangphai Branch YMA managed to sneak into nearby Genda village (Bru village), Assam and threatened them to evacuate the village within 3 days.

 However, @ 4:00 PM, a group of Assam Police numbering 30 to 40 came to the place of incident and dismantled all the reconstructed Farm huts again, taking advantage of the absence of 1st IR Bn. on duty at the site. At the time of this incident, one platoon of 1st IR Bn. proceeded to Buhchangphai site awaiting for the replacement of another platoon.

9.5.2014 Around 40 members of the so called ‘Justice For Mizoram’ gathered today, i.e. 9.5.2014 at the premises of Aizawl District Court in support of Pu K. Chhawnthuama, who attended the Court hearing today. The Court process was however, completed before this group could organize itself properly. Leaders of this same group later met Aizawl District Deputy Commissioner, Pi Juhi Mukherjee, IAS demanding classification order for Pu K. Chhawnthuama citing that he is a prominent citizen. Pi Juhi Mukherjee, Deputy Commissioner explained that the matter would be decided on the basis of Medical Report of Pu K. Chhuanthuama furnished by a Psychiatrist. Discontent with the reply of Deputy Commissioner, Aizawl, the agitated members of ‘Justice For Mizoram’ refused to disperse for a brief period of time. However, at 7:55 PM, the agitated members peacefully dispersed after Deputy Commissioner, Aizawl agreed to fulfill their demand.

19.5.2014 Mizoram Forest Field Staff (MFFS) held a meeting today i.e 19.5.2014 at Tuikhuahtlang, Aizawl under the chairmanship of Pu Lalthantluanga, President, MFFS and was attended by 34 members. The meeting reviewed the incident that took place on 16.5.2014 at Selam area, Champhai District where the angry villagers of Selam burnt one Forest &amp;Environment Department's truck (MZ-01-D-6940) due to misunderstanding between a team of Forest Protection Squad and Selam villagers. The meeting instructed all of its members to assembly tomorrow i.e 20.5.2014 @ 11:00 AM at Aizawl City Park to discuss about their course action on Selam incident.

21.5.2014 today i.e 21.5.2004 @ 7:15 AM a police party numbering 117 personnel (armed and unarmed police) accompanied by two Executive Magistrates i.e. SDO (C) Khawzawl and BDO Ngopa reached Selam village, Champhai District. The ring leaders of Selam village who spearheaded the violence on 16.5.2014 are arrested by Mizoram Police at around 1:30 PM after the ring leaders refused to surrender before the Police.

29.5.2014 1) Activists from Dinthar Veng NGOs assembled today @ 10:30 AM infront of the Office of the Chief Judicial Magistrate Office, Aizawl and observed a silent protest against Malsawmtluanga (21) S/o Ronghinglova, Ramrikawn and C. Lalzuiliana (52) S/o Thanmawia (L), Dungtlang who had allegedly raped and molested three youths from their locality during the early part of this month. The accused were produced before the Chief Judicial Magistrate, Pi Sylvie Z. Ralte today. However no untoward incidents were reported during this event.

 2) Members of Mizoram University Teachers Association, Mizoram University Non-Teaching Employees Association and MZU Students Association gathered at Vaivakawn, Aizawl today, i.e. 29.5.2014 @ 9:00 AM in protest against the delay in repair works of Vaivakawn to Mizoram University approach road. The protesters stopped all vehicles and shouted in unison for works to begin at once. The road block was called off at around 3:00 PM after the delegation of the contractor (i.e. Sunshine Overseas Ltd.) and representatives of Mizoram University students, teachers and non-teaching staff associations signed the following points of agreement in presence of EE, PWD, Aizawl Road North Division and SDC, Aizawl District :-

 (i) that black-topping work of a stretch of road between FCI Godown to MZU Gate will be undertaken from tomorrow or from the first sunny day.

 (ii) that efforts will be taken to complete the work before the coming monsoon period

 (iii) that suspension of black-topping work from FCI Godown to MZU Campus is due to ‘diversion/engagement of labour to other works’ and henceforth, such type of engagement should be avoided.

 (iv) that steps will be taken for resumption of resurfacing work of road  from the junction of Ch.Chhunga High School to Ropaiabawk.

 The protest organized under the initiatives of MIMA has received an overwhelming support from influential Joint NGOs Coordination Committee (CYMA, MHIP, MZP, MSU). Today morning, around 70 members of MIMA and supporters of the protest assembled infront of Millennium Centre, Aizawl and the following persons addressed the gathering :-

 (i) Pu P.C. Laldinthara, President, MIMA

 (ii) Pu Lalbiakzuala, President, CYMA

 (iii) Pu Lalhmachhuana, President, MZP

 (iv) Pu R. Lallawmsanga, General Secretary, MSU

 (v) Dr. Thanpuii, Vice President, MHIP

 The volunteers went to New Market Sobji Bazaar and requested all the vegetable vendors to join the protest and following the request of the volunteers, all the vegetable market within New market area also look deserted.

 The Aizawl Municipal Council authorities, however, said insisting on Tribal Certificate from the applicants, as was being demanded, would be unconstitutional. So far, 534 nos.of Trade License had already been issued and out of which, 39 had been issued to non-tribal under this AMC Licensing Regulations-2012. No untoward incident is reported during the 12-hours protest.

25.8.2014 Today, i.e. 25.8.2014, Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) conducted written examination for recruitment of the post of Staff Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department, Government of Mizoram amidst a strong protest from three Nurses Associations of Mizoram, viz. All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA), All Mizoram Contract Nurses Association (AMCONA) and Non-Government Nurses Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM). Around 330 agitating nurses from the above mentioned three associations assembled near two MPSC Exam Centres, i.e. Pachhunga University College and Central Government Higher Secondary School, Aizawl and after a brief clash with the Police and the agitating nurses, 269 candidates appeared for the written exam. AMNUDA, AMCONA and NOGNAM demanded for cancellation of written examination and instead urged the government to conduct the recruitment through personal interview only. Information has been received that the agitating nurses are still determined to intensify its protest tomorrow i.e. 26.8.2014 second day/final day of written examination for the said post.

26.8.2014 1) Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) continued to conduct written examination for recruitment of the 20 post of Staff Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department, Government of Mizoram amidst a strong protest from three Nurses Associations of Mizoram, viz. All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA), All Mizoram Contract Nurses Association (AMCONA) and Non-Government Nurses Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM).

 A group of agitators numbering around 300-400 from the above mentioned three associations assembled near MPSC Exam Centres, i.e. Pachhunga University College, Aizawl to prevent the aspiring candidates from entering the Exam Centre. However, after a brief clash with the Police and the agitators, altogether, 210 candidates appeared for the written exam under Police protection.

 In the afternoon, at 3:00 PM leaders of AMNUDA, AMCONA and NOGNAM called a Press Conference at Aizawl Press Club and briefed the media on the following main points :-

 (i) Demand conduct of recruitment for the 20 post of Nurses only through personal interview.

 (ii) Trained Nurses are competent enough in theory and practical, therefore, it is felt meaningless to conduct written examination.

 (iii) Demand for proper Service Rules for Nurses in Mizoram.

 (iv) Blame parents of some Nurses in Mizoram for not understanding the concept of Nursing profession.

 (v) Accuse the candidates for being too self-centric and neglecting the dignity of the profession of Nurses.

The leaders of the student association declared that, if their agitation do not yield satisfactory results, they will resort to new methods to meet their demands for appointing teachers for Geography and Sociology subjects at Government Higher Secondary School, Lawngtlai.

28.8.2014 Today, Lai Students Association, General Headquarters, Lawngtlai continued picketing of Government High Schools and Education Offices within Lawngtlai area for the third day in a row.

30.8.2014 On 30.8.2014, All Mizoram Contract Nursing Association (AMCONA), Non-Government Nursing Association of Mizoram (NOGNAM) and All Mizoram Nurses Degree Holder Association (AMNUDA) organized ‘Sit-in Demonstration’ infront of Millennium Centre, Aizawl and around 40 members participated in the said protest. After the demonstration, a joint meeting was held at Nurses’ Conference Hall, Aizawl Civil Hospital under the leadership of Pi Lalhmingmawii, President, AMNUDA and was attended by 50 members. The joint meeting passed the following points of resolution :-

 (i)  Praised the Government for its approval to recruit 50 post of Nurse under Health &amp; Family Welfare Department only through personal interview. At the same time, blamed those applicants who recently appeared for the written exam for the recruitment of 25 post of Nurse despite a strong protest from AMCONA, NOGNAM and AMNUDA.

 (ii) Urged the Government and public to respect the dignity of nursing profession and asserted that, nursing profession is one form of profession under Medical Science and should not be compared with other non-medical profession.

 (iii) Urged the Government to conduct separate written exam for its  members who could not enter the MPSC Exam Centre due to closure of  the gate by Police.

3.9.2014 1) Picketing against AMC staff entered its third day and around 150 members from NGOs took part in the picketing. At 12:00 Noon today, a meeting was convened at Thuampui YMA Committee Room and the meeting was presided over by Pu Lalbiakzuala, President CYMA and 15 members were present in the meeting. The meeting decided to continue with the picketing as there has been no efforts made by the AMC staff to fulfill their demands and if no positive feedback as desired by the NGO Coordination Committee is received within this week, the NGO Coordination Committee, from next week, will resort to more severe measures to meet their demands.

 2) Lai Students Association (LSA) called off their agitation today, i.e. 3.9.2014 at 5:00 PM after they were convinced by the steps adopted by the Government.

4.9.2014 1) Today, i.e. 4.9.2014 @ 3:10 PM, a joint meeting between Political Party Coordination Committee comprising of leaders from MNF, ZNP and MPC and NGO Coordination Committee was convened at Thuampui YMA Committee Room and the picketing was called off indefinitely from today after the Political Party Coordination Committee assured the NGO Coordination Committee that they will take up the on-going issue to the Government. The meeting came out with the following agreements :-

 (i) The Political Party Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) will make efforts to materialize the demands of the NGO Coordination Committee regarding the AMC Licensing Regulations Act-2012 latest by 30th September 2014

 (ii) The Political Party Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) will ensure that while the AMC is in the process of amending the Licensing Regulations, the AMC will not make efforts to introduce the Licensing Regulation, 2012.

 (iii) The Joint Coordination Committee (MNF, ZNP and MPC) also  stated that they will take necessary steps in amending the alleged  loopholes found in proposed Property Tax.

25.9.2014 Thousands of students took out a protest rally today, i.e. 25.9.2014 within Aizawl City in demand of annulment of the inclusion of Chakma students in Category-I of the State Technical Entrance Examination (STEE). The agitating students were divided into two groups and marched towards office of the Technical Wing of Higher &amp; Technical Education Deaprtment, Chaltlang causing disruption of traffic movement within Aizawl City. All roads leading to Chaltlang area were blocked by the agitating students. They were, however, unable to cross the Police cordon at two locations, i.e. at Chaltlang Dawrkawn and near the office of Technical Wing, H&amp;TE Department. All the agitating students peacefully dispersed at around 2:20 PM after the leaders of MZP General Headquarters reached an agreement with the Government of Mizoram.

 Similarly, in some of the District Headquarters like Lunglei, Mamit, Kolasib, Champhai and Serchhip, the concerned MZP Sub-Headquarters have also organized a peaceful protest/agitation.

 In Champhai, around 700 students participated in a protest rally and the rally ended peacefully at 1:25 PM after passing resolutions like cancellation of seat allotment to Chakma students under STEE, demand of immediate release of arrested student leaders, demand of resignation of Dr. B.D. Chakma from the Cabinet, etc.

 In Mamit, around 80 students staged a peaceful sit-in demonstration in front of the Office of the Deputy Commissioner (DC), Mamit District. It was called off at 1:30 PM.

 In Lunglei, around 300 students have also participated in a protest rally and the rally ended peacefully at around 2:30 PM after the student leaders addressed the rally.

 In Kolasib, around 300 students organised a peaceful sit-in demonstration infront of the Office of the Deputy Commissioner, Kolasib and dispersed peacefully at 1:00 PM after passing resolutions like demand of immediate release of arrested student leaders, asked fifteen Chakma students to discontinue their training at DIET, Kolasib, etc.

 Today, at around 10:30 AM, around 300 students staged a sit-in demonstration infront of Office of the Deputy Commissioner, Serchhip and the students peacefully dispersed at 11:00 AM after student leaders read out the objectives of their demonstration.

(Pi Vanlalhruaii has been accused of involving in illicit liquor business by the NGOs) Although Pi Vanlalhruai took this matter to the court, and the court issued a stay-order for her, she left Zuangtui areas under heavy pressure from the NGOs.
