****2015****

22.1.2015 Today, i.e. 22.1.2015, around 1100 party activists/workers of MNF, the main opposition party of Mizoram took out a procession christened as ‘Mipui Thlavang Hauhna Kawngzawh’ (procession to safeguard the interest of the people) within Aizawl City. The participants in the protest rally held different placards which read, ‘We don't want selling of liquor in Mizoram,’ ‘We will continue to safeguard the interest of the people of Mizoram,’ ‘We are fed up with government under family-dynasty.’ etc. The protest rally peacefully ended at around 2:15 PM after which sitting MNF MLA’s and party leaders submitted a Memorandum to Hon’ble Governor of Mizoram highlighting the following points for justifying their protest rally :-

 (i) Increase of price of rice

 (ii) Motor Vehicle Tax

 (iii) Blood unit price

 (iv) Upward revision of various taxes and utility charges

 (v) Increase of land revenue and fees, etc

 (vi) MLPC Act

 In Saiha, around 100-120 MNF party workers attended the protest rally and the procession commenced at 10:30 AM from Vety junction and peacefully ended @ 12:15 PM at Bazar junction. During the procession, the participants chanted the following slogans:

 (i) We protest hike in price of Rice to Rs.15 per Kg

 (ii)  We protest increase in water and electric tariff.

 (iii) We protest increase in land revenue tax and fees

 (iv) We condemned the government that lifted liquor prohibition

 In Kolasib town, Public meeting was held at Kolasib Diakkawn under the aegis of Kolasib Block MNF Committee and passed the following resolutions :-

 (i) Urge the Congress Government led by Pu Lal Thanhawla to stop indulging in expensive and luxury affairs.

 (ii) Demand for immediate roll back of hike in price of rice.

 (iii)  Demand for immediate roll back of hike in traffic of water and electric charges.

 (iv)  Strongly condemned the decision of the Congress Government to lift Liquor Prohibition and demand for immediate repeal of MLPC Act.

 (v) Demand for immediate repair of dilapidated conditions of road, especially linking Kolasib to Kawnpui and Bairabi to Rengtekawn before the onset of monsoon.

 (vi) Urge the Congress Government to take immediate measures to stop harassment of Mizo land owners along Assam-Mizoram border area.

 In Lunglei town, around 300 MNF party activists participated in the procession and the protest rally peacefully concluded at around 2:00 PM.

 In Champhai, around 100 MNF party activists peacefully staged a protest rally within Champhai town.

 In Mamit, around 50 MNF party workers pasted posters in different locations within Mamit town and they peacefully dispersed at around 2:15 PM.

 In Serchhip, around 130 MNF activists participated in the procession which started from AOC Veng to Bazar Veng. Speeches were delivered by Pu C. Lalramzauva, Adviser, MNF General Headquarters and Pu H. Rammawi, Ex-Minister.

 In Lawngtlai, the procession started from Chawngte Peng (L-4) to Areopagi (Bazar). Around 130 activists took part in the procession. Pu Lalduhsaka, MDC and Pu Lalramliana Colney, President, MNF, Lawngtlai delivered speeches.

 In Chawngte 'C', around 60 activists of MNF took part in the procession.

 In Tlabung, around 200 persons took part in the procession which commenced from Zodin Veng to Bazar Veng. Pu P. Thanhawla, Pu P.R. Chakma and Pu Vanlalmawia delivered speeches.

25.2.2015 The State-wide Total Bandh called by MNF party in protest against Congress Government's decision to hike the price of rice, increase in tax, hike in electricity bill, water bill and charging of blood processing fee, etc evoked a good response in different parts of Mizoram except within Chakma Autonomous District Council area where polling of Village Council Elections was held today, i.e. 25.2.2015.

 In the State capital, Aizawl, the bandh passed off peacefully at 3:30 PM. All Government, party and private offices, shops, markets and other educational institutions were closed during the bandh. The streets of Aizawl were left deserted except some vehicles; most of security forces, hospital staffs and private vehicles carrying patients (on emergency) were seen on the roads. Police deployment was made in all the important picket points/junctions to prevent untoward incidents.

 In Aizawl, Pu Tawnluia, MNF Sr. Vice President &amp; Chairman, Action Committee, today @ 3:00 PM called a Press Conference at Mizo Hnam Run during which he thanked the people of Mizoram for their support for the state-wide bandh. He clarified that MNF party was not against/protest in imposing of tax per se but what the MNF party protesting was massive hike in taxes, etc. He further said that the decision to impose a steep hike in taxes on land revenue, price of essential commodities, etc brought an enormous problems and burdens to common people and demanded the Government of Mizoram to immediately rollback such decision.

 In a statement, he said that on 22.1.2015, MNF Youth Wing had staged mass rally/procession in Mizoram in protest against the decision of Congress Government to hike rice price, etc. He also mentioned that Memorandum of grievance was also submitted to the Governor against the ruling Congress. He added that the purpose of the bandh is to safeguard the interest of the people of Mizoram. He also stongly accused Congress Government of failing in financial management and austerity measures. Commenting on the recent tragedy over the death of patients admitted in Kolasib Hospital and TB Hospital, Falkland he blamed the Health Minister of failing to take responsibility. He also asked the Government to take measures for prevention of incident of abduction especially on the western side of Mizoram.

 In Sakawrdai, Darlawn and Saitual of Aizawl District, the bandh passed off peacefully at around 1:00 PM .

 In Mamit District, the total bandh had been observed in major towns and villages such as Mamit, West Phaileng, Kawrthah, Kanhmun, Phuldungsei, Rengdil, Luimawi and Saikhawthlir. In Zawlnuam, MNF volunteers had displayed posters, etc within the town instead of observing total bandh. The bandh was peacefully called off at Kanhmun village @ 12:30 PM and in Kawrthah, the bandh passed off peacefully @ around 1:00 PM. All the remaining towns and villages within Mamit District have peacefully called off the total bandh at 2:00 PM.

 In Saiha District, the shutdown had been observed in Saiha and Tuipang village. All offices, shops, banks, business establishments and schools were closed during the bandh. The bandh was called off @ 3:45 PM.

 In Kolasib District, the total bandh received a good support in Kolasib, Bilkhawthlir, Bairabi, Vairengte, Buhchangphai and Kawnpui throwing normal life out of gear. At Bairabi, the bandh passed off peacefully @ around 1:00 PM. The total bandh within the entire Kolasib District was called off at 3:30 PM.

 In Vairengte, a team of officials from Assam led by Pi Kimi Thado, ACS with Dholai Police, CRPF came to the duty/picket point of MNF volunteers at Auto stand located along NH 54 in between Vairengte, Mizoram and Lailapur, Assam and raised their concern over the activities of MNF volunteers. However, after clarification was made, no untoward incident was reported and both the parties dispersed peacefully at 3:30 PM.

 In Champhai District, the total bandh had also evoked a good response from the public and it was peacefully called off at 2:30 PM.

 In Serchhip District, normal life also got paralysed due to the total bandh and it was peacefully called off at 3:10 PM.

 In Lunglei District, the total bandh received a good support from the public and was called off peacefully at 3:40 PM.

 However, in Lawngtlai District, except within CADC area, due to the indefinite total bandh launched by Young Lai Association (YLA) since yesterday, i.e. 24.2.2015, the bandh is still enforced while writing this report. YLA has launched indefinite total bandh within Lai Autonomous District Council area in demand of better roads, posting of EE in P&amp;E Department, etc. Information has been received that the YLA Central Executive decided to dissolve YLA Diltlang branch for their objection to the demand of CYLA.

Hqrs. and Aizawl City College Joint Students Union(ACCJSU). One group of students from northern side of Aizawl started the procession from Chanmari junction and proceeded towards Vanapa Hall.  2. Payment of Rs.538.39 lakhs of 2014-15 Post Matric Tribal Scholarship by the Government before 10th March, 2015.

25.3.2015 A team of MZP led by Lalhmachhuana, President and L. Ramdinliana, General Secretary, Mizo Zirlai Pawl General Headquarters conducted verification drive against non-locals running business in the name of local residents (Mizos) and without legal permits within Khatla Local Council area, Aizawl today, i.e.24.3.2015 from 2:00 pm. The MZP team instructed owners of 11 (eleven) shops to shut down their shops as they claimed that they were running business without having trade licences. The MZP also expressed their intention to continue cracking down of illegal business run by non-locals in Mizoram.

Around 40 members gathered carrying banners and posters demanding impartial treatment towards the appointment of Governor for the State of Mizoram, besides chanting slogans against the Central Government’s way of handling the post of Governor for Mizoram. No untoward incident took place during the protest and the swearing-in ceremony of the Governor of Mizoram was concluded smoothly.

8.4.2015 1) Around 250 student activists took out a procession within Lunglei town today, i.e. 8.4.2015 in protest against shifting of school timing in Mizoram. The protest march was jointly organized by Mizo Students' Union, Regional Headquarters, Lunglei; Chawngte Area Students' Union; Pang Zirlai Pawl, Lunglei Branch and Pawngzawl Students' Union, Lunglei. The procession commenced from Chanmari, Lunglei at 11:30 AM and marched towards Venglai, Lunglei where they held a rally in front of Mizofed office at Venglai. The procession peacefully ended at 1:30 PM after they passed a resolution demanding the Government to roll back its decision on shifting of school timing in Mizoram.

 Similarly, a peaceful procession was also organized within Hnahthial town today under the aegis of Mizo Students' Union Sub-Headquarters, Hnahthial and around 300 student activists participated in the procession and the march peacefully ended at 11:30 AM.

 2) In a show of their protest against frequent transfer and posting of Governor of Mizoram, Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) General Headquarters, Aizawl still stood firm on their stand to stage a 'Silent Protest' in front of Raj Bhawan Main Gate during the visit of President of India on 9.4.2015 in which the students will wear black shawls and put up placards/posters. It is anticipated that around 40 to 50 MZP activists would participate in the protest.

9.4.2015 1) In a show of their protest against frequent transfer and sacking of Governors in Mizoram, today i.e. 9.4.2015, MZP General Headquarters, Aizawl has staged a 'Silent protest' along the roadside from the main gate of Mizoram State Assembly House, Treasury Square to Raj Bhavan Northern Gate while the Hon'ble President of India arrives in Aizawl for his two day visit to the state of Mizoram.  2) Around 30 activists of MSU General Headquarters, Aizawl assembled in front of Mizoram Public Service Commission (MPSC) Office today to picket against Pu Andrew Lalherliana, Chairman, MPSC. However, as the Chairman, MPSC did not attend the Office today, the MSU activists dispersed peacefully at 10:30 AM.

10.4.2015 Today, i.e. 10.4.2015, around 5000 people took out a procession within Chawngte town, Lawngtlai District in protest against the recent Amendment of the Mizoram (Selection of Candidates for Higher &amp; Technical Courses) Rules, 1999 made by the Government of Mizoram. The procession was organized by all political parties and NGOs within Chakma Autonomous District Council (CADC) area under the aegis of Chakma National Council of India (CNCI), Mizoram. During the procession a copy of the said amendment rules was also burnt. In this regard, a memorandum was submitted to Hon'ble Chief Minister of Mizoram through SDO(C) Chawngte, highlighting the following points :-

 (i) That, the Chakmas and Brus in Mizoram are the most backward in almost all socio-economic indicators from that of Zo-ethnic people of the state.

 (ii) That, the Chakmas and Brus are as indigenous as that of Zo-ethnic people of Mizoram.

 (iii) That, the Chakmas and Brus are disadvantage groups in all respect vis-à-vis the Zo-ethnic people of the state.

 The processionists carried placards which read the following messages :-

 (i) No racism in the land of democracy.

 (ii) Down with racist rule.

 (iii) We demand reservation of seats in Technical Courses for the Chakmas in Mizoram.

 (iv) Mizoram Government cannot question racism in Delhi while racism is rampant in the state.

Lalrinhlua, President, MSU assembled near MPSC Office to organize picketing against the MPSC Chairman. However, the agitating MSU activists could not cross the Police barricade and Pu Andrew Lalherliana ,Chairman, MPSC could attend the office. 4.8.2015 Today, i.e. 4.8.2015 @ 6:30 AM, a mob of around 150-200 people attacked Chawngte/ Kamalanagar Police Station, Lawngtlai District after 9 (nine) leaders of Joint Chakma NGOs have been arrested this morning (4:30 AM to 5:30 AM) at Chawngte Police Station on the ground of preventive measures for the 'Total Bandh' called by Joint Chakma NGOs (CYCA, MCSU &amp; CMS) w.e.f. 6:00 AM today. The angry mob pelted stones and damaged some of the properties of Chawngte Police Station like window panes, Solar plates, etc and to disperse the irate mob, the Police resorted to lathi charge and eventually opened fire (around 8 rounds) as ordered by Executive Magistrate, Pu Lallawmawma. Unfortunately, one Class-XI student identified as Agosh Chakma (16 yrs) S/o Nomoni Chakma, Kalamanagar Higher Secondary School (HSS) succumbed to injury suspected to have been caused by a deflected bullet. Three Policemen also sustained minor injuries. In the ensuing violence, the angry mob ransacked and damaged several properties belonging to the CADC leaders, including residential buildings and vehicles within Chawngte town. The arrested 9 (nine) leaders of Joint Chakma NGOs were released at 10:15 AM and the violent mob also dispersed at around 12:00 noon.

 2) Last night i.e 13.10.2015 at around 7:00 PM an irate group of local resident of Bawngkawn, Aizawl under the aegis of Bawngkawn Local Council pelted stones at the newly constructed Baptist Church of Mizoram (BCM) (Assam Type building) in Brigade area, Bawngkawn, damaging 46 nos. of window glass, 30 nos. of tiles sheet and 1 no. of door of the Church building (value of around Rs. 15,170 approx). 27.10.2015 Some local youths of Laisawral village picked up a quarrel with Chakma youths of Marpara South Village on 25.10.2015 over love affairs. Laisawral youths were reportedly beaten up by Chakma youths. Accordingly local leaders of Laisawral went to Marpara South yesterday i.e. 26.10.2015 to inquire the matter with a view to find amicable solution. However, local youths (Chakma) of Marpara pelted stones against Laisawral local leaders.

 Infuriated with the action of Chakma youths, local youths of Laisawral numbering about 50 (fifty) went to Marpara South early this morning i.e. 27.10.2015 with vengeful mindset. Meanwhile, Police party headed by Addl. SP, Mamit District and SDPO West Phaileng assisted by around 50 Police personnel had already stationed at early this morning at Marpara to take stock of the situation. It was reported that an agreement had reached between the two parties although there were reports of altercation at 2/3 places at Marpara. Situation is reportedly under control.

28.10.2015 Information has been received that today, i.e. 28.10.2015, a peaceful rally has been organised at Marpara South @ 12:00 Noon. It was attended by about 100 persons and the rally ended peacefully at 2:30 PM after adopting the following resolutions :-

 (i) Immediate arrest of the persons who were involved in the assault of innocent Mizo youths.

 (ii) No innocent Mizos should be assaulted in future.

 (iii) Steps may be taken towards checking of illegal foreigners residing in Mizoram.

 (iv) Whenever any kind of misunderstanding occur in future, the matter should be immediately brought to the notice of concerned local/state authority.
9.11.2015 Today @7:00am, around 400 activists of NGO co-ordination committee(YMA, MZP, MSU, MHIP&amp;MUP) organized picketing against a team of State Election officials, Mizoram at Mamit in protest against Election Commission of India(ECI)’s instruction to conduct Special Summary Revision of Electoral Roll of Bru refugees living in the 6 relief camps of Tripura. The picketing duty NGO activists has been deployed within Mamit under the supervision of a team of NGO Co-ordination committee who came to Mamit from Aizawl. After DC, Mamit District failed to persuade the NGO activists, the security personnel made an attempt to disperse the activists. However, as the activists outnumbered the security force, the team of State Election officials could not proceed to Tripura today as per schedule. The NGO activists also peacefully dispersed at around 4:00pm. Meanwhile, a team of NGO co-ordination committee, Aizawl comprising of 19 members returned to Aizawl today.

As many as 100 (one hundred) Police personnel were also deployed at picketing site.

Commissioner (DC), Mamit District appealed and persuaded volunteers of All NGO &amp; All Political Party Coordination Committee, Mamit to stop their picketing duty/protest. However, leaders of All NGO &amp; All Political Party Coordination Committee, Mamit reiterated their commitment to stage protest until their demands are met.

13.1.2016 A new Liquor Shop at Bawngkawn Lunglei Road owned by Pi Ramnghaki, D/o Pu Hrangchuanga of Bawngkawn was ransacked by a mob of Bawngkawn locality numbering around 500 (five hundred) last night, i.e. 13.1.2015 @ 12:30 AM by overpowering the Police on duty at the spot. The residents of Bawngkawn locality were asked to gather at Bawngkawn Traffic point last night i.e. 12.1.2015 @ 9:30 PM through Public Information system and at around 11:00 PM, the irate mob proceeded towards the Liquor Shop. Due to the tussle between the irate mob and the Police, some Policemen sustained minor injuries. The proprietor of the Liquor Shop stated that liquor worth around Rs. 5 lakhs were destroyed by the irate mob.

18.1.2016 1) Today, i.e. 18.1.2016 @ 9:00 AM, around 80 members of Aizawl City College Joint Students Union (ACCJSU), Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Differently Abled Society (DAS), Physically Challenged Society (PCS) and Zoram Entu Pawl (ZEP) under the aegis of Mizo Student Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Aizawl assembled infront of the office of Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities (PwD), Chaltlang, Aizawl in protest against extention of the re-employment period of Pi B. Sairengpuii, MSS (Rtd.) as Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities under Government of Mizoram. They carried placards and chanted slogans demanding resignation of Pi B. Sairengpuii from the post of Commissioner of Persons with Disabilities. They peacefully dispersed at around 11:30 AM after they learnt that Pi B. Sairengpuii would not attend the office for the day. Leaders of ACCJSU and MBS will hold a Joint Meeting this evening at MSU office under the aegis of MSU General Headquarters and the meeting is likely to discuss about their roadmap for agitation against Pi B. Sairengpuii, etc.

 2) Last night, i.e. 17.1.2016 at around 10:30 PM, about 70 residents of Vairengte assembled infront of Vairengte Police Station after an incident of altercation between three civilians and Armymen took place on the same night @ 8:30 PM within the area of CIJW School, Vairengte. It is reported that three civilians (residents of Vairengte) namely, (i) C. Lalrinpuia (31 yrs) S/o Lalzarmawia, (ii) Zosangpuia (19 yrs) S/o Lalthlengliana and (iii) Lalenkawla (18 yrs) S/o Lalhmingmawia had altercation with an Armyman namely, Sanjay Kumar (30 yrs) S/o Surendra Kumar of CIJW School over road traffic, etc due to which one civilian C. Lalrinpuia (31 yrs) S/o Lalzarmawia was beaten by Armymen and he sustained injuries (as the other two civilians fled from the spot). However, due to timely intervention of Vairengte Police, leaders of Vairengte NGOs and Senior Army Officers of CIJW School, Vairengte, the residents of Vairengte who assembled infront of Vairengte PS peacefully dispersed at 4:00 AM this morning, i.e. 18.1.2016. CIJW School, Vairengte agreed to meet all the medical expenditure incurred by the injured person.

21.1.2016 Today i.e. 21.1.2016 around 1300 strong students took out a possession within Aizawl City under the aegis of Mizo Students Union (MSU) General Headquarters, Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) in protest against extension of the re-employment period of Pi B.Sairengpuii as Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities (PwD) under Government of Mizoram. The students marched from Zarkawt Junction to the office of the Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities, Chaltlang, Aizawl. The demonstrators further staged a 'Sit-in demonstration' infront of the office of Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities at Chaltlang, Aizawl demanding removal of Pi B.Sairengpuii before 5:00 PM today. At around 4:00 PM, the agitating students tried to break Police Barrickade infront of the office of Commissioner, (PwD) and the Police were compelled to resort to Lathi charge and Tear Gas as the agitating students started attacking the Police personnel by pelting stone etc. Finally, at around 5:00 PM, all the agitating students withdrawn from the spot of demonstration i.e. infront of Office of Commissioner, PwD, Chaltlang and march towards Vanapa Hall, Aizawl and they dispersed from Vanapa Hall premises at 6:20 PM. During the clash between the two sides, 3(three) students and 8 (eight) Police personnel reportedly sustained minor injuries. In this regard, Bawngkawn PS Case No 26/16 Dt. 21.1.2016 u/s 143/145/147/149/152/ 353/427 IPC has been registered.

  Information has been received that leaders of Mizo Students Union (MSU), Mizoram Blind Society (MBS), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) decided to intensify their agitation tomorrow i.e. 22.1.2016 and decided to assemble infront of Vanapa Hall at 9:00 AM. Further, leaders of the students expressed their readiness to discuss about their demand with any representative of the Government of Mizoram and at the sametime expressed their strong determination to continue the agitation till their demand is fulfilled by the Government. The meeting of the leaders of MSU, MBS and ACCJSU is being held at MSU Office from 6:30 PM and the meeting is underway while writing this report.

22.1.2016 Today, i.e. 22.1.2016 @ 9:00 AM, more than 2000 (two thousand) students under the aegis of Mizo Students’ Union (MSU), Aizawl City College Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) and Mizoram Blind Society (MBS) gathered infront of Vanapa Hall, Aizawl in continuation of their protest against extension of re-employment period of Pi B. Sairengpuii as Commissioner, Persons with Disabilities (PwD) under Government of Mizoram. The demonstrators blocked the main road at Vanapa Hall at around 10:00 AM. At the same time, Mizoram Police have made elaborate security arrangement within Aizawl City to prevent any untoward incident due to the agitation. At the same time, P.C. Lalrinhlua, President, MSU and Lalruatpuia, President, ACCJSU met Pu P.C. Lalthanliana, Hon'ble Minister, i/c Social Welfare Department in his bungalow and received the revocation order of Pi B. Sairengpuii, MSS (Rtd) (vide Memo No.B.13016/35/2010-SWD, Dt.22.1.2016) and the agitation was called off at around 11:30 AM. The students also dispersed peacefully after passing the following resolutions :-

 (i) Urged the Government of Mizoram to immediately appoint new Commissioner, PwD having special knowledge or practical experience in respect of matters relating to rehabilitation of persons with disabilities

 (ii) Urged the Government of Mizoram to immediately frame recruitment rule for the post of Commissioner, PwD under Government of Mizoram.

 (iii) Demanded payment of compensation to the injured students (who sustained injuries during the clash with Police force).

 (ii) Demanded ex-gratia payment to the family of HS.Lalmuankima (L)

 (iii)  Demanded setting up of Police Beat Post within Ramthar Village Council area.

 It may be mentioned that all the three accused persons namely (i) Lalduhawma (30 yrs) S/o Suaktlaia, Lunglawn, Lunglei (ii)C.Lalmuanzuala (17yrs) S/o C.Lalhmachhuana, Lunglawn,Lunglei (iii) Lalruatfela (17yrs) S/o Lalbiaksanga, Lunglawn, Lunglei were already arrested by Lunglei Police and a criminal case vide Lunglei PS Case No.8/2016 dt.16.1.2016 u/s 325/34 IPC has already been registered.

Lalsangzuala on his alleged corrupt practices, indulgence in alcohol, lack of discipline in school, poor quality of mess, inadequate budget of their school, etc. The students chanted on a slogan demanding the removal of their Principal and Pi Zorampari, Teacher Cum Hostel Warden. 29.2.2016 1) Today, i.e. 29.2.2016, around 1000-1500 people took out procession rally within Aizawl City under the aegis of Zoram Taxi Owner's Association (ZTOA) and Zoram Taxi Drivers Association (ZTDA) in protest against the decision of the Government to impose rotational plying of Taxis in Aizawl, hike in vehicle tax, etc in Mizoram. The protesters marched from Vanapa Hall to Chanmari Junction and leaders of ZTOA, ZTDA namely Pu R. Pahlira, President, ZTOA, Pu Zoramthanga, Vice President, ZTDA and Pu Laldawngliana, President, ZTDA adressed the rally.  2) In continuation of their demands for appointment of Science Teacher at Government High School, Thingsai and Headmaster at Government Saikuti Middle School, Joint NGO Coordination Committee, Thingsai continued their Hunger Strike today, i.e. 29.2.2016 for the 9thconsecutive days at YMA Run, Thingsai. 1.3.2016 Today, i.e. 1.3.2016, commercial vehicles like City Buses, Taxis, Trucks, Pickups, Maxicabs stayed off the roads across the state of Mizoram due to strike called by Commercial Vehicle Joint Action Committee (CVJAC) in protest against the Government's decision to hike Vehicle Tax, order for rotational plying of taxis, cancellation of all Mizoram Plying Permit, cancellation of replacement of old vehicles, impose of compulsory payment of life-time (15 years) tax on vehicle. As many as 26 (twenty six) Government buses including Mizoram State Transport buses were pressed into service within Aizawl city today. Hundreds of commercial vehicles (Trucks, Maxicabs) were also stranded on the National Highway (NH-54) at Rengtekawn, etc which is one of the lifeline of Mizoram.

 The leaders of Commercial Vehicle Joint Action Committee (CVJAC) held a meeting today @ 1:00 PM at the office of Mizoram Tipper Drivers &amp; Owners Association, Bawngkawn. Pu Jeffry L. Fanai, General Secretary, CVJAC chaired the meeting and was attended by 35 members. The meeting decided to intensify its agitation tomorrow, i.e. 2.3.2016 and also threatened to boycott the KTP General Conference to be held at Champhai during 3rd - 6th March, 2016 unless positive response is received from the Government.

 However, Pu Lalmalsawma, IAS, Chief Secretary has immediately convened a joint meeting with the leaders of CVJAC in his office chamber today @ 5:00 PM. The joint meeting decided to constitute a team of officials (study group) to study the grievances and demands of the CVJAC and as a result of which leaders of CVJAC agreed to call off their strike. Further, taxi services will resume from tomorrow, i.e. 2.3.2016 within Aizawl city till further order. The joint meeting was attended by Addl. Secretary (Home); DC, Aizawl; SP, Aizawl; SP, Traffic; Director, Transport and seven (7) members of CVJAC led by Jeffry L. Fanai, General Secretary, CVJAC.

14.3.2016 Mizoram Auto Rickshaw Owners Association (MAROA) General Headquarters, Lunglei organised a procession/rally today, i.e.14.3.2016 @ 11:45 AM from AOC, Lunglei to Venglai Traffic Point in protest against the Government's decision to hike Vehicle Tax (6%) and onetime payment of Life-Time Road Tax (15 years) on vehicles. Pu Saithuama, President, MAROA delivered a speech and a copy of the Government order on Vehicle Tax (6%) and onetime payment of Life-Time Road Tax (15 years) were burnt at 12:50 PM. About 180 (one hundred eighty) owners/drivers of Auto Rickshaw have participated in the procession and they expressed their commitment to continue their protest till the Government rolls back the order.

4.4.2016 Today i.e.4.4.2016 @9:00 AM around 10 (ten) activists of MZP Sub Headquarters, Tlabung staged picketing of Civil Hospital, Tlabung staff in demand of posting of sufficient Staff Nurses and X-Ray Technician at the said Hospital. MZP Activists, however had called off their picketing after the Chief Medical Officer (CMO) assured them that he will take initiative for the fulfilment of their demand. It was also learnt that leaders of MZP Sub Headquarters, Tlabung intended to pursue this matter.

5.4.2016 1) About 34 (thirty four) Staff of Goodwill Foundation and Open Doors (2 NGO's) jointly organised picketing against staff of Aizawl District Project Management Unit, North East Rural Livelihood Project (NERLP), at Thuampui, Aizawl today i.e.5.4. 2016 @8:30 AM in protest against discontinuation of their contract agreement for facilitating the services of Project Facilitation Team (PFT) under NERLP within Aizawl District. The agitating staff of Goodwill Foundation and Open Doors also displayed placards demanding the removal of Pu Reuben Ranglong, Project Manager of Aizawl District Project Management Unit, North East Rural Livelihood Project (NERLP).

 At 2:00 PM Pu Christopher Lun, Chief Functionary, Goodwill Foundation and Pi Lalrokimi Pautu, Chief Functionary Open Doors jointly convened a Press Conference at Aizawl Press Club. They conveyed the Media Persons about their agitations and their demands for the removal of Pu Reuben Ranglong.

About 2500 students from Government Hrangbana College, Government Aizawl North College, Government Aizawl West College, Pachhunga University College, Government Aizawl College, T.Romana College and Women Polytechnic participated at the procession whereas Government Johnson College, Zirtiri Residential Science College, Government J. Thankima College, Mizoram University and Aizawl Law College did not participate.

 The following resolutions were passed during the procession :-

 i) Slammed the Government over sending of Mizo students to an unverified Institution outside the State and urged the Government to take care of them.

 ii) Insisted the Political Executives of Mizoram to seek an apology to the students of NIAS for making adverse remarks on them.

 iii) Urged the Government to take measures for facilitating the students to appear their exam and take initiative against issuance of fake certificates to the students.

 iv) Demanded the Government to provide compensation to the students of  NIAS over the pecuniary loss incurred by them at NIAS. They also  expressed their commitment to continue their protest if the Government do  not give compensation to the students immediately.

17.8.2017 Today, i.e. 17.8.2017, Chakma National Council of India (CNCI), Mizoram State Committee and Chakma NGOs, Kamalanagar, Chawngte organised 'Chakma Black Day' by gathering at Kamalanagar-II (Rexi Square) in condemnation of the Radcliffe Award of Bengal Boundary Commission which awarded Chittagong Hill Tracts unjustly to Pakistan during partition of Indian Sub-Continent in 1947. As many as 200 (two hundred) people participated at the 'Chakma Black Day' and they burnt the copy of the Radcliffe Award of Bengal Boundary Commission. Shri Rasik Mohan Chakma, President, CNCI, Mizoram; Shri Alak Bikash Chakma, Vice President, CNCI, Mizoram and Shri Amarsmriti Chakma, Vice President, CNCI, Mizoram delivered speeches during the function in which they demanded the intervention of Government of Great Britain in resolving the crisis of Chakmas in Bangladesh. They also urged the International Chakma community to start observing the Chakma Black Day. The gathering was peacefully called off @ 1:30 p.m.

Lalmalsawma, President and Lalthanzuala, Gen. Secy. entered Chakma House at Hunthar Veng, Aizawl today, i.e. 28.9.2017 @ 2:30 p.m and damaged 2 (two) Computer Sets, 1 (one) Computer Printer and 1 (one) Steel Almirah. They also threatened all Chakmas lodging at Chakma House excluding sick persons to leave Chakma House before 7:00 p.m (tonight).

29.9.2017 1) Today, i.e. 29.9.2017 @ 10:00 a.m, MSU General Headquarters and Aizawl City Colleges Joint Students' Union (ACCJSU) organised procession from Vanapa Hall and they marched towards Chakma House, Hunthar Veng, Aizawl. The procession was organised in protest against the alleged assault of leaders of MSU Sub-Headquarters, Chawngte by some Chakma students at Chawngte yesterday, i.e. 28.9.2017 and as many as 2000 (two thousand) students participated at the procession. Mizoram Police formed a barricade at Vaivakawn-Hunthar junction and they obstructed students from proceeding toward Chakma House. After a successful persuasion and negotiation was made by DC, Aizawl; DIG(NR) and SP, Aizawl, selected leaders of MSU, ACCJSU and media persons numbering about 15 (fifteen) members entered Chakma House under the escort of Mizoram Police. They were contented as they found only 2 (two) sick Chakmas staying at Chakma House. A function was held at Vaivakawn-Hunthar junction in which R.B. Lalmalsawma, President, MSU delivered a speech and they called-off the procession @ 1:35 p.m

 2) Consequence upon the alleged assault of MSU leaders at Chawngte yesterday, i.e. 28.9.2017, MSU Regional Headquarters, Lunglei prohibited Chakma community living in Lunglei from moving out of their house today, i.e. 29.9.2017 from 6:00 a.m to 6:00 p.m. In this regard, about 10 (ten) activists of MSU Regional Headquarters, Lunglei performed duties. No untoward incident is reported due to such imposition of restriction on the movement of Chakmas within Lunglei areas.

 MSU Regional Headquarters, Lunglei also issued a Press Release in this regard today wherein they urged the people of Lunglei not to rent out their houses to Chakma community.

Members of FMGE&amp;W (except from emergency services like Police, Hospital, Jail, PHE, etc.) turned up for their respective offices/work places wearing black badges and refused to discharge their duties/perform works.

The meeting also decided to hold another meeting today, 25.1.2018 @ 8:00 p.m. at YMA Conference Hall, Sihphir.

3.2.2018 Around 200 (two hundred) students from Govt. J. Thankima College organised a demonstration on Saturday, i.e. 3.2.2018@ 10:00 a.m. at Govt. J. Thankima College Landsite, Bawngkawn Brigade area, in protest against the alleged construction of House by Pi B. Lalhmangaihi, Chaltlang Dingdi Veng which was occupied by Pi Ramfangzauvi &amp; Family within the college area. The protestors pulled down portion of the wall, kitchen shed and damaged 2 (two) water storages. The situation was kept under control by the timely intervention of Police. It is reported that some leaders of MZP and MSU had joined the demonstration. The following resolutions were passed by the protestors :-

  (i) Pi Ramfangzauvi &amp; Family should evacuate themselves from Govt.  J. Thankima College Landsite, Bawngkawn Brigade Area.

  (ii) Government of Mizoram should evict the families who are allegedly   occupying Govt. J. Thankima College Landsite at Bawngkawn  Brigade Area.

  (iii) Eviction should be completed by the State Government on or before   10.2.2018.

  (iv) Students of Govt. J. Thankima College will hold protest   demonstrations if their demands for eviction of the family is not  met.

6.2.2018 on 6.2.2018 @ 1:00 p.m, around seventy (70) residents of Melbuk Village, Mizoram forcefully retrieved Twenty (20) vehicles owned by individuals from Melbuk which were detained by Myanmar Police at the bank of Uilui River, near the Indo-Myanmar border approximately 45 Kilometres from Champhai. These vehicles mostly of medium vehicles carrying fertilizers were reportedly detained by the Myanmar Police since 28th November, 2017 for allegedly entering into their territory without proper permit.

 According to information received, these villagers surprised the Myanmar Police personnel posted at this place during their lunch break and tied them up before taking away these vehicles but no injury was caused to Myanmar Police.

 Residence of Melbuk Village claimed that they have been taking enormous efforts to reclaim these vehicles detained by Myanmar Police. They had requested the Deputy Commissioner of Tiddim and Falam, Myanmar about this issue but to no avail. The owners of these vehicles have not received any seizure memo from Myanmar authorities; in fact, all they had received was that their vehicles were not confiscated. As these vehicles were reportedly the main source of income for the residents of Melbuk, they forcefully retrieved their vehicles.

9.2.2018 In a protest demonstration held today, i.e. 9.2.2018 @ 12:40 at Sazaikawn, Lunglei, Youths of Lunglei demanded speedy execution of On-going Road Construction works between Lunglei to Kanghmun South. The agitators launched blockade at Lunglei - Sazaikawn road and caused delay to a group of MsLA led by Pu Zodintluanga, Hon'ble UD &amp; PA Minster from attending the inaugural function of Multipurpose Hall at Sazaikawn. Other MsLA included Pu PC. Thanliana, Hon'ble Minister for Social Welfare ; Pu S. Laldingliana, MLA, Vice Chairman, HPC Lunglei and Pu Chalrosanga, MLA, Lungei West. Around 60 (sixty) youths participated in the agitation and the blockade was lifted by 2:00 p.m. The following resolutions were passed by the agitators:-

 (i) Demanded immediate Release Order of Road Maintenance Funds between Lunglei to Kanghmun South currently pending with the Finance Department. The release order must be made on 9.2.2018.
 (ii) PWD must reinforce road construction labourers at Lunglei - Kanghmun South.

  (iii) Publication of names of Contractor(s) engaged in the Lunglei - Kanghmun South Road construction works.

 (iv) Completion of road construction work before 15th April 2018.

 (v) Allocation of additional funds for Lunglei - Kanghmun South road construction.

21.2.2018 Yesterday, i.e. 20.2.2018, at around 10:30 a.m, miscreants suspected to be members of Students' Union of Govt. J. Thankima College dismantled the house of Pi B. Lalhmangaihi which was rented by Pu R. Lalhmingmawia at Bawngkawn Brigade Veng, Aizawl which was supposedly constructed within the premises of Govt. J. Thankima College land site. The tenants were away while the incident took place. The miscreants have already fled the scene when Police arrived at the place of occurrence. Situation is under close watch.
27.2.2018 Today, i.e. 27.2.2018, around 50 (fifty) members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) from Aizawl and Bairabi constructed "Zofate Chawlhbuk" (Shed) at Zophai near Bairabi located at Mizoram- Assam border. The construction work of 12x6 feet shed was reportedly completed at around 4:00 p.m followed by a short function held at the Shed under the chairmanship of L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, President, MZP. It was also reported that Assam Police, Assam Forest Deptt. staff and Mizoram Police commanded by Commandant IstIR Bn., Mualvum were present at the spot during the construction. The Assam Police reportedly requested for demolition of the shed by a joint Assam and Mizoram Police force in order to avoid further escalation of Law and Order problem at the disputed site.

28.2.2018 It has been reported that 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' constructed by Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) yesterday, i.e. 27.2.2018 at Zophai located at Mizoram-Assam border has been demolished by unknown miscreants reportedly with an excavator last night, i.e. 27.2.2018 at around 9:25 p.m, barely five (5) hours after it was constructed by MZP. In this regard, an FIR has been lodged at Bairabi Police Station by Ricky Zorinsanga, President, MZP Sub-Headquarters, Bairabi last night itself. At the same time, in their Press Release issued today, i.e. 28.2.2018, MZP strongly condemned the demolition of Zofate Chawlhbuk which they claimed was constructed within their own plot of land within the territory of Mizoram. They also expressed their intention to re-construct 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' at the same disputed site on 8.3.2017. They also demanded that those miscreants responsible for the demolition of the shed should be arrested on or before 5thMarch, 2018 and that all the materials of the shed that were stolen from the site should be returned to MZP. Around 40 (forty) Mizoram Police personnel are performing duty at Bairabi in order to prevent any untoward incident at the disputed site and its surrounding areas.

9.3.2018 Yesterday, i.e. 8.3.2018, a large number of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) from Aizawl, Kolasib and Bairabi town went to Zophai near Bairabi with an intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk (Shed) near Assam-Mizoram border. At around 11:45 a.m yesterday, a minor scuffle broke out between members of MZP and Assam Police when some members of MZP tried to unload their building materials from the vehicle. The Assam Police resorted to Lathi-charge, as a result of which around 15 (fifteen) MZP members and some media persons from Mizoram reportedly sustained minor injuries. Adamant with their intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk, a good number of MZP members remain camped at the disputed site throughout last night, i.e. 8.3.2018 and the Assam Police also performed duty at the site the whole night. The Government of Mizoram promptly sent Pu Lalrinmawia Ralte, Political Adviser to Chief Minister and other officials last night itself to prevent further escalation of dispute at the site and no further untoward incident was reported last night.

 Today, i.e. 9.3.2018 around 40 (forty) members of Aizawl City College Joint Students’ Union (ACCJSU) led by Lalnunpuia, President, ACCJSU left Aizawl for Zophai to join MZP. It has also been reported that leaders of Central Young Mizo Association (CYMA) including some members of political parties have also proceeded to the site.

 Today, i.e. 9.3.2018 at around 6:00 p.m, Pu Lalrinmawia Ralte, Political Adviser to Chief Minister; Pu Lalbiakzama, Addl. Secretary, Home Department; DC, Kolasib and SP, Kolasib held a meeting with leaders of MZP at the residence of Pu Sanghmingthanga, Bairabi. The Government officials advised leaders of MZP to approach the Court with matters regarding the land dispute to tackle the issue legally. Appeals have been reportedly made to the students not to go ahead with their intention to reconstruct the shed at Zophai in order to avoid further escalation of Law and Order problems and to leave the issue in the hands of higher officials between the two states. In this regard, it has been reported that leaders of MZP are likely to appeal and appraise the proposal to their members present at the disputed site.

 In order to prevent any untoward incident, hundreds of Mizoram Police under the command of SP, Kolasib and Commandant, 1st IR Bn. are performing duty in and around the disputed site. A good number of MZP members and Assam Police are still present at the site while writing this report.

 It may be pertinent to mention here that Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) had constructed a Shed named ‘Zofate Chawlhbuk’ at Zophai near Bairabi on 27.2.2018 as they strongly claimed that the said land belongs to Pu Ch. Chhunga (L), the first Chief Minister of Mizoram. At the same time, a Police Duty Post have also been constructed supposedly by Assam Police at the same disputed site on 2.3.2018 but the two structures were dismantled within same days they were constructed.

10.3.2018 Today, i.e. 10.3.2018 @ around 11:00 a.m, a scuffle broke out again between Assam Police and members of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) when around 100 (hundred) strong MZP members proceeded to the disputed site at Zophai near Bairabi along Assam - Mizoram border with their building materials to reconstruct ‘Zofate Chawlhbuk’ at the site. The students were intercepted by Assam Police before they reached the disputed site and they subsequently used force to disperse them. It has been reported that the Assam Police initially used Lathi but later on resorted to firing and around 8 (eight) shots were reportedly fired as a result of which one Ricky Lalchhandama, Secretary i/c Establishment, MZP reportedly sustained gunshot injury on his right ankle and around 49 (forty nine) others sustained injuries on their persons. Out of 49 (forty nine) injured MZP members, 7 (seven) of them reportedly sustained serious injuries and were referred to other Hospitals for necessary treatment. The Assam Police burnt down the temporary shed constructed by the MZP near the disputed site and the following vehicles belonging to MZP members were also ransacked by the Assam Police today :-

 Sumo  - 1 no

 Taxi  - 1 no

 Car (Nano) - 1 no.

 M/Cycles - 3 nos.

 After they were forcefully dispersed by the Assam Police, at around 12:30 p.m, the MZP members gathered in front of Bairabi Police Station wherein they expressed their anger to the Mizoram Police for their inaction in the wake of atrocities committed against them by Assam Police. Thereafter, they proceeded to Bairabi PHC where their fellow students are being treated with their injuries.

 The MZP passed the following resolutions regarding the border issue as under:-

 1. Zofate Chawlhbuk shall be constructed at Zophai by MZP.

 2. MZP strongly condemned the use of firearms against their members by  Assam Police.

 3. MZP strongly condemned Government of Mizoram for not taking  significant steps towards protection of the State territory.

 4. The Assam Government should duly compensate the students whose  properties have been destroyed by the Assam Police.

 5. MZP will look after the injured students and will not leave them in the  lurch.

 6. MZP is thankful to residents of Bairabi for their support.

 7. MZP will organise a procession in Aizawl and at all other MZP Hqrs. &amp;  Sub-Hqrs. on 12.3.2018 (Monday) in order to show their strong  determination to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk.

12.3.2018 Today, i.e. 12.3.2018 @ 10:30 a.m, a procession called ‘Ram Humhalh Kawngzawh’ was organised under the aegis of Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) in Aizawl and in other towns of the State such as Lunglei, Champhai, Serchhip, Kolasib, Thenzawl, Vairengte, Sairang, Saitual, Tlabung, Bairabi, Bilkhawthlir, Zawlnuam and Mamit wherein a large number of students took to the streets. Situation was peaceful in all the towns and it has been reported that an effigy of Shri. Adil Khan, DC of Hailakandi District, who had reportedly given the firing order against MZP members on 10.3.2018, was burnt by MZP at Tlabung.

  In Aizawl, the procession began at 10:30 a.m from Chandmari in the North and from Sikulpuikawn in the South and converged at Vanapa Hall. Around 6,000 (six thousand) students participated in the procession who shouted slogans condemning the State Government for its alleged inaction relating to the border issue and their strong intention to construct Zofate Chawlhbuk at Zophai. A function was held in front of Vanapa Hall under the chairmanship of Michael Lalramsanga, Treasurer, MZP Gen. Hqrs. wherein Lalnunmawia Pautu, Gen. Secy., MZP; B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP; R.B. Lalmalsawma, President, MSU and Zorammawia, Vice President, Aizawl City Colleges Joint Students’ Union (ACCJSU) and Pu Vanlalruata, President, CYMA delivered speeches. Adamant with their intention to reconstruct Zofate Chawlhbuk, B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP announced before the gathering that MZP will reconstruct 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' at Zophai on 14.3.2018 (Wednesday). They also appealed all political parties of the State not to politicise the issue in order to gain political advantage.

 MZP passed the following resolutions today :-

  i) MZP strongly condemned the Assam Government for invoking Section 144CrPC on the soil of Mizoram and also condemned the State Government for turning a deaf ear to the border issue.

   ii) Government of Mizoram should protect the boundary of the State.

  iii) MZP will continue to render utmost effort to protect Mizoram and her people.

   iv) 'Zofate Chawlhbuk' should be reconstructed.

 The processionists peacefully dispersed @ 1:30 p.m and no untoward incident has been reported from any part of the State today. Further input indicated that MZP will hold an Extended Office Bearers’ Meeting at their office tomorrow, i.e. 13.3.2018 @ 10:30 a.m and they are likely to discuss their future course of action regarding the border issue.

13.3.2018 The Mizoram Journalists’ Association (MJA) General Hqrs. had observed a Sit-in Demonstration in front of Vanapa Hall today, i.e. 13.3.2018 from 12:00 noon - 1:00 p.m in protest against the alleged brutal attack on Journalists by personnel of Assam Police on 10.3.2018 at Zophai, Kolasib District at Mizoram-Assam border. The same had also been observed in other Districts by MJA members across the State. Pu Lal Thanzara, Hon'ble I&amp;PR Minister who visited the MJA Sit-in Demonstration in front of Vanapa Hall today @ 12:25 p.m had expressed support for their cause and told Journalists that the Government had already conveyed displeasure to Assam Government, and also wished speedy recovery to the injured Journalists. The Minister was accompanied by Pu P.C. Lalthanliana, Hon'ble Minister, LAD and Pu Chalrosanga, MLA. The Press Council of India, in a letter dated 10.3.2018 addressed to the Chief Reporter, Chief of Bureau, had also expressed strong condemnation of Assam Police for their brutal acts on Journalists, and demanded the Assam Government to identify and take strict action against Police personnel involved in the assault.

Students of NIT, Mizoram urged the Hon'ble Chief Minister of Mizoram and authorities of HRD Ministry to take steps towards improving the NIT administration and also to take necessary action against the erring officials. Students of NIT, Mizoram also intended to meet the Hon'ble Governor of Mizoram at the earliest.

 2) Lawngtlai District Land Owners' Association (LDLOA) held a meeting at their office, Lawngtlai today, i.e. 2.4.2018 @ 7:00 a.m under the chairmanship of Pu H. Remmawia, President, LDLOA. The meeting decided to stage indefinite blockade of a highway constructed under the Kaladan Multi-Modal Transit Transport Project (KMMTTP) from today, i.e. 2.4.2018 in protest against alleged non-payment of compensation for their lands to be acquired for the ongoing highway construction works. The LDLOA slammed the Central Government for turning a deaf ear to their demands even after the Deputy Commissioner of Lawngtlai had reportedly approved as many as 303 (three hundred three) compensation applications. They passed a resolution that LDLOA will not allow any constructions works to be carried out by RDS and ARSS companies at the site and that any violation of the diktat will invite stern reaction from the LDLOA.

9.4.2018 1) Khawzawl District Implementation Demand Committee (KDIDC) in a Press Release issued today, i.e. 9.4.2018 highlighted that they organised a public rally at Dinthar Bazar, Khawzawl, Champhai District this morning demanding immediate implementation of Khawzawl as a full-fledged District. Around 300 (three hundred) residents of Khawzawl participated in the rally and passed the following resolutions:-

 (i) The State Government must declare Khawzawl as a full-fledged District before a Model Code of Conduct is enforced in the State.

 (ii) If the State Government implements Khawzawl as a full-fledged District, only Congress party may contest Tuichang Constituency in the upcoming Mizoram Legislative Assembly General Election, 2018. 

 (iii) If Khawzawl is not declared as a full-fledged District along with other towns, Congress party may not take the trouble of contesting the Constituency and KDIDC volunteers will take all necessary steps towards implementation of its demands.

 2) Tawipui South Joint Action Committee in a Press Release issued on 8.4.2018 demanded that :-

 (i) The State Government should cancel the transfer order of Headmaster, Govt. High School, Tawipui South and that two posts of Teacher that are lying vacant at the High School due to transfer and retirement of incumbent Teachers must be filled immediately.

 (ii) The State Government should take necessary action to run Govt. Primary School-I, Tawipui South as an English Medium School from the Academic Session 2018-2019.

 (iii) The State Government must appoint Ayush Doctor, Dental Surgeon, Pharmacist and Health Supervisor (Male) at the Primary Health Centre (PHC), Tawipui.

 (iv) A Police Station/Out Post should be opened at Tawipui South.

 In demand for immediate implementation of their various demands, Tawipui South Joint Action Committee begun indefinite picketing of all Educational Institutions at Tawipui South from today, i.e. 9.4.2018.

10.4.2018 1) Joint Action Committee of Tawipui South continued picketing of all Educational Institutions at Tawipui South, Lunglei District for the second day today, i.e. 10.4.2018 demanding cancellation of the transfer order in respect of Headmaster, Govt. High School, Tawipui South and immediate posting of two Teachers at the same school, etc. It has been reported that if no positive response is received from the State Government, they will continue with their strike tomorrow, i.e. 11.2.2018 and that they are likely to convene a meeting tomorrow to discuss their future course of action on the issue.

 2) PWD staff across the State wore a black badge/ribbon today, i.e. 10.4.2018 in protest against the alleged verbal abuse uttered against Pu C. Lalchhuana, SE, PWD by Lunglei Thalai Pawl at Lunglei on 2ndApril, 2018.

Information received suggested that they may organize an indefinite Total Bandh from 16.4.2018 onwards.

About 100 (one hundred) picketers, mostly students, participated and the picketing will continue tomorrow, i.e. 13.4.2018.

17.4.2018 A procession organized by Darlawn District Demand Committee (DDDC) was held at Darlawn today, i.e. 17.4.2018 @ 10:30 a.m. About 1,000 (one thousand) people participated and all Government offices, Educational Institutions and Shops remained closed during the procession.

 The processionists adopted resolutions demanding the Government to immediately take steps to create a new Administrative District for the Northern Hill area which they claimed is lagging far behind in terms of developments compared to other parts of Mizoram, and that the 41 (forty one) villages within their demand area should not be divided or included in other districts. The procession was peaceful and there was no untoward incident during the procession.

Zakhai, Chief Executive Member (CEM) of MADC is likely to hold a meeting with leaders of MSO this evening at around 7:30 p.m. It has also been reported that MSO will continue with their agitation if the meeting fails to find solutions on the issues. Zakhai, CEM, MADC held a meeting with leaders of MSO last evening, i.e. 18.4.2018 @ 7:30 p.m. The MSO were apprised by the CEM regarding the Contractor's commitment for better construction and maintenance work of Boys Hostel Building at Chawlhhmun, Aizawl. The Contractor for Girls Hostel Building at Zotlang, Aizawl is also expected to oblige the same at the earliest.

4.5.2018 The imbroglio between Zokhawthar NGOs and Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab operators over the rate of Maxi Cab Fare continued till today, i.e. 4.5.2018 as the Maxi Cab operators on Champhai side had stopped and stranded 4 (four) Sumos carrying passengers from Zokhawthar at Ruantlang en-route Champhai today @ 3:00 p.m. It is reported that about 25 (twenty five) Maxi Cab drivers remained on duty at Ruantlang today which has been seen as a fallout of the Zokhawthar NGO's stoppage of Maxi Cab Service since 30.4.2018 demanding lowering of rate of Maxi Cab fare from ` 150/- to ` 100/-. It is learnt that the 4 (four) Sumos stranded at Ruantlang had come after agreeing the rate fixed by the Zokhawthar NGOs, i.e. ` 100/-.

8.5.2018 The two-day Total Bandh called by Tawipui South JAC was observed from 5:00 a.m today, All Government offices and Educational Institutions remained closed. The National Highway 54 has been blocked and about 150 (one hundred fifty) persons turned up for Bandh duty. Around 35 (thirty five) different vehicles have been stranded at the time of writing this report. The situation is reported to be otherwise peaceful and no untoward incident reported during the day.

9.5.2018 1) The imbroglio between NGOs of Zokhawthar and Maxi cab operators over the rate of Maxi Cab fare continues even as DTO Champhai served a notice to the Maxi Cab operators to follow the rate fixed by the Government. Following the stoppage of Maxi cab service by NGOs of Zokhawthar and the counter action by the Maxi Cab operators, the DTO had issued by a notice on 8.5.2018 to the Champhai to Zokhawthar Sumo Service Association to follow the Government approved rate, i.e. Rs. 67.20 (Rs. 2.40 per km unmetalled) and threatened to initiate action to the extent of cancellation of their Route permit. It may be recalled that the Maxi Cab operators had earlier charged Rs. 100/- and later increased the rate to Rs.150/- on their own. In reply to this, the Maxi Cab operators had submitted a petition to the DTO Champhai in which they pleaded that even Zokhawthar to Aizawl service Maxi Cabs had not been following Government approved rates, and also that the rates of Taxi and Two wheeler service within Zokhawthar Town are Rs. 100/- and Rs. 50/- respectively which is much higher in comparision to that of Champhai to Zokhawthar.

 In the meantime, the Villace Council and NGOs of Melbuk had also issued a statement on 8.5.2018 expressing support to the NGOs of Zokhawthar stating that not only the people of Zokhawthar, but also the people of Melbuk had been affected by the increase of Maxi Cab fare.

 It is reported that the Maxi Cab owners of Zokhawthar are willing to ply at the rate of Rs. 100/- whereas, the Association maintained their stand at Rs. 150/-.

 2) The 2nd day of Total Bandh organized by Tawipui South JAC was observed today. All together 33 (thirty three) vehicles have been stranded and about 175 (one hundred seventy five) people turned up for bandh duty. The situation is reported to be otherwise peaceful without untoward incident during the day. A meeting between the JAC leaders and the officials of District administration was held at 3:00 p.m at VC Conference Hall. Outcome of the meeting is awaited.

10.5.2018 1) Following the notice issued to the Maxi Cab operators to follow the Government approved rates, the Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab operators met the DTO, Champhai today, i.e. 10.5.2018 @ 1:00 p.m in his office chamber in which the DTO had offered them to continue their service at the rate of Rs. 100/- instead of Rs. 67.20/- (Government approved rate). It is learnt that the Maxi Cab operators will have a consultation amongst themselves on the offer made by the DTO, and in the meantime, called off their duty near Ruantlang temporarily for coming two/three days.

 2) The two-day Total bandh organized by Tawipui South JAC had been called off at 7:00 p.m tonight, i.e. 10.5.2018 following the assurance by DC, Lunglei to pursue their demands with the Government except their demand pertaining to establishing a Rural RD Block at Tawipui South. The JAC will decide their further course of action if their demands are not met by the Government on or before 30.5.2018.

21.5.2018 1) A Sit-in demonstration was staged in front of Vanapa Hall, Aizawl today, i.e. 21.5.2018 organised by Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP) and North East Students' Organisation (NESO) in protest against the Citizenship Amendment Bill, 2016 which incorporated the provisions of regularisation of Citizenship of foreign nationals namely, Bangladesh, Afghanistan and Pakistan if he/she resides in India for a period of six (6) years which they perceived will open the doors for assimilation of Zo-indigeneous people by foreign nationals. The programme was chaired by B. Vanlaltana, Vice President, MZP and a speech was delivered by L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, President, MZP. MZP has urged all MsLA to pass a Resolution opposing this Bill in the Assembly House. It is reported that around 80 (eighty) students including 54 (fifty four) students from Springfield HSS attended the Sit-in demonstration programme. It is also reported that representatives from CYMA, MUP, MHIP and MSU expressed their resentment against the Citizenship Amendment Bill, 2016.

24.5.2018 The impasse over the rate of Maxi Cab fare on Champhai - Zokhawthar route had finally been solved as both the NGOs of Zokhawthar and the Maxi Cab operators agreed at the rate of Rs. 100/- after several rounds of negotiations. It is reported that a meeting between NGOs of Zokhawthar and Maxi Cab Operators (Champhai - Zokhawthar Sumo Service Association and Champhai - Zokhawthar Maxi Cab Owners Welfare Committee) held last night (23.5.2018) at Zokhawthar YMA Hall which was attended by about 30 (thirty) members, had reached an agreement and decided to continue their service at the rate of Rs. 100/- from today, i.e. 24.5.2018.

6.6.2018 Mizoram Underground Returnees Association (MURA) has decided to go ahead with their proposed hunger strike from this evening, i.e. 6.6.2018 at their office to press upon the MPCC to fulfill the agreement with respect to grant of rehabilitation to the MURA members. In a statement issued today, MURA has expressed disappointment with the MPCC for non-implementation of the agreement signed almost ten years ago, and stated that they had to carry out a 'fast unto death' until their demands are met. It is reported that 20 (twenty) persons have volunteered for the hunger strike to be started from this evening at their office at Tuikual.

7.6.2018 Mizoram Government Lumpsum Grant-in-aid Higher School Association (MIGLAHSSA), 9 (nine) Higher Secondary Schools run by local bodies, observed 'Demand Day', today, i.e. 7.6.2018 in which they attended school without teaching the students in demand for up-gradation to Adhoc-aided status. In each school, the teachers addressed their students apprising them of the reasons for their action and the need for up-gradation of their school. They claimed that the Government's neglect compelled them to resort to this action and that they will continue pressing their demand so that these 9 (nine) schools, which have been managed by local citizens for more than 13 years, can get Adhoc-aided status.

As per the agreement, BSNL will upgrade the Internet Broadband speed from the current 14 Mbps to 100 Mbps within 6 (six) months. BSNL has also agreed to give a 50% rebate for three months, i.e. March to May, 2018 to its postpaid subscribers.

CYMA came to know that Mamit DC had left Mamit for Aizawl @ 6:30 p.m the same evening and spread emergency notice for public gathering to receive him. The public gathered at Aizawl Tennis Court (around 150), New Secretariat Gate-1 (around 50) and Gate-2 (around 70) under the aegis of CYMA and later dispersed @ 12:15 to 12:30 a.m after the DC did not arrive as expected.

 Input has been received that all NGOs Mamit picketed Mamit DC Office and Mamit DC Office was closed today. More than 1,000 (one thousand) persons gathered in front of Mamit DC Office gate. The public gathering was presided over by Pu Lalropuia, Treasurer, Sub-Hqrs. YMA, Mamit. Pu K. Ely Rosanga, President, Sub-Hqrs. YMA, Mamit addressed the picketers and burnt the effigy of Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary and they dispersed @ 10:50 a.m.

19.9.2018 Information has been received that NGO Coordination Committee, Mamit had stopped picketing of Mamit DC Office and the Office is opened normally as Mamit DC, Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary left Mamit. But they stated that they will strongly react if Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary return to Mamit. Input has been received that NGO Coordination Committee, Aizawl do not have action plan, but they intended to hold Coordination Committee Meeting soon to deliberate on whether to organize a procession or Total Bandh in demand of the transfer out of Pu Bhupesh Chaudhary from Mizoram.

20.9.2018 Information has been received that All Mizoram Tanker Drivers' Association called off their strike following talks with Police authorities in which it was decided to relax 'No Entry' between Edenthar and Thuampui, Aizawl. They have resumed transportation of Oil from today, i.e. 20.9.2018.

24.9.2018 NHM (National Health Mission) Contractual Association of Mizoram (NCAM) has issued a statement today, i.e. 24.9.2018 informing all its members across Mizoram to wear black badges today to show their grievances over non-receipt of their salaries regularly. About 30 (thirty) members gathered at High Field later in the afternoon today @ around 2:15 p.m with an intention to submit a Memorandum to the Hon'ble Health Minister, with a copy to the Hon'ble Chief Minister.

 It has been reported that the NCAM members, upon learning that the Hon'ble Health Minister had left office for the day, dispersed @ 4:00 p.m and notified all its members presently staying in Aizawl to assemble at High Field to submit the Memorandum tomorrow at 11:00 a.m.

25.9.2018 MNYF in a Press Release issued today, i.e. 25.9.2018 stated that MNYF submitted a memo today to Pu Lal Thanzara, Hon'ble PWD Minister demanding the publish of Enquiry Report on the collapsed of Tuirini Bridge before the end of September, 2018. The PR stated several MNF youths led by 2 (two) of their leaders went to submit the memo and Pu Lalzahawma Khiangte, MNYF Treasurer addressed these youths in which he stated that Pu Lal Thanzara has no idea the reason and those responsible for the collapsed of Tuirini Bridge which clearly indicated that he is incompetent to execute the responsibilities of his office.

 It has been reported that MNYF led by their 2 (two) leaders numbering around 20 (twenty) proceeded towards Chief Minister's Office (CMO) to submit the memo @ 11:00 a.m. MPYCC, having caught wind of this also proceeded towards CMO and around 50 (fifty) members gathered in front of CMO. In order to prevent possible altercation between both party youths, the Police prevented all MNF youths from entering the premises and allowed 10 (ten) persons to enter with another 5 (five) led by their leaders entering the building to submit the memo after which they left the CMO peacefully. It was also reported that MPYCC intended to block if all of them were allowed to enter the CMO premises which could possibly have led to a serious Law and Order situation.

26.9.2018 It has been reported that Kolasib District MNF Joint Block Committee organised National Highway (NH-54) Road Block today, i.e. 26.9.2018 from 5:00 a.m at the following points, viz. Kawnpui, Khuangpuilam, Rengtekawn Zero Point, Bairabi, Bilkhawthlir Chemphai peng, Bualpui and Vairengte-Lailapur Aurorickshaw Stand.  The road blocks had been called off in different places between 4:00 p.m to 4:30 p.m. No untoward incident reported during the period of blockade. Proper Police deployment was made in every blockade points.

28.9.2018 1) All India Organization of Chemists &amp; Druggists (AIOCD) closed their shop today, i.e. 28.9.2018 in protest against 'On-line Sale of Medicine through E-Portal'. In support of this, Mizoram Chemists &amp; Druggists Association (MCDA) also closed all their shops excluding Hospital Canteens and Government Pharmacies. Posters showing the reason of their strike and regret for inconveniences to patients were attached on the walls of their shops.

 2) AMFU Gen. Hqrs. organized a Protest March, "Mizoram Kuthnathawktute Chhanchhuahna Kawngzawh" today, i.e. 28.9.2018 as a demand for implementation of Land Reform and Agricultural Marketing, in which around 200 (two hundred) members participated. The procession started from Chanmari Kawn @ 12:30 p.m wherein a short programme was held. Pu Lalnungliana, Vice President, AMFU addressed the public in which he asked public forgiveness for the inconvenience they caused due to their procession and Pu Zion Lalremruata, Gen. Secretary also delivered a speech. Pu Lalnungliana also burnt copies of ‘The Mizoram Agriculture Produces (Restriction on Movement) Order, 1994’ and ‘The Mizoram Agriculture Products Prohibition (Amendment) Order, 1999’. The procession halted at Israel Point in which Pu R. Laltluanga, Treasurer, AMFU delivered a speech and stated that the Government neglected the farmers and they need a new Government who cares for the farmers. The procession was stopped at Vanapa Hall and Pu Joseph H. Lalthanzuala, President, AMFU addressed the procession and stated that it is sad to organize a protest march because the Government neglected the farmers and that the Government’s claim of farmers as their VIP is a lie. He also stated that they condemned the accusation of farmers as being responsible for the low production of food and agricultural products. He further stated that NLUP scheme is not designed for the development of farmers but for political tools. Gingers brought by the farmers were dumped in front of Vanapa Hall as it is claimed there is no market. They shouted together demanding for Land Reform, Regulated Market and Government who cares for farmers. They also held placards, "We want good marketing system", "We want to sell our products at a better price", “We demand APLM Act Implementation", "We want a reliable system of Agriculture Marketing", etc. The procession was dispersed at 2:15 p.m and it was followed by an Executive Committee Meeting at AMFU Office, Venghlui, Aizawl. The meeting was chaired by Pu Joseph H. Lalthanzuala and attended by 15 (fifteen) members. The meeting decided to wait for the Government till 3.10.2018 and if there is no action taken from the Government, they intended to organise Economic Blockade date and time of which will be decided later.

 3) Champhai MZP had started closing down all Educational Institutions and Government Offices today, i.e. 28.9.2018. About 450-500 College students participated in the picketing which was done at the following 8 (eight) places :-

 i) District Court, Zote.

 ii) SDEO's Office, Bethel.

 iii) BDO's Office, Ruantlang.

 iv) PHED Office, Vengsang.

 v) Chief Medical Officer's Office, Vengsang.

 vi) DEO/SSA Office, Kahrawt.

 vii) Chanem Building (Treasury Office and Supply Department Office).

 viii) DC/SP Offices, Keifangtlang.

 The MZP picketers converged at their Office at Chanem Building @ 3:30 p.m in which they discussed about their future course of action and decided to go further ahead with their 'Action Plan' on 1.10.2018.

1.10.2018 The DC, Champhai had promulgated 144 CrPC, 1973 yesterday, i.e. 30.9.2018, prohibiting gathering of more than 5 (five) persons with intention to disrupting official works within 1(one) Km of DC and SP Offices. As soon as the MZP noticed about the Promulgation order, members of MZP proceeded to DC Complex and gathered the whole night. Police immediately encircled DC Office to restraint MZP to enter into vicinity of DC Complex. MZP Sub-Hqrs. of Khawbung, Dungtlang, Farkawn, Khuangleng and Hnahlan also issued a Press Release yesterday, i.e. 30.9.2018 for supporting the agitation of MZP Hqrs., Champhai. In continuation of the agitation, MZP Hqrs., Champhai organized a procession today, i.e. 1.10.2018 as demand for filling up the posts of Ophthalmologist and Orthopaedic at Champhai District Hospital. The procession was started from Champhai Vengsang @10:00 a.m in which around 500 (five hundred) students participated in the procession. The agitating College students were joined by Higher Secondary Students today. Students held placards and raised slogans of demanding Orthopaedic and Ophthalmologist at Champhai District Hospital and blamed the Mizoram Government for the neglect of District Hospital, Champhai. After conducting the peaceful procession at around 11:00 a.m, OBs of MZP were called by DC, Champhai and told the good news about the Mizoram Government proposal for posting of Ophthalmologist. The agitating students gathered at Govt. Champhai College Complex waiting for the posting order of the demand doctors and further instructions from their leaders. Agreement was made by making condition that Ophthalmologist will be posted and Government of Mizoram will do its level best for posting of Orthopedic as soon as possible. The MZP officially withdrew their agitation at 2:30 p.m.

3.10.2018 Mizoram Maxi Cab Owners' Association (MMCOA) organized an indefinite strike in which all Maxi Cab service ceased their service from today, i.e. 3.10.2018 as a demand from the Government to raise Maxi Cab rate for metalled road @ Rs.3/-per Km/head and unmetalled road @ Rs. 3.50/- per Km/head and also re-issue of All Mizoram Permit. Information has been received that there was no Maxi Cab service throughout the State in support of this strike.

 MMCOA issued a Press Release today, i.e. 3.10.2018 in which they condemned the Press Release issued by the Mizoram Consumers’ Union yesterday, i.e. 2.10.2018 regarding against the indefinite strike organized by MMCOA. In their PR, they accused the MCU of interfering beyond their duties. The PR also asked public to bear with them for the inconvenience caused due to their strike.

6.10.2018 Mizoram Maxi Cab Owners Association (MMCOA) held an Executive Meeting on 6.10.2018 @ 4:30 p.m at MMCOA Office, Chaltlang which was chaired by Pu C. Lalthanmawia, President, MMCOA and attended by 10 (ten) members. They issued a Press Release which stated that their indefinite strike was called-off due to announcement of MLA Election for Mizoram State and further added notes of apology to the public for inconvenience they caused during the strike.

10.10.2018 1) CYMA organized a procession today, i.e.10.10.2018 @ 11:00 a.m as a demand for dissolution of Chakma Autonomous District Council (CADC) which they believed was created illegitimately. The procession started from two points - Sikulpuikawn and Chanmari simultaneously and moved towards the courtyard of Vanapa Hall, around 8,000 (eight thousand) members participated and students also participated as well. At Chanmari Kawn, a short function was held before the procession started which was presided over by Pu Lalrochuanga Pachuau, Treasurer, CYMA and L. Ramdinliana Renthlei, MZP President delivered a speech. A short function was also held at Sikulpuikawn which was presided over by Pu Peter Chhakchuak, Asst. Secretary, CYMA and Pu R. Lalngheta, Vice President, CYMA delivered a speech. The procession started from two points was converged at the courtyard of Vanapa Hall which was followed by a short function in which Pu R. Lalngheta presided over the programme and Pu Vanlalruata, President, CYMA addressed the participants. Slogans were raised and placards against CADC were also displayed during the procession. The procession ended peacefully at 12:40 p.m. After the procession, around 10 (ten) CYMA leaders met Governor at his residence and submitted a petition for permanent abolition of unconstitutional and illegal creation of CADC. The petition contains that Chakmas were not the indigenous inhabitant of Mizoram and they are illegal migrants and foreigners who entered Mizoram illegally. Even the indigenous peoples (Mizos) have no rights in CADC areas. There were a number of lapses and unconstitutional procedure for the creation of CADC which violated North Eastern Areas Re-organization (NEAR) Act, 1971 and UT Act, 1971. They strongly requested the Governor to abolish the unconstitutional and illegal creation of CADC in Southern Mizoram.

 Simultaneous processions were also carried out by 5 (five) Sub-Hqrs., 7 (seven) Groups and 6 (six) Branches at various town/villages within the State in which more than 10,000 (ten thousand) members participated.

 In regard to the procession held within Aizawl City and various parts of Mizoram today, CYMA issued a Press Release today itself wherein they expressed their gratitude towards those who participated in their procession which was held today and further added their apology to public for causing inconvenience in the said regard. CYMA in their PR also requested public cooperation towards their initiatives in safeguarding Mizoram and its people in the future.

 2) MZP Hqrs. Champhai is intending to restrain the Chakma students who are going to give Secondary School (Cl-X) and Senior Secondary School (Cl-XII) Examinations at Zokhawpui Higher Secondary School (National Institute of Open Schooling), Champhai. 10 (ten) Chakma students from Lunglei Study Centre have reached Champhai to give exam at NIOS Centre Champhai, scheduled on 11.10.2018. Leaders of MZP Champhai Hqrs. have informed Pu Lalhmingmawia, Teacher of Lunglei Study Centre, who accompanied the Chakma students at Champhai that the MZP would not allow Chakma students to do examination. Later @ around 5:00 p.m, leaders of MZP Hqrs. Champhai went to the place where the Chakma students are accomodated (Pu Chalbawiha building, Champhai Vengthlang) and warned them not to give examination at Champhai and not to choose Champhai Centre in future. It is learnt that the Chakma students accordingly agreed to go back and they are planning to return to their place on 11.10.2018.
